full compassyon sory herte theym daye leyeth doune alleluya songes myrthe melodye taketh tractus ben songes mornynge palso holy sacramente weddynge moche defouled vanyte synne therfore leyde doune dayes aduente many ben wedded gyueth theym luste lykynge bodyes flesshely luste worlde thynketh full lytell dethe full greuous cometh soo sone redde grete clerkes spedefull mannes soule goo hous corp systerne sayd ye knowe well clene mayden ony dede grete lust speke synne partye hath grete payne ye may se wherfore praye systerne praye youre prayer may holpen beware tyme comynge ye may se peryll tooke mekely paciently charyte gyuynge ensample crysten people doo wyll lyue rest pea shall haue grete persecucyon euyll people suffre mekely martyr god confortynge holy chirche maketh mynde mencyon thus pwe rede holy man called ioseph suffred grete persecucyon suffred mekely therfore god brought hym grete worshyppe prosperyte ye shall hystorye longe therfore shall take moost nedefull atte tyme ioseph fader named iacob xi sone bretherne ioseph fader loued hym moost specyally therfore bretherne hated hym especyall dreme dremed wherby supposed sholde haue lorde ouer al sholde hym worshyppe anone toke theyr counceyll togyder sayd venite ita que occidamu illu lete v go therfore slee hym yet durste drede god anone vedidert eu egipto solde hym egypt man thyrty pen god solde therfore god hym man stewarde kynge pharao bought hym named putyphar ye fende grete enmyte towarde ioseph tempted ye lady sore hym ppost multos ita que dy iniecit domina oculos ioseph et ait veni dormi mecu daye lady loked ioseph tooke hym mantell sayd come slepe soone ioseph vnderstode meanynge anone yede fledde waye lefte mantell thenne woman cryed tolde husbonde ioseph wolde haue lyen sholde saye nay kepte mantell therfore lorde made cast ioseph pryson pharao hadde put boteler baker felle slepe dremed whiche dreme tolde ioseph sayd kynge wolde restore boteler offyce agayne within thre dayes baker sholde hanged within thre dayes sayd thenne happened kynge dremed hym selfe coude man tell sholde fall therof cou sell ye boteler kynge sent ioseph whan ye kynge hadde tolde hym dreme ioseph sayd god sente hym fayre warnynge puruey hym fore sholde come sayd sholde come seuen ple teuous yeres corne maner fruytes vytayles sholde come seuen yeres people sholde spende goten fore thenne ky ge sayd knowe man coude puruey soo well suche thyge thou coudest wherfore make gretest vnder realme shall vnto meat thy commaudemente thenne anone ioseph let make gretest berne euer seen gadred corne fast seuen yere sone came seuen yeres thynge scar dere thenne iacob iosephs fader herde corne sell egypte sente thyder x sone corne whan came thyder saw ioseph fell doune theyr knee dyde worshyp vnto hym lyke dreme knewe hym thought ben lorde countre knewe wel ynough thenne spake theym latyn surge sayd spyes come knowe ye londe sayd n bretherne al one man sone brother home theyr fader wyst whether lyue mente ioseph preue ye trouthe made bynde one theym hyght symeon sayd sholde byde hym tyll set hym home lete fyll theyr sackes corne preuely put theyr money thyr sackes vnwytyng whan came home theyr fader put theyr corne foude theyr money tolde theyr fader thenne sory symeon sone lefte behynde pryson ouer must nedes sende hym whiche loued moost beniamyn iosephs hole broder halfe bretherne ioseph whan iacob fayled corne must nedes sende thenne sente forth beniamyn whan ioseph sawe beniamy myght forbere wepynge none delyuered hym symeon set theym mete fylled theyr sackes corne preuely put cuppe dranke beniamyns sacke bad theym go theyr waye none ioseph sente theym sayd ye blame whyle good chere bere waye cuppe ye dranke heuy sadde sayd soo ransaked founde benyamyns sacke came agayne ioseph sore wepynge whan ioseph sawe theym wepe owne broder benyamyn made moost sorowe founden hym ioseph badde theym good chere youre broder ioseph thynge adred god hath sente hyther youre profyte anone sente fader soo dwelled togyder grete whyle londe moche prosperyt storye redde weke holy chirche goddes chylderne sholde take ensample olde faders suffre trybulacyon parsecucyon mekely perfyte charyte goddes sake suffred v grudgeth agaynst trybulacyon persecucyon god sendeth must shryue hym take penaunce people wyll saye doth god thus haue trespassed ayenst hy grete peryl theyr pacyece truely wordes may lette moche grace pnarratio pwe fynde myracles wenefryde ye virgyne yt man came nyght vpo ii cruches full many maner syknes helpe god holy vyrgyn man hole soo wente wolde hole daye abbaye thanked hyghely god holy vyrgyn hele nyght wente bedde good hele morowe syknes tooke hym ayen sorer dyde leye cryenge grete pyte thenne came monke hym asked hy done syknes come ayen sayd thynge thenne sayd monke thou shryuen sythen thou hole sayd nay nede stale nother oxe cowe dyde greuous syne thought monke though man none deedly synne may doo soo many venyall synnes may make deedly synne ryght man may many smale cornes charge stronge horse may lade soule many smale synnes may falle ye pytte helle thenne anone man wente preest shroue hym hole body soule euer confessyon prayer holy vyrgyne amen pdnica iiii quadragesime good men woman iiii sondaye lenten whiche holy chirche maketh mencyon holy prophete called moyses whiche fygure oure lorde ihesu cryste many yere oure lorde borne rede holy chirche moyses ye deserte synay god spake hym sayd vidi afflictione populi mei que est egipto clamore ei audiui pharao ye kynge egypte oppressed people israell boundage vnresonable werkes woo cryed socour helpe wherfore go thou thyder brynge theym oute theyr boundage shall brynge theym offre theym wyll brynge theym londe plenteuousenesse goodes whan taught moyses sholde moyses wente thyder gadered olde people togyder knewe ye prophecy sholde ladde londe sayd theym god badde hym thenne full gladde wente hym olde yonge tylle come reed se god euer daye pyler clowde refreshe hete sonne ye nyght pyler fyre lyght fro harme venym bestes whan pharao herde moyses forth people toke ccc charyots owne ccc ye londe lxm horsmen cccm fotemen went whan moyses sawe people come prayed god helpe god hym selfe bad hym smyte see yerde et per cussit mare rubrum whan smyten ye see waye hym people see cloue two partyes water stode stylle euery syde hylle grounde drye sonde moyses went forth people hym thenne thought pharao haue passed also sewed oost wha hadde oost within see water wente togyder drowned hym oost whan moyses sawe people thus perysshed thanked god seuen dayes euery daye wente see thankynge god theyr passage makynge grete meledye lorde done soo yet mynde herof eester weke make solempne processyon fonte reed see thenne wente moyses forthe people deserte tylle come vnto ye hylle synay lefte people benethe stabat moyses super monte moyses stode vpon ye hylle god xl dayes xl nyghtes without mete drynke thenne god gaue hy ii table stone ye god wrote owne fyngers x comau dementes toke theym moyses bad hym teche people whan moyses come doune people face bryght sone two spytes stondy ge heed lyke two horne ye people myght speke hym clerenes abscondit moyses facie suam thenne moyses hydde face kerchyef thenne one leef wryten thre commaudementes longen god ben pthe fyrst thou shalte worshyp thy god loue hym aboue thynge thou shalte dyrecte maner thynge goddes wyll thyn owne sue thyn owne wyll pthe seconde comaudement thou shalte take vayne saye thou shalte called goddes chylde crysten man serue fende thenne yt vayne also thou shalte swere god parte body thynge yt made forderynge trouthe yet whan thou arte constrayned therto pthe thyrde comaudemet thou shalt kepe thyn holy daye saye thou shalte erely vp late doune serue god holy daye yu arte werkedaye thyn owne werke besy shalte thou holy daye serue god pthe fourth comaudement thou shalt worshyp thy fader thy moder brought worlde also thy godfader thy godmoder made crysten man thy fader vnder god hath cure charge thy soule pthe v thou shalt slee man nother tonge thy honde thy euyll ensample pthe vi thou shalte stele mannes good pthe vii thou shalte doo lecherye pthe viii thou shalte bere fals wytnesse pthe ix thou shalt coueyte thy neyghboures goodes ne thynge longeth hym ayenst wyl pthe x thou shalt desyre thy neyghboures wyfe counseyll waye doo euyll sholde harme vylonye husbonde pthese ben x commaundementes whiche euery crysten man woman boude kepe thus moyses fygure token cryst moyses came gaue lawe cryste came gaue grace mercye maner moyses fette people egypte thrughe reed see hylle synay wyse cryste whan come prechynge myracles doynge fette people derkenes synne euyll lyuynge thrughe water baptysme hylle vertuous lyuynge therfore wyll shryue hym clene leue foule lyuynge kepe commaudementes god made couenaunt kepe crystenynge thenne shall encreaced hygher ony hylle erthe yt heuen wyll thus must fedde fyue loues two fysshes pwe rede daye holy chirche gospell cryste fedde fyue thousande people fyue loues two fysshes fyrst loofe fyue contrycyon synne seconde shryfte mouth thyrde satysfaccyon theyr trespas fourth torne agayne synne often aferde shall well fyfte perseueraunce good lyuynge two fysshes ben good orysons almesdedes norysshed water yt wepynge teeres deuocyon ii fysshes geten wyll pnarracio pit wryten yt somtyme man yt called pyers ryche man harde begger myght gete good hym thenne tyme happened soo many beggers sette togyder place spake pyers myght gete good hym thenne spake one theym mayster sayd wyll ye leye wt shall gete noo good hy soo made wager thenne wente man forth came pyers place sat hy doune ye porche ye halle dore bode tyll pyers came anone sawe pyers spake horryble pyers grete angre seruauntes came hym basket brede toke loof myght cast beggers hede smote breste sayd stoppe thy mouth therwith deuyll stoppe none begger caught loof ranne way felowes shewed loof gate wager thenne nexte nyght happened pyers shryuen brought bedde dyed none fendes came take soule lady redy bad theym brynge soule dyde nothynge helpe soule onely loof cast begger sayd fendes gaue agaynst wyl therfore ryght sholde helpe hym thenne went lady sone praynge hym graunt soule go body gayne loke wolde amende hym thenne lorde bad bere soule gayne body whan soule body anone satte vp gaue grete syghynge called hym seruauntes tolde theym harde dome hadde dampned loofe caste ye begger therfore none made selle good dealed poore people goddes sake whan done made hym selfe hermyte holy man phere ye may well wyte grete almesdede prayer made man soo preuy god syker ayenst dome haue done almes dedes goddes sake shall saued yf oute deedly synne pwe fynde auoutry take mannes wyfe woman man tha husbonde greuous synne ye shal ensample pnarracio pthere somtyme man made charke cole wood whan hadde made grete fyre leye nyght therby soo aboute mydnyght come woman rennynge fore man blacke horse fast myght ryde hunted aboute naked swerde aboute fyre last man slewe moman hewe pyeces cast fyre rode agayne myght soo whan man sawe done many nyghtes thenne wente lorde tolde hym mater thenne lorde abolde knyght sayd wyll wyte mente come thyder nyght founde man tolde knyght asked ye spyryte dyde thenne sayd suche man tolde name seruaunt lytell tofore woman knyghtes wyfe leye husbondes lyfe therfore bothe putte penaunce sayd hors yt ryde ye fende yt breneth c folde wors ony fyre myght yt erthe payne must suffre tylle helpe good prayer mass almesdedes tolde hym many thynges knyght dyde thynges sayd sholde theyr helpe delyuered payne euerlastynge blysse whiche god brynge v amen pdnica passione dere frendes daye called sondaye passyon weke daye lorde ihesu cryste begane passyon daye iewes suche enuye hym cause tolde theyr defautes vyces meslyuynge soo cause repreued hym daye full assented hy dethe boute often letted thynge moost fere comyn people helde hym prophete daye knytte theym togyder fully accorded wolde spare thynge sholde deed wherfore gospell telleth cryst preched themple iewes rebuked hy spytuously sayd nuc cognouim qa demoniu habes knowe thou hast fende ye tempte hym haue made hym speke euyll wordes whiche myght haue put hym repreef tolde theym goddes sone redy haue stoned hy deth knewe theyr malyce ihesus aute abscondit se et exiuit de teplo ihesus hyd hym selfe went ye temple thus lorde daye began passyon wherfore holy chirche redeth weke boke iheremye prophete fyrst prophecyed crystes passyon tolde maner iewes sholde doo hym deth thenne ye shall vnderstonde well wyse yt iewes pursued cryst deth wyse fere gretely leste ben moche fals people crystened pursuen cryst heuen holy saynt austyn sayeth synne greuously pursue hym heuen iewes dyde pursueden hym erthe pthen yf ye wyte whiche ben take hede cryste marked theym sayd thus qui ex deo est verba dei audit god hereth worde god hereth worde god swereth many grete othes full falsely ben tho pursuen hym heuen ben gladde theyr hertes whan haue done foule dede grounden foule cursyd lyuynge synne wyll amende theym prechynge techynge euer doo foule dedes anone ben redy fyght chy whith theym telle theym theyr defautes shewed lorde ihesu cryste harme ndycyons people suche dayes shall haue many enemyes wyll saye trouth may preue ensample pnarracio pthere somtyme mawmette cyte wolde telle oony thynge stolen myssed hadde soo happed tyme yonge man hadde stolen thynge ferde mawmette anone wente mawmette sayd thus well wote thou mayste doo grete shame vylony god byleue vpon thou dyscouer wyll breke thy heed soo wente forthe waye soone come myssed good praynge mawmette telle theym hadde whan hadde longe prayed atte laste mawmette spake sayd tymes ben chaunged people ben wors sayth trouthe heed shall broken soo wyll saye trouthe shall shente soo true man shall hunted soo plucked shall wyte whome shall speke whome may telle counseyll truste wyll sonest deceyue hym wyll somtyme speke moost fayrest wryten booke kynges two knyghtes hadde grete enemyte one one hyghte ioab amasa ioab sayd amasa met heyle broder kyssed hym honde behynde slewe hym knyfe smote hym herte pthus fayreth nowe dayes moche people speke full fayre people behynde theym wyll slee theym shrewde knyfe euyll cursed tongue ben pursued hym heuen sette noughte goddes worde though yf theyr e e synketh downe theyr hertes wherfore god playnethe hym greuously prophete iheremye sayd thus gylte founde faders yf haue trespaced ony maner thynge telle ala shame obstynat pryde god ryght soo treateth v ben wronge profred mercy aske maketh hym mercyfull theym dyspleseth hym sheweth loue none worthy thus ben theyr hertes harder ony stone thus ben wors tha iewes thus vnkynde hym shewed v kyndnes euer cryed v sayd haue left erthe ye sholde scrypture torne agayne wyll receyue ye lo armes redy spred clyppe yt heed redy bowed kysse sydes redy shewe myn herte hondes foot bleden shewe suffred thou tornest awaye frome yf thou parfyte lyfe wyll gyue tresour without nombre shall auaunce comparyson gyue reste without ende faute shall founde thus oure lorde profereth techeth v ben full fewe wyll hym lette wordes passe theyr hertes take none hede theyr mynde rychesse prosperyte worlde present lyfe take full lytell hede lyfe comynge lorde ihesu cryst suffred dethe brynge v euerlastyge blysse therfore crystes passyon maketh ye prophete grete lamentacyon grete vnkyndnes seeth mankynde sayth thus thou man vanyte thou stynkest thy rusty synne therfore crye wepe thou hast thy hede garlonde floures haue one thornes thou haste thy hondes payr whyte gloues haue many blody woundes thou haste thyn armes spradde lede karolles daunces armes ben nayled tre sharpe nayles thou haste thy clothes pynched full smale body full grete wheles one thynge greueth moost thou settest passyon suffred full sore thy sake thyn horryble swerynge thou vpbroydeste many grete othes myn heed eyen armes nayles sydes woundes foot bone myn herte passyon thou sholdest doo worshyppe thou doost grete despyte repreef pnarracio pwe rede gestes romayns emperoure sent grete man londe iustyce came noo man countree coude swere othe ye nay whan iustyce came amonge theym made people swere bookes sessyons gaue theym charge soo people toke ensample iustyce swere men dyde oure lordes passyon sydes armes nayles face woudes blode herte forth toke soo vse comyn people swore dyde thenne daye iustyce satte offyce charged people came tofore hym fayre woman clothed grene brought fayre chylde lappe blody martyred heed prycked face dysfygured eyen oute armes broken hondes smyten thorugh nayles cutte foot cutte frome legges sydes rente bowelles herte drawen oute body thenne sayd woman iustyce worthy haue haue thus doo chylde sayd worthy haue dethe thenne sayd thou thy men youre horryble othes haue thus dysmembred swete sone ihesu cryste moder vnto thus ye haue taught youre countree wherfore thou shalt haue thyn owne dome insyght people erthe opened iustyce felle doune helle people sore agast lefte suche othes dyde amende theyr lyues soo lete v leue othes lyue crysten people sholde reuerence passyon lorde ihesu cryst cause redempcyon whiche shall come euerlastynge blysse neuer shall haue ende amen dnica palma rum good frendes ye knowe well sondaye called palme sondaye cause seruyce daye loge wyl telle shortely called palme sondaye saynt iohan sayth lorde ihesu cryst came betanye sayth venit ihesus betaneam vbi lazarus fuit mortu quem resuscitauit reysed lazar frome dethe lyue leye foure dayes deed lazar broder vnto marye mawdeleyne martha syster thenne ihesu cryste wyste passyon nyghe toke lazar hym rydynge asse came towarde iherusalem whan people herde therof people wente agaynst hy non propter ihesu tatum sed vt lazarum viderent quem resuscitauit mortuis onely ihesu see lazar rysen frome dethe lyfe also see cryst hym worshyppe acceperunt ramos palma rum et ster nebat via toke brauches palme floures strawed waye agaynst comynge spradde theyr clothes waye songe benedictus qui venit nomine domini blessed cometh name oure lorde kynge israell wherfore holy chirche maketh daye solempne processyon mynde processyon made agaynst cryst also ioye myrthe rysynge dethe lyfe ley al yere dedly synne trust god ben reysed vnto good lyuynge ouer aungelles heuen make grete ioye vpreysynge oute synne thus take palme floures processyon dyde go processyon knelynge crosse worshyp mynde hym doone crosse worshyppynge welcomynge hym wt songe chyrche people dyde lorde ye cyte iherusalem thenne iohan belet asked questyon sayth yt lorde gretest worshyp rydynge asse euer worlde worshyp crosse asse questyon answereth hymselfe sayth worshyp worlde salomon sayd al vanyte maketh man forgete god hym selfe grete trybulacon dysease heuynes causeth man thynke vpon god crye hym socoure helpe knowe hym selfe therfore crysten people sholde put awaye worldly vanytees bryngeth moche people grete myschefe many euerlastynge payne worshyp crosse cause redepcyon saluacyon brynge v euerlastynge ioye blysse hope come thenne anone whan cryst come cyte iherusalem went temple droue byers seller founde ther sayd domus mea domus orationis vocabi hous hous prayer ye make denne theues thus lorde gaue crysten people ensample leue enge sellynge holy daye especyall chyrche called palme sondaye bycause palme betokeneth vyctorye wherfore crysten people sholde bere palme processyon tokenynge yt hadde foughten fende ennemye hath ye vyctory hym shryft mouthe satysfaccyon dede mekely doone penaunce grete contrycyon herte maner wyse ouercame goostly ennemye fende helle pwe rede gestes romayns ye maner guyse somtyme yf ony londe rebell agaynst themperoure anone themperoure wolde sende worthy knyght grete puyssaunce londe putte theym doune make theym subgettes emperoure rome whan knyght hadde done soo sholde sette chayre arayed clothes golde beste wyse braunche palme honde tokenynge hadde vyctory grete worshyppe broughte rome whan came ony worthy cyte thenne sholde stande one hym bete hym mouth braunche olyue sayenge thus knowe thy selfe vnderstonde though thou grete haue vyctory make moche thy selfe may fortune tyme thou mayst haue worse torne moche vylonye worshyppe therfore proude thy selfe thus sholde ye bete youre selfe mouthe youre soule braunche olyue vertue mekenes soo holde loue meke herte euermore dredynge ferynge leste ye falle agayne synne soo leue worshyppe ye haue trust thus truly mekenes vertue moost soonest ouercometh youre ghoostly enemye fende soonest gadreth man vertuous lyuynge may haue vertue mekenesse pacyence charyte ouercome oure ghostly enemye fende euer amen pferia iiii post festum palma rum dere frendes ye shall vnderstonde holy chirche vsed thre dayes saythe seruyce euen tyde mekenesse wherfore calle tenebre holy chyrche calleth tenebris thenne seruyce thus done mekenesse holy faders tellen thre cause pone nyght lorde taken went vnto ye mounte olyuete prayed thus pater mi si possible est transeat calix iste fader yf possyble bytter passyon may passe fro yf faders wyl ellys drede fere bytter passyo felte spyryte swette bothe blood watyr pand cause anone mydnyghte came iudas fyfty knyghtes moche people take cryst derke coude well knowe saynt iames lyke cryst therfore iudas sayd quem osculatus fuero tenete eum sothe quod hym shal kysse take ye hym saynte iames soo lyke sauyoure ihesu cryst moost parte people called hym crystys owne broder thus ye haue herde iudas betrayed owne mayster thus sauyour ihesu cryst take mekenesse wich spyte enmyte iewes coude doo vntoo hym alsoo betynge oure sauyour ihesu cryste alsoo spyttynge blyssed face pand alsoo thyrde cause whan oure sauyoure ihesu cryste spredde naked vpon holy crosse also whan holy hondes foot hanged nyne clocke vntoo none thenne ye sholde haue seen sonne drawe lyghte soo obscure derke throughe worlde shewynge vnderstondynge maker lyght tyme payned vnto dethe thre certayne cause seruyce nyght done derkenes whiche seruyce maketh mencyon iudas betrayed oure sauyoure lorde ihesu cryste iewes thenne iewes came preuely coude fere drede comyn people wherfore daye belle ronge vnto seruyce sowne made woode tree wherby crysten people may haue knowlege vnderstondynge come vnto holy seruyce preuely secretely without makynge ony maner noyse ouer people sholde speke comynge goynge sholde sowne tree saye holy crosse oure sauyoure ihesu cryste spredde vpon bytter passyo also wordes sauyoure ihesu cryste spake hangynge crosse also sayd vnto blyssed moder mulier ecce filius tuus woman se thy sone thenne oure lorde commaunded blyssed moder vnto saynte iohan euangelyste kepynge sayd theef henge hym sayd thus domyne quado veneris regnu tuum memento mei lorde whan thou comest thy kyngedome haue mynde thenne oure sauyour ihesu cryst sayd vnto hym hodie mecum eris paradiso daye thou shalte paradyse toke spyryte faders hondes sayd manus tuas domine c soo yelded vp ghooste thus comynge goynge chirche crysten people sholde come leue vanyte ydle talkynge speke oonely vnto crosse oure redempcyon cause whan yt iudas betrayed cryst saw treason sholde deed anone felle dyspayre henge hy selfe tre dyspleased cryst dede trespace done fore cryst mercyfull asked mercy sholde haue mercy also seruyce sette certayne candels quere ye vse place vse whiche ben quenched one tokenynge crystys dyscyples wente waye eche whan al candels ben taken way lyght gone yet one bydeth styll whyle tyll ye clerkes haue songe kyryes verse whiche betoken wymmen made lamentacyon crystys sepulcre thenne candell brought agayne another lyght betokeneth blessyd lady fayth lost saue oonely lady al enformed taught also betokeneth cryst hym selfe manhode deed layde ye sepulcre thyrde daye rose frome dethe lyfe gayne gaue lyght loue al deed quenched dyspayre stroke preest gyueth boke betokeneth clappes thonder whan cryste brake hell yates dyspoyled theym fet oute adam eue yt bought bytter passyon haue ye herde somwhat seruyce betokeneth thynke vpon vnkynde lorde god suffred pfor vnkyndnesse synne stynketh syght god saynt ambrose sayth may noo man fynde payne grete ynoughe punysshe vnkyndnesse ye shall ensample pnarracio pi fynde alysaunder neham telleth somtyme knyght whiche went owne countre ferre straunge londe seke aduentures happened came grete forest herde grete noyse best semed dyspayre wolde wete mente wente nere sawe grete horyble adder grete length beclypped lyon bounde hym tree laye slepte wha lyon woke founde hymselfe boude myght helpe hy selfe made horryble noyse desyrynge helpe knyght wolde fayne haue holpen hym drade whan louse lest wolde haue fallen hym bycause knyght lyon kynge beestes dystresse toke swerde dyde smyte adder asonder ye lyon fel ye knyghtes fete alway folowed knyght euery nyght lyon laye beddes foot euery batayle lyon redy helpe mayster moche people spake vntoo knyght lyon yet counsell people lyon insuspecte wherfore whan wente intoo owne countre gayne pryuely whyles lyon slepte toke ye water went shyppe sayled forth whan lyon awoke myssed mayster anone gaue grete rorynge wente hym see swa hym longe myght whan myght fayled hym thenne drowned knyghte ye may vnderstonde goddes sone heuen come oute ferre countree oute heuen worlde boude mankynde olde adder fende tree inobedyence wherfore sharpe swerde passyon losed mankynde oute bou de made hym free goo wolde therfore crysten people ben bounde worshyppe hym thanke hym losynge buxom hym tyme haue lyfe folowe sewe lore holy chyrche shall passe thrughe ye water saye thrugh payne dethe shall come ioye euer shall last withoute ende whiche god brynge v amen pdyuerse questyons many wyll aske dyuerse questyons seruyce dayes suche preestes suppose make redy answere putte hy shame hym vylonye repreef wherfore haue tyteled whiche nedeful euery preest knowe yf wyl loke kepe redely herte may make redy shall hy profyte worshyp fyrst yf man aske sherethursday called ye may saye holy chyrche called cena domini lordes souper day day souped discyples openly souper gaue flesshe blood ete drynke sayd thus accipite et manducate hoc est corpus meu take ye ete myne owne body anone wysshe owne dyscyples foot shewynge mekenes hym ye grete loue theym also englysshe called sherthoursday olde faders dayes people wolde daye shere theyr hedes clyppe theyr berdes polle theyr hedes make theym honest yenst ester day good fryday doo theyr bodyes none ease suffre penaunce mynde hym day suffred passyon man kynde ester euen tyme theyr seruyce seruyce make holy daye wryten lyfe saynte besy saterday none made man shaue hym none fende redy gadred vp here holy saw commaunded hym tell dyde soo sayd thou doost reuerence vnto thy holy daye therfore wyll kepe here tyll day dome grete repreef anone lefte shauynge toke here frome fende made theym brenne owne honde suffre penaunce bode vnshauen tyll monday sayde al thoo repreef worshyp saterday none thenne iohan bellet sayth sherthursday man sholde polle clyppe berde preest sholde shaue crowne soo sholde nothynge twene god hym here come veynes humour stomake sholde pare theyr nayles hondes foot cometh superfluyte fylthe oute forth thenne shryue theym make clene within soule thus make theym clene bothe veyle lente hath drawen twene v quere betokeneth passyon hydde vnknowen tyll day came whiche thyse dayes done waye awter openly shewed people dayes cryste suffred passyon openly hangynge crosse sayenge consumatum est ended saye prophesye passyon hath ende wherfore clothes myne awter ben taken waye crystys clothes take waye hym soo done naked crosse saue oure lady moder wounde karchyf aboute hym couer membres auter stone betokeneth crystys body drawen crosse sky ne parchement harowe al bone myght tolde besom awter wesshen betokeneth scorges bete lordes body thornes crowned water wyne wasshen betokeneth blode water yt ranne downe woundes syde peryshed spere wyne pored vpon awter fyue cross betokeneth blode ra ne downe frome precypall woundes body also day paxe gyuen ye masse iudas betrayed cryst nyght kysse thus prophesye passyon daye ended wherfore nyghte whan souped made sacramente owne body gaue dyscyples ete drynke began sacramente masse newe lawe souper wysshe discyples foot maner newe lawe full sayd peter wasshen clene dedly synne hath nede wasshen betokeneth afflyccyon dedly synne thenne yf people aske preestes masse souper cryst dyde tourned honest saluacyon mannes soule haymo telleth vpon ye pystle saynt poule many begynnynge fayth come chirche sherethurdaye ryche brought mete drynke theym eten dranke theyr bellyes full thenne atte nyght tooke theyr housell sayd cryste gaue ensample whan ryche ete dranke moche poore people abydeth withoute tylle ryche hath done sore hu gred thenne ete releef lefte soo people toke theyr housell pystle daye telleth saynt poule rebuked theym therof tourned foule vse honest clennesse holynesse saye atte masse fastynge people take theyr housell fastynge eester euen pascall made chyef tapre chirche soo cryste chyef aboue ye sayntes heuen pascall also betokeneth pyler lyght fyre wente moyses chyldern israell whan moyses ladde theym egypte londe byhest iherusalem soo passed saue sounde soo seuen dayes come vnto see thanked god theyr passage mynde holy chirche vseth eester weke goo processyon fonte reed see crysten people ben crystened fonte water fonte betokeneth reed see bloode water wounde crystes syde whiche power pharao fende helle drowned myght loste crysten people saued fonte halowed eester euen wytson euen begynnynge chyldern abode crystened vnto two dayes crystened atte fonte halowynge cause many longe abydyge deed withouten crystendome therfore holy chyrche ordeyned crysten tymes yere saue eyght dayes fore euyns chylde shall byde fonte halowynge yf may peryl deth ellys thus pascall halowed lyght newe fyre tapres candelles ben lyght al holynes good techynge good lyuynge cometh cryst techynge holy chyrche lyghteth crystes passyon brennyng loue charyte pyeces conscyence ben stycked pascall maner crosse token fyue woundes lorde bede sayeth suffred body shall fresshe swete ony enscence tyl day dome grete repreef shall dampned byleue crystes passyo wyl aske mercy yeuenes theyr synnes fonte halowynge preeste casteth water foure partyes fonte cryste dyscyples goynge prechynge techynge foure partyes crystendome name fader sone holy ghoost preest bretheth water holy ghost makyng worlde borne water whan god adam synne cursyd erthe londe cursed water wherfore lawfull man ete lenten ye cometh water droppeth wexe water candell brennyng whiche betokeneth hode cryst fulled water putteth oyle creme water ye vertue sacramente ben heuen erthe ioyned gyder preued crystes baptysme fader heuen spake sayd hic est filius meus dilect quo mi hi bene coplacui welbeloued sone wyll please holy ghoost sicut columba whyte douue pthus onte halowed two tymes ye yere whytsontyde ester whan people broughte thraldum crystes passyon fro ye daunger fende atte wytsontyde holy ghoost gyuen remyssyon synnes thenne frome fonte people gone quere syngynge letanye prayenge sayntes heuen praye god gyue yt ben crysten kepe worthy sacrament goddes pleasaunce couenaut haue made theyr crystenynge thenne preest gooth masse cryste heed holy chirche rysen kyryeleyson sayd euery prayer especyall masse grete nede aske helpe socour god kepe v frome maner temptacyon fende putteth v namely goddes seruyce gloria excelsis sayd fader heuen hath grete ioye beholde people sone hath bought passyon see pea reste charyte eche one greyle sayd ben newe crystened ben yet parfyte walke grace vertues alleuya sayd grete ioye aungels see crystenynge nombre restored ayen alleluya tract sayd hyghe songen thoughe crystenynge wasshed frome synne yet must traueyll besely kepe frome comberaunce fende falle deedly synne offertory sayd woman comen oynementes offre crystes body founde hy tombe agn dei sayd paxe gyuen cryst heed pea rysen postcomyn said ben newe crystened sholde houseled day morowe olde tyme came crystenynge people grete age thenne shorte euensonge done chyldern crystened wherof gretely noyed sykenes colde longe seruyce thenne endeth vnder shorte colet ye sacramente crystenynge ended passyon cryste whiche crysten people restored euerlastynge blysse ye whiche god brynge v amen pin die parasceues good frendes daye called good frydaye al lorde ihesu cryst suffred daye tourned v grete ioye daye suffred passyon vnder ponce pylate sake olde sawe foule begynnynge hathe foule endynge se pylate began cursedly endeth full wretchedly saynt austyn sayeth cursed lyuynge fyrst asketh cursed ende forgeteth hym selfe lyuynge full lyke forgete hymself last ende pylate knyghtes sone called tyrus gate hym woma hyght pyle woman fader hyght ate whan chylde borne sette moders name grande fader bothe name called hym pylate thenne whan thre yere aege moder broughte hym kynges courte knyght sone nye lyke pylates aege knyghtes sone rule gentyller manfully goodly beloued pylate hate enuye therof pylate daye slewe knyghtes sone knight wonder sory yet wolde sle pylate sent hym rome hostage trybute yt knyght sholde paye themperour happed yt kynge fraunce sent sone thyder ye cause cause whan pylate sawe beloued cherysshed therfore pilate slewe hy cursed emperour counceyle ye romaynes sent pylate countre called po ce people coutre cursed yt slewe ony yt came theyr mayster ouer whan pylate came thyder applyed hym theyr maners yt wyles subtylte ouercame maystry gate name called pylate ponce grete domynacyon power kynge iherusalem sent made hym lyuetenaunt vnder hy londe iury pylate lyked well thoffyce pryuely sent themperour offyce confermed hym vnwetynge kynge herode tyme beynge ky ge wherfore whan kynge herode herde done wrothe enmyes vnto tyme yt lorde ihesu cryst take became frendes agayne fell bothe one assent crystes dethe thenne happened afterwarde ye themperour fel seke sent cryste hele hym tolde hym cryst heled euer wolde come hym al maner sekenes euer pylate done hym dethe messenger came whan emperour vnderstode sente pylate made hym come hym pylate herde sore aferde toke crystes cote whan came rome emperour presence made pylate good chere whyle crystes cote emperoure swore sholde deed thenne toke cote anone cote emperoure sore wrothe pylate put hym pryson tyll hadde taken counceyl dethe sholde deye thenne soone pylate wyst vnderstode sholde deed toke owne knyfe slewe hym selfe therwith whan emperour herde therof dyde vnderstande hadde slayne hym self knyfe thenne anone commaunded bynde grete stone forsayd pylates necke caste hym ryuer rome named tyber without euer sene people thenne whan casten therin fendes made suche noyse aboute cyte rome sore afreyed thenne whan emperoure sawe made take hym vp ayen thenne caste water bytwix two hye hylles longe tyme water many horryble syghtes seen aboute cursed man pthus oure lorde ihesu cryste suffred passyon dethe mankynde fyrste whan taken dyde buffet hym stryped hym naked bete hym scourge vertice capitis v que ad plantas pedum non fuit eo sanitas frome hyest place heed soole foot thynge lefte hole hym rawe made crowne thornes sette heed bete doune staues reed perysshed brayne whan payned hym ladde hym forth blody admonte caluarie mount caluarye thende dethe yet woman cyte wha see hym foule faren lugged drawen veray pyte wepte vpon hym thenne sayd lorde nolite flere super sed super vos filios vestros ye woman iherusalem wepe ye vpon youre chyldern shall dayes come whiche ye shall blysse wombes barayne pappes neuer gaue souke thus oure lorde preched vengeaunce fylle vpon iherusalem whiche prophecye iheremye prophete spake redde holy chirche thre dayes atte tenebras whiche horryble many dyuerse myschyues especyall hungre chyldern laye deed hungre stretes thenne waman come grete byrthe hungre tooke owne chylde deed pappes slewe parted two partyes rosted halfe halfe kepte tylle morowe thenne people came strete hadde sauoure rost anone came haue hadde parte therof whan sawe moder roste owne chylde soone heuy foule dysmayed wolde ete therof wente theyr waye forth ayen thenne tooke moder chylde ete therof sayd maner wyse myn owne sone myn owne chylde bare body fedde pappes wyll rather ete deye hungre therfore telle shewe somwhat vengeaunce fylle iherusalem dethe oure lorde ihesu cryst thenne ladde hym ye mout caluarye streyned hym soo crosse euery bone body myght knowen one nayled hym honde foote crosse lyfte vp crosse boody togyder grete peyce lete crosse body falle doune togyder mortesse body dasshed bone craked ioyntes vaynes braste oute blode sydes armes legges foot hondes blode lefte hym yet toke clothe whyle blode hote wonde aboute body tylle blode colde thenne drewe awaye clothe pulled awaye flesshe fro bone grete pyte soo whan sholde deye began iohan belet sayth deus meus respice soo sayd verse suynge tylle come vnto verse te dne speraui soo atte verse manus tuas dne commendo spiritum meum redemisti domine deus veritatis gaue vp spyryte grete ensample oure lorde ihesu cryste gaue crysten people euery man sholde haue mynde verse theym saye saye theym euery daye shall deye maner myschyuous vengeable deth passyon saye orysones knelynge euery oryson saue oryson sayd iewes ye oryson holy chyrche kneled cause iewes scorne knelynge thre tymes cryst whan scrourged hym thenne thyse orysons holy chirche prayed maner people iewes sarasyns cysmatyks heretyks crysten people whyle ony man woman standeth acursyd dampned god dampned shall deth repente hy made hy whyle lyueth presente worlde take hede saynt austyn sayth siscirem certo pater meus esset inferno non orarem pro illo nisi vt dyabolo yf wyst trouth fader dampned helle wolde neuer praye hym deuyll helle ther prayer holy chirche helped dampned man thenne thyse orysons crosse brought forth whiche crysten people sholde worshyp hym daye deyed crosse praye lorde forgiue v trespace cryst prayed fader heuen forgyue dyde hym crosse pnarracio pthere knyght somtyme grete lorde hadde worthy man vnto sone happed knyght man felle debate knyghte slewe hym wherfore fader man deed gadred grete multytude people dystroye vtterly vndo hym pursued knyghte place euerhe wente haue slayne hym nyght daye myght haue rest euer dyde flee fere lyf thenne happed good frydaye knyght sawe crysten people go chirche bethought hym cryste deyed daye crosse mankynde put hym onely mercy almyghty god wente chirche people serue god chirche anone knyght worde come moche people chirche swerde drawen honde slee hym whan knyght sawe wyst well trespaced hym fylle downe flatte grounde armes spradde abrode lorde ihesu cryste spradde armes crosse sayd loue daye spradde hi armes ye crosse suffredde passyon deyed al mankynde haue thou mercy forgyue thy sone deth thenne knyght thought horryble thynge smyte hym whyle laye cryed hym mercy mekely anone put vp swerde sayd hym maner wyse loue day deyed crosse mankynde fyrgyue toke forsayd man vp kyssed hym anone went doo worshyp crosse knelynge whan knyght wolde haue kyssed ye foot crosse ymage loused armes fro crosse beclypped knyght necke kyssed hym spake thus people herde forgyue thou hast forgyuen loue thus cryste people sholde thenne sholde haue mercy grace god euerlastynge blysse amen pin die pasce good frendes ye shall knowe wel daye called many place goddes soday ye knowe wel ye maner euery place worshyp daye fyre halle ye blacke wynter brondes thynge foule fume smoke shall done awaye fyre shall gayly arayed fayre floures strewed grene rysshes aboute shewynge grete ensample crysten people lyke made clene theyr house vnto rhe syght people wyse ye sholde clense soulys doyng way foule brenny ge synne lecherye put waye cast thy foule dust strewe soulys floures fayth thus make soulys able receyue lorde god feest ester deponentes omnen maliciam put waye malyce sorowe ryght ye wyll suffre nothynge house stynketh sauoureth euyll wher ye may deceyued ryght cryst whan cometh hous soules finde ony stynke wrath enuy ony dedly synne wyll abyde none goth waye thenne cometh fende abydeth thenne may soule forsaken god betaken vnto fende thus wrath enuy ony dedely synne wyll forgyue hathe trespaced vnto prayer shall forgyuenes haue oure lorde sayeth thus dimittite et dimitte mini forgyue ye shal haue forgyuenes therfore euery crysten man woman sholde serche well theyr co scyence make able receyue theyr sauiour ihesu cryst god man pnarracio pthere tyme holy bysshop prayed often tymes besely vnto god myghte haue grace see knowe whiche worthy receyue holy sacrament come goddes borde thenne tyme houseled ye people saw come theyr face reed blood dropped theyr mouthes theyr face blacke ony pytche fayre reed lusty holde whyte ony snowe thenne amonge sawe two comyn woman come theyr face shone bryght sonne bysshop grete meruayle syght prayed god gyue hym reuelacyon betokeneth thenne came hym aungell sayd haue blody face blode droppeth theyr mouthes ben enuyous people wrathfull wyll amende theym selfe therof euer backebytynge sclaundrynge theyr neyghbours ben euer redy swere othes therfore theyr mouthes shall droppe blacke blode tyll come amendement haue blacke face pytch lecherous wyll leue theyr synne ben grete synners many degree wyl amende haue theyr face whyte ony snowe yt haue done grete synne ben shryuen therof sory theyr synnes wepynge theyr eyen hath wasshed theyr soules made clene ben clene lyfe truely laboure theyr lyuynge two comyn woman shyne bryght passynge grete synners sore aferde whan came chyrche toke grete repentaunce theyr hertes yt made vowe god praynge hym hartely take noo vengeaunce wolde forsake theyr synne neuer amysse wherfore god grete grace mercy hath forgyuen theyr trespace theyr synnes sorowe theyr hertes hath wasshen theyr soules yt shyne bryghter aungell went waye bysshop kneled doune tha ked god reuelacyon therfore take example two comyn woman sory synnes repent hertes purpose neuer torne ayen synne trust verely ye shall haue grace socoure endles blysse wherfore thyke certayne though ye make glosyge wordes dysceyue goostly fader saye ye charyte ye begyle selfe truste truly ye shall begyle god seeth euery corner herte therfore deceyue owne soules ye loue god also besy redy meke soules clene syght god ye ben make house syght men ye wolde aray best clothes ye haue agaynst comyge best frendes sholde ye araye receyue best frende maker lorde ihesu cryste tyme suffred passyon dethe brynge v euerlastynge lyfe daye called passynge daye especyall two cause one daye crysten people reuerence god sholde forgyue theym haue trespaced perfyte loue charyte crysten people haue mysse done yere daye sholde amended salue heleth sore yt charyte caritas cooperit multitudinem peccato rum charyte couereth multitude synnes also passynge daye daye sholde goddes chyldren passe euyll lyuynge good lyuynge vyces vertues pryde mekenes couetyse largenes slouthe holynes enuye loue charyte wrathe mercy glotony abstynence oute lechery chastyte fendes clawes oure mortall ennemye goddes armes grete ennemy make dere frende passeth thus worthy come good feest whiche lorde ihesu cryst maketh daye people called also goddes sonday daye goddes sone rose frome dethe lyfe soo gladded seruauntes vprysynge wherfore holy chyrche maketh myrth melody daye syngeth thus phec est dy quam fecit dominus exultemus le temur ea daye lorde made ioy glad wt hertes fader heue aungelles maketh grete melodye vprysynge sone maketh daye passynge grete feest byddeth crysten people therto well yt ben heuen ben erthe shall full welcome cometh feest clothed goddes lyuery good clothyng loue charyte also euyll shall welcome yt shal come fendes leuery clothed wrathe enuy gospell telleth shall caste pryson hell whyle laugheth make mery shall wepe sory whyle ete drynke goddes borde shal gnasshe wt theyr tethe saye quante sunt tenebre wo wo wo many derkenes ben shall thynke may fele derkenes derke paynes hell shall harde wormes shall gnawe theym ete theyr euen crysten erthe false backebytynge sclaundrynge wherfore charge goddes name yt none come thus goddes borde yf ye perfyte loue charyte clene shryuen full purpose leue synne wyste certayne whiche charyte deedly synne muste lawe holy chyrche loude voyce say thus hym audyence people gyue thy housell thy saluacyon thy dampnacyon tyll yu come amendement therfore euery crysten man woman sholde serche well conscyence make hym able receyue sauyour ihesu cryst helth soule maye come fynall lyfe euerlastynge ioye amen progationum pferia iiiiiiiii ante ascencionem dni fredes thyse thre dayes saye modaye tuysdaye wenesdaye ye shall fast go processyon man woman seruaunte syners haue nede praye god helpe grace mercy may excuse fro processyon may lawfully thenne yt wtdrawe hy self fro ye comaundemet holy chirche wylfully synneth full greuously fyrst synned pryde vnbuxon also synned slouthe knoweth hym self synne wyll dylygence come therof ryght withdraweth hym people ben gadred serue god ryght wyll god put hym company heuen prayer yt ben done holy chirche tyll come amendemet therfore crysten people come oonly gyder praye thyse thre dayes sayntes heuen praye god v haue syned many tymes yere ayenst commaundement god therfore thyse thre dayes shall fast praye god mercy remyssyon synnes put awaye power fende kepe v myschyef perylles drede fallen tyme yere ony tyme tyme fall many grete thondres lyght wynges lyncolnyence sayth fendes fleteren thayer fere ye blast thondrynge whan cryst come helle yates whan dyspoylled helle yet whan thonder thayer ben soo agast therof fallen downe thenne go vp ayen tyll haue done rered cursyd dedes make tempestes see drawe downe shyppes make debate amonge people make one slee tende fyre brenne house drawe downe steeple tree cause wyme ouerlaye theyr chyldern make peple hage themself drowne selfe wanhope dyspayre doo many cursed dedes put awaye suche myscheues power fende holy chyrche hath ordeyned al crysten people shall faste go processyon thre dayes pray god lady sayntes heuen helpe socoure wherfore processyons belle rongen baners dysplayed crosse cometh people sueth ryght kyge whan gooth batayle trompettes gooth tofore baners cometh kynge hoost folowynge processyon belle goddes trompettes baners cometh cometh crosse crystes lykenes kynge crysten people sue hym theyr good prayer chase awaye fendes haue power lyke cursed tyraunt wyll sore aferde adred whan hereth trompettes kynge ennemye seeth baners spleyed felde hoost comy ge towarde hym wyse ye fende tyraunte hell aferde dredeth hym sore whan belle rynge baners ben borne crosse people come prayenge fleeth dare abyde putteth awaye power processyon pnarracio pwe rede ye cyte constantyne people went processyon dysease yt people songe latyny sodaynly lytell chylde plucked vp ayre borne heuen angelles taught hy synge ge sete de scte fortis scte et imortalis miserere nobis anone laten doune agayn ye erthe songe ye songe anone delyuerd theyr dyseases say englysshe holy god holy stronge god holy wtout dethe haue mercy v god yt holy neuer shall dye haue mercy v god wylleth wyl stronge fyght fende ye worlde ye flesshe thenne wyll haue mercy v brynge v place thenne angelles synge sancte de sancte fortis holy god holy stroge god haue mercy v bryng v blysse amen pin die ascensionis dni good frendes suche daye ye shal haue hye solempne fest holy chirche called ascensyon lorde ihesu cryst daye fayth byleue techeth god god man styed vp heuen wherfore tokenyng pascall chyef lyght holy chirche hath stande openly quere ester vnto daye remeued awaye tokenynge cryste chyef lyght holy chirche lorde dyuerse tymes openly appyered dyscyples taught theym fayth byleue daye styed vp heuen wyll abyde vntyll daye dome ye shall maner ye ascensyon ester daye tyll daye dyscyples alwaye dyuerse tymes appyered vnto appyred saten theyr mete ete wt shewe yt god man flesshe blood doubte lest spyryte yt nother flesshe ne blood therfore preue trouth ete wt theyr syght badde go ye hylle olyuete syght dyscyples blessyd styed vp heuen left ye steppe foot threst downe ye harde marbyll stone token ascensyon thenne ye shall vnderstande ye hylle olyuete betokeneth mercy wherfor cryste styed vp hylle olyuete shewynge wel heed mercy euer redy gyue mercy aske mercy meke herte thenne vpstyeng calle ascesyon angelles made moche melody yt tonge may telle glade comynge ascendit velociter styed vp swyftly momet erthe heuen grete clerke phylosopher yt called rabby moyses sayth ferre heuen erthe holy man myght lyue thousande yere euery daye go thousande myle yt met waye knoweth best waye shall met ryghtfull good man pthenne ascensyon hadde hym grete multytude soules whiche fette helle fendes boundes styed vp also wt woundes reed fresshe blody bede sayth fyue cause fyrst verifye ye fayth resurrecon rose flesshe blood deyed crosse mankynde seconde shewe woundes fader grete helpe socour al mankynde thyrde shewe ryghtful dampned yt wyll byleue passyon resurreccyon iiii shewe mercyfull vnto wyll byleue aske mercy fyfth bare hym sygne vyctorye sykernesse mankynde lyke lorde syker hath true aduocate iuge answere hy lyke wyse mankynde fynde hym aduocat euermore redy answere v nede ye fende ghostly enemye maketh ayenst v wherfore sayth holy scrypture asykerer attorneye may noo man god vbi mater ostendit filio pectus et vbera wherfore moder sheweth sone brestes pappes filius patri latus et vulnera sone sheweth fader sydes beten woudes bledynge sholde ony thy ge put away ordeyned ther suche token loue shewed may fare yll yt hath suche ii fredes heue also styenge vp heuen lorde ihesu cryst man hath goten grete dygnyte man se owne fleshe blood syttynge ryght syde fader heuen trone wherfore aungels consyderynge ye dygnyte man wolde suffre man worshyp dyde thyncarnacyon cryst worshyp man god hymselfe hath take mankynde hy heuen bodely man may see moche beholde god boude thral fende helle nowe made frere lorde ihesu cryst hath gyuen man fredom aboue ony angel therfore bounde vnto hym hym seruyce reuerence worshyp angelles kept somtyme ye yates paradyse brennynge swerdes soule myght come inne fayth lorde ihesu cryst mankynde hath cast vp ye yates warneth man entre therin stedfast byleue saynt austyn sayth aperuisti credentibus regna celo rum thou hast opened yates heuen byleue also ye shall byleue ryght kyng worlde hath countree offycers dyuerse degree hyer lower preuyer lorde styenge vp tyme lower angel grete wonder crystys ascensyon whan sawe hym flesshe blood styenge vp heuen grete multytude soules hym also grete wondre whan sawe fendes ayer flee awaye drede fere stronge comyge wonte sparynge nothyge assayle ye soules yt come thene flewe awaye grete fere comyge also good angel came ye hast yt myght doo lorde ihesu cryste seruyce reuerence worshyp thus grete wonder yt lower angel vp styenge asketh hyer angel sayd quis est iste qui venit de eodem cometh worlde blody clothes kyng ioye deth suffry ge reed scourgynge syke deed crosse stronge helle bodely doynge ferfull rysynge thus hath ouercome ennemys kyng glorye heuen pthenne whan lorde ihesu cryst styed vp heuen thene dyscyples standynge moder grete wonder syght also melodye herde thayer loked vp heuen sodaynely two angel clothed whyte stode theym sayd thus viri galilei quid statis aspicientes celu hic ihesus qui assumptus est vobis men galyle stande ye beholdynge heue ihesus styed vp shall come daye dome ayen deme quycke deed therfore crysten people lyfte vp hertes lorde ihesu herte shall haue mercy shall saued though man neuer synfull wyll aske mercy meke herte wyl gyue hym mercy cor contritu et humiliatu deus non despicies meke contryte herte god shal neuer despyse wyll aske mercy sory synnes lorde wyll take hym mercy thenne shewe grete goodnesse copassyon yt lorde hath mankyde shall telle ensaple pwe rede lyfe saynt carpe man mysse beleue torned crysten man faythe narracio forsoke beleue crystendome wherfore holy man carpe sore angred fell grete sykenes whan sholde haue prayed god amendement dyde pray god nyght daye myght se haue bodely vengeaunce thene happed mydnyght prayed thus sodaynly house lay cleued foure partes loked vp sawe one hanged pyteously pyte se loked vp heuen sawe lorde ihesu cryste grete multytude aungelles syttynge trone loked vp agayne vengeaunce wonder fayne therof loste syght lorde ihesu cryst holy aungelles herte two mennes vengeaunce sorye soo longe put vnto theyr payne rose went hym selfe helped euer myght whan ouen carpe gladde therof thenne loked vp heuen sawe lorde ihesu cryste sawe hym ryse frome trone grete pyte compassyon two men came downe toke theym theyr payne sayd thus carpe extede manus tuas contra stretche meum take ye ete myn owne flesshe blode dyde sholde haue mynde hym gaue al prestes power make owne body breed wyne thus euery preest hathe power make sacrament good bad sacrament may noo man amende ne appayre yt good man holy contemplatyf lyuer helpeth gretely whiche prayeth saynge masse mynystreth offyce preest worthely truely appertayneth hygh ordre preesthode shal glad ioyfull euer borne haue mynystred worthely precyous body sauyour redemptoure fourme breed lorde ihesu cryste grete goodnesse hathe gyuen preest gyfte power erthe whiche gaue neuer aungelles heuen ye loue man make owne body fourme breed therfore ye shall haue worship heuen ony tongue tell herte thyke euyl lyuer knoweth hy selfe deedly syne presumeth mynyster worthy sacrament wyll amende hym may sure perpetuall dampnacyo fendes hell euerlastynge payne detestable tourmentes haue well deserued theyr vnclene lyuynge thenne ye shall vnderstande mooste benygne mercyfull sauyour graunteth moost worthy sacrament precyous body vsed mynystred euermore moder holy chyrche foure cause necessary nedefull vnto crysten people pthe fyrste mannes grete helpynge ayde pthe seconde redemptoures passyon myndynge pthe thurde grete loue shewynge pand fourthe grete mede getynge pnota quod propter nouem raciones prodest homini audire missam secundum augustinum psaynt augustyn sayeth prouffyteth gretely crysten people masse specyally nyne cause sayth maner wyse quia illo die qua audierat missam necessaria cibaria conceduntur pfor daye hereth masse shall fayle noo bodely fode sustenaunce necessary thynge shall belongy ge appertaynynge vnto hym lette ne impedyme te shall haue iourney hath go ryde euer trauayleth seconde cause venyall sy ne shall forgyuen hym vertue ye masse ydle wordes thyrde yf man deye shall stande hy housell fourth shall yt daye lese syght fyfth ydle othes daye shal forgyue hy vi daye shall deye soden deth vii longe hereth masse shal wexe olde viii steppe towarde warde holy chyrche good aungell rekeneth saluacyon ix ye whyle beholdeth holy sacrament wyckedde spyrytes flee hym haue power ouer hym neuer grete synner helpe socoure haue holy ghost sacrament herein erthe last ende crysten people wyll sende preest come hym goddes body receyue knowynge well byleueth stedfastly yt flesshe blood yt cryste toke lady saynt mary borne body god man suffred passyon dethe crosse mankyde layde tombe rose fro deth lyf sytteth fade ryght honde heue shall come ayen daye dome deme quycke deed euery man deseruynge parfyght byleue crysten people shal armed made stronge withstande fendes wyll come assayle departynge bytwene body soule thenne fendes comen besely brynge hym byleue thenne shall sacrament man hath receyued lyf make hym myghty stronge shall sette fendes nought ouercome theym skylle sacrament brought man aske mercy cryst remyssyon synne hauynge full trust byleue cryste euer redy forgyue al wyll aske mercy meke herte dauyd sayth cor contritu et humiliatu deus non despicies contryte herte meke lorde shall neuer despyse may seues whiche men cursed lyuynge therfore ordeyned deed one asked mercy meke herte sayd domine dum venet regnum tuum memento mei lorde quod whan thou comest thy kyngedome haue mynde anone fyrst askynge gaue hym mercy ouer sayd thus hym hodie mecum eris paradiso daye thou shalt paradyse wolde aske mercy wyse pryde herte therfore dampned helle thus lorde ihesu cryste shedde blode vpon crosse helthe al mankynde masse shewith blode grete socoure helpe saluacyon mankynde ye flesshe blode shewed euery day masse sholde beleue stedfastly yt beleueth thereon verely shall saued dredeful daye dome narracio ptherfore tell ensample lyfe odo bysshop caunterbury pthis bysshop hadde hym clerkes beleued perfytely sacrament awter sayd myght beleue body cryst myght mynystred masse bysshop sory prayed god besyly theyr amendemet daye whan masse made fraccyon sawe blode droppe frome host ye chalyce thenne made sygne vnto theym beleued come nere hym se whan sawe fyngers blody blode ranne frome thoost ye chalyce anone grete fere cryed sayd thou blyssed man hast grace holde crystes body thyn hondes yt droppeth blode ye chalyce beleue verely theron beseche pray hym v yt yu haste thyn hondes yt take vengauce v mysbyleue crye mekely mercy anone ost torned fourme breed fyght men byleue skyll sacramet made awter make man often syght therof ye sooner haue myde crystys passyon haue myde ye best defence ayenst temptacon fende saynt austyn sayth mynde crystys passyo putteth awaye temptacyons power wycked spyrytes cause roodes ymages ben set hye ye chirches soone man cometh chirche sholde see haue myde thyke cristis passyo wherfore cross ymages full necessary nedefull someuer thyse lollers saye ful profytable holy faders wolde haue destroyed many yeres agone ryght ye peple done worshyp ye kyges seale loue ye seale reuerence kyng yt cometh fro roodes ymages set ye kynges seale heuen saytes ye wyse ymages ben lewde peples bokes iohan belet sayth ben many thousandes peple yt ymagyne hertes cryst done ye crosse se ymagis ye chirches place ben haue ye bytter myde crystis passyon tell ensample pnarracio pthere crysten man englond yt went ye holy londe hyred hethen man guyde came fayr forest sawe many fayr thyges crysten man merueyled gretely yt herde noyse byrdes therof grete merueyll sayd hethen man merueyll moche yt songe byrdes wode sayd hethen man ye weke yt ye calle passyo weke yt grete phete deyed wherfore sondaye ye last yt ye calle palme sondaye ye foules wood deyed sorowe al weke shall lye deed daye nexte come yt ye calle ester daye quycken ayen yere make melodye wherfore loke vp tree see sawe euery bowe tree lye full byrdes flat spred ye crosse thene syth byrdes haue myde crystys passyon make suche morny ge sorowe moche cause makyde yt brought fro euerlastyge dapnacyon euerlastyge saluacyon passyon thyrde cause ye sacramet vsed awter man sholde ye syght therof thyke god ihesu cryst fader heuen yt hath one sone yt loued passy ge thyge spared sende hy downe world suffre passyo deth shedde pcyous blood mankyde bye hy ye fendes bondes wryte charter wt owne pcyous blood fredom euermore mankynde yt man forfeyt charter dedely syne yt loued god wyll kepe charter god asketh man loue sayth th da mihi cor tuu sufficit mihi sone gyue thyn herte ynough thenne take hede ensample pnarracio pthere erle venys yt called syre ambryzt yt loued ye sacrament ye awter passynge well dyde ye worshyp reuerence yt coude myght wha leye syke sholde deed myght receyue ye sacramet castynge thene sory made dole thene lete make clene ryght syde couer fayre clothe sendell leyde goddes body therin sayd thus thost lorde yu knowest yt loue ye herte wolde feyne receyue ye wt mouth durst therfore may leye yt place yt next herte shewe loue herte yt may wherfor beseche ye good lorde haue mercy euen therwith syght people hym syde opened thost went syde thenne closed ayen anone deyed departed worlde lete v loue sacrament lyf reuerence worshyp thenne laste ende whan shall deye passe worlde wyll socour v brynge v euerlastynge blysse thus sacrament vsed grete mede getynge byleue therin thoughe haue lykenes breed taast flesshe semeth breed quycke semeth deed ye must byleue verely goddes blessyd body toke fleshe blood ye virgyn mary deyed ye crosse roos fro deth lyf styed vp heuen sytteth faders ryght honde shal come ayen daye dome deme quycke deed receyue byleueth verely therupon shall haue euerlastynge lyf ye kyngdom heuen gospel sayth qui manducat huc pane viuet ineternu ereth breed shal lyue euer neuer deed receyued byleued thus reus erit iudicio daye dome shall dampned euerlastynge payne augustin sona xpi manduca non mutabis te sed tu mutaberis saynt austyn sayth persone cryste ete shall torne chauge yu shalt torne chauge pnarracio pwe rede iewe went cryste man felowe chirche crysten people herde masse et post missa dixit iudeus whan masse done iewe sayd ye crysten man siego tantum edisse quatu tu comedisti esuria vt puto trib dieb yf eeten moche yu hasteten wolde hu gred trowe thre dayes thene sayd ye cryste ye iewe vere nihil comedi forsoth sayth ye crysten ye iewe ete maner mete daye sayd iewe ego vidite comedere puerum pulcerrimu quale sacerdos eleuauit ad altare sawe ye ete childe ye whiche ye preest helde vp awter et tuc venit pulcerrim ho habens mltos pueros gremio suo thene came sayr man many child lappe et dedit vnicui que vestru vnu pueru tale quale sacerdos medit gaf eche crysten man childe suche ye preest ete pyet sharpe byleue ye holy sacrament wyll telle ensample pnarracio pwe rede saynt gregoryes tyme woman yt hyght lacyua made breed ye pope prestes synge housel wt people whan pope came woman gyue housel sayd goddes body woman smyled laughed tha pope wtdrewe honde layd ost vpon ye awter torned woman lacyua sayd smylest yu whan yu sholdest receyue crystis body sayd callest yu crystis body yt made wt myn owne honde gregory ye pope sory mysbyleue bad ye peple praye god shewe myracle womas helpe whan hadde prayed longe gregory wente ye awter ayen foude ye ost torned reed flesshe blood bledyng shewed woma thene cryed sayd lorde crye ye mercy byleue yt yu art god man goddes sone heuen fourme breed thene badde gregory ye peple praye ayen yt sholde torne ayen bredes lyknesse dyde wt ye ost houseled woma lacyua therfore lete v ye worshyp may sacrament may mysbyleue pnarracio palso fynde deuenshyre besyde exbrydge woman yt laye seke nye deed sente holy parsone mydnyght haue ryghtes man haste myght arose went chyrche toke goddes body boxe yuory put bosom went forthe warde woman wet forest fayre mede nexte way happed boxe fell bosome grounde went forth wyst came woman herde confessyon asked yf wolde houseled sayd ye syr thene put hande bosom sought boxe whan founde full sory sad sayd dame wyll go goddes body come agayne anone went forth sore wepynge symplenes came wylowe tree made therof rodde stryped hym self naked bete hym selfe blode ranne doune sydes sayd thus hym selfe thou symple man haste thou loste thy lorde god thy maker thy fourmer creatour whan thus bete hym selfe dyde clothes went forthe ware pyller fyre lasted frome erthe heuen astonyed therof yet blyssed hym went laye sacrament fallen boxe grasse pyler shone bryght sonne lasted frome goddes body heuen beestes forest comen goddes body stode compasse rounde kneled iiii knee saue one blacke horse yt kneled one knee thenne sayd yf yu ony beest may speke charge yt goddes name present fourme breed tell thou knelest one knee sayd fende hell wyll knele myght made agaynst wyll wryten euery knelynge heuen erthe shall worshyp lorde god arte thou lyke horse sayd make people stele suche towne one hanged suche toune sayd holy persone commaunde goddes flesshe bloode thou go wyldernesse yu shalte neuer dysease crysten people anone went waye might lenger abyde man wet forth woman dide ryghtes whiche saued wente euerlastynge saluacyon whiche brynge v yt v shed blode ye way saynt iohan sawe hym sayd dyscyples ecce agn dei q tollit p ta mundi se lambe god shall awaye synne ye worlde saynt andrewe herde anone left saynt iohan baptyst sued cryste whan herde cryst preche pleased hym soo well anone went fetched peter broder cryst preche kest grete loue god soone see galyle fysshynge cryste came called anone left fysshynge shyppe nette yt hadde sued cryste euer hy vntyll styed vp vnto realme heuen pnarracio pthenne saynt andrewe preched amonge people thenne daye preched happed soo man amonge people called nycoll lyued many wynters lechery yet grace god thought amende lyfe whan herde worde god grete vertue sholde put away temptacyonns synne lete wryte gospell bare hym soeuer went wc vertue therof abstayned hymselfe fro synne yet day temptacyon fende forgate hymselfe went agayne brodelles hous vsed came woman loked vpon hym cryed hym sayd thou olde sely man doost thou go home agayne se many meruayles yt may haue nycoll thoughte yt ye gospell vpon hym anone went saynt andrewe tolde hym case prayed saynt andrewe pray hy yt soule myght saued saynt andrewe wolde ete ne dryke tyl wyst yf nycol sholde saued saynt andrew fasted v dayes breed water prayenge nyght day came voyce sayd yu hast fasted prayed make nycoll thenne shall saued thenne saynt andrewe badde nycoll faste fyue dayes breed water praye besely vnto god dyde thenne come voyce vnto saynt andrewe agayne sayd thy prayer thy fastynge hath made nycoll lost founde agayne shall saued pnarracio palso myracle yonge man come saynt andrewe tyme sayd pryuely hym syre moder hath longe sholde lye wolde wyll hath accused bysshop sayd yt wolde haue done synfull dede wt wherfore wote well yt shall deed yet leuer deye scauder moder foule therfore beseche praye may take mydeth pacyently saluacyon soule sayd saynt andrewe go forth thy dome shall go sother people come fette hym bysshop wha moder accused hy sayd thyge helde pea thenne sayd saynt andrewe innocens sanguis eius dap nabitur cursyd woman lust body wrongfully dampne owne childe deth vengeaunce wyl come thenne sayd loo syr iustyce euer syth myght haue wyll hath drawen man counseyll socour thenne iustyce comauded caste yonge man water drowne hym put saynt andrewe pryson tyll auysed deth sholde deye thenne saynt andrewe prayed besely vnto god helpe socour thenne anone come grete thondre made people aferde yt fayne fette saynt andrewe pryson euen therwith come lyghtnyge fyre brenned ye moder ye yonge man syght people thus page missing daye waxed wood deyed amonge al people whan maximilia wyfe herde therof anone toke andrewes body buryed tombe tombe welleth manna oyle togyder people countre knowe whan sholde dere whan grete ple te whan shal plente welleth plentefully wha shall derthe scarcely pnarracio pit fell soo bysshop loued well saynt andrew fende myght wyfe brynge hym purpose came bysshop lykenes fayre woman prayenge hym myght speke hym counceyle confessyon graunted ther syrshe sayd knyghtes doughter haue moche cherysshed nourysshed grete tendernes se worlde vanyte trust vpon haue auowed chastyte fader wolde mary worthy prynce wolde breke vowe come pryuely away poore araye thus herde grete holynes come haue counceyle socoure helpe wherfore praye ordeyne ye fende haue power let purpose thenne bysshop conforted badde sholde thanke god set suche purpose wolde sende grace therwith contynue sayd esto secura filia thou seker doughter day thou shalt dyne thenne shal good aduyse whan haue dyned deyne ye shal ryght well nay syr sayd leest people wolde haue ony suspeccyon bad rule ye sayd bysshop therof charge plurimi erunus et non solo shall many company shall suspeccion thenne thanked hym fayre set fore bysshop chayre mete euer whan ye bysshop loked semed fayre gretely tempted almoost forgete hym self thenne anone came pylgryme gate bete faste gate within hall sore astonyed noyse cryed lete lete thenne sayd bysshop shall man come thenne sayd lete hym answere questyon fyrst yf worthy come nygh presence thenne sayd bysshop pray make questyon auysed tyme thenne sayd vnto messenger interroga quod est magus miraculu qd deus vn quam paruare fecit aske hym ye gretest myracle euer god made fote erth thenne whan pylgryme asked answered sayd mannes face whiche fote mannes owne face though men woman euer borne stode afore yet sholde knowe one degre whan gaue answere gretely commended therfore sayd se yt wyse bydde hym gyue answere questyon aske hym whyder erth hygher heuen thenne answered sayd thus crystes body erthe crystes body kynde kynde erthe therfore crystes body erthe hygher heuen gyuen ye answere well alowed boden come nay sayd let hym assoyle ye thyrde questyon aske hym ferre frome heuen hell thenne whan opposed answered messenger go agayne sytteth chayre bysshop byd gyue answere better tell quando de celo abissum cecidit fende helle hathe metten dyde neuer fell heuen pryde presumpcyon lucyfer whan messeger herde heuy gaf answer al men myght thene fede vanysshed awaye horryble stynke thenne ye bysshop bethought hym temptacyon sory herte anone made sende pylgrym yt messenger came ayen yate gone bysshop made men praye god sende wetynge pylgrym goodly nycolas came themperour laye bedde sayd thus hy hast ye wrongfully dapned thyse knyghtes deth aryse vp anone delyuer pryson el wyl praye god reyse batayll vp ye ye whiche thou shalt deye wylde bestes shall ete ye thene sayd themperour hy art thou ye soo boldely spekest thretest thene sayd nycolas ye bysshop myrre thene theperour anone sent ye knightes sayd wytchecraft ye yt thus hath trauayled nyght knowe ye ony man yt hyght nycolas bysshop myrre thene soone herde name felle downe ye groude helde vp theyr hondes thankyge god sayt nycolas whan tolde themperour lyf holy ye emperour bade go hym thake hy lyues dyde prayed ye knyghtes praye nycolas threten hy nomore praye god hy reame dyde thus ye may see yt hath grete copassyon yt dysease thene whan sayt nycolas sholde deye prayed god sende hym aungell fetche soule whan sawe aungell come saynt nycholas louted sayd manus tuas dne comendo spiritu meu redemisti domine deus veritatis soo yelded vp goost whan buryed heed tombe sprange welle oyle dyde medycyns al sore thenne happened many yeres turkes dystroyed ye cyte myrre saynt nycolas laye whan people cyte barus herde yt ye cyte myrre destroyed xlvii knyghtes ordeyned go thyder thenne arayed shyppes wente thyder tellynge foure monkes lefte knewe saynt nycholas tombe vndyde anone founde saynt nycholas bone swymmynge oyle thene toke vp brought cyte bar grete solempnyte thenne grete myracles yt done cyte myrre encreased agayne pand soo saynt nycholas deed chose bysshop stede anone enuyte people put downe frome bysshopryche thenne anone oyle ceased ranne thenne ye bysshop called agayne cyte thenne oyle sprange agayne dyde tofore dyde many myracles pnarracio pthere crysten man borowed certayne somme money iewe iewe sayd wolde lene none yf borowe crysten man sayd none saynt nycolas grauted take saynt nycholas borowe ye crysten man swore awter wolde pay well truely money agayne departed went theyr way tyll day payment came whan daye passed iewe asked money ye crysten man sayd yt payed hy iewe sayd nay sayd yes wolde doo lawe swere vpon boke whan daye came yt sholde go lawe crysten man made hym holow staffe put golde therin came lawe sholde swere went ye boke toke iew staffe golde holde meane swore payed iewe whan sworne toke staffe iewe agayne wente homewardes went waye passynge slepy layde hym downe hye way thene happed came carte rennynge went ouer man slewe hym brake staffe golde ye golde fell people sawe came grete vengeaunce falshode doone fette iewe badde hym take vp money thene iewe sory sayd wolde yf wolde pray saynt nycholas reyse hym agayne wolde crystened reuelauit defuctis defunctu deed man reysed frome dethe lyfe prayer saynt nycholas baptisatus aut iude viso miraculo thenne iewe yt beleue syght myracle crystened narracio palso
