good whan iewe came home agayne sawe good gone wrothe wt saynt nycholas toke staffe bete ymage sayd ecce oia bona mea posui vram custodia lo quod toke good kepynge grete truste stolen awaye ye haue deceyued therfore thou shalte abye euery daye tyll haue good agayne thenne theues departed good saynt nycholas came sayd cur tam indirecte fecistis flagellare haue ye made beten thus sore thenne sayd quis e tu arte thou speketh thus v thenne sayd ego sum nicholaus seruus dei nycholas seruaunt god yt ye haue made thus sore beten shewed sore beten good borne awaye yt taken hym kepe bad goo bere good agayne anone elles goddes vengeaunce shall fall ye shal hanged hell euerychone sore aferde bare agayne ye good nyght morowe whan iewe came sawe good brought agayne anone crystened holy man euery yere saynt nycholas day grete loue saynt nycholas also sone clerke made grete feest saynt nycholas day thenne happened tyme vpon saynt nycholas day badde many clerkes feest thenne came fende gate lykenes pylgryme asked good goddes sake thene good man made feest toke sone almesse bere pylgryme chylde went gate thenne pylgryme gone chylde folowed fende whan good way frome faders place fende caught chylde slewe whan fader herde therof full sory toke chylde layde chambre cryed sorowe sayd saynte nycholas rewarde mede shall haue grete worshyppe anone ye chylde rose dethe lyfe man ful glad thanked god saynt nycholas pnarracio pan myracle man yt prayed god saynt nycholas yt myghte haue chylde yf chylde wolde lede chyrche saynt nycolas wolde offre cuppe golde soone chylde whan chylde reasonable aege fader lete make cuppe golde whan made lyked hym well lete make thenne wente towarde saynt nycholas must passe ouer see whan see fader badde sone take vp water wt cuppe chylde wolde haue taken water cuppe fell oute hande see thenne chylde wolde haue caught cuppe agayne fell see ye chylde drowned see thenne fader made moche sorowe yet went forthe ye cuppe pylgrymage whan came saynt nycholas chyrche offred vp cuppe set auter anone caste frome awter set agayne cast ferder yet thyrde tyme set agayne thenne cast moche ferder thenne came chylde cuppe hande sayd people yt saynt nycholas toke hym vp honde whan felle see ledde hy safe thenne fader gladde offred vp bothe cuppes went home agayne ioye myrthe pnarracio pthere ryche man ye prayer saynt nycholas hadde chylde made fayre chapell ye worshyppe god saynt nycholas soo happened daye chylde taken enmyes ledde straunge countree seruyce kynges courte happened saynt nycolas daye bethought hym grete myrthe solempnyte made daye faders chapell home heuy syghed wonder sore thenne ye kynge herde therof sayd hym nycholas menest thou syghe sore mery thou must nedes abyde wt v anone came grete wynde smote ye hous braste chylde caught vp cuppe bare hande set gate chapell fader made feest thenne made grete ioye myrthe myracle lo thus ye may se grete compassyon saynt nycholas myschefe dysease bokes saye chylde normandy taken soudan beyonde see often beten one whan beten saynt nycholas daye put pryson thenne wept sore fell slepe wha awoke ye chirche fader pde concepcione beate marie virginis good men wome suche day ye shall haue ye concepcyon lady yt whiche daye feest moder holy chyrche maketh mynde mencyon ye concepcyon blyssed lady forthre specyall cause fyrste faders holynesse seconde moders goodnes thyrd mekenes fader called ioachym soo holy man whan fyftene yere aege departed goodes thre partyes one party deled wydowes faderles chyldren seconde partye gaue poore nedy thyrde parte kepte hym selfe housholde whan xxxii yere aege grete goodnes anne wedded whan wedded togyder xxii yere whiche tyme anne neuer dyspleased hym wt maner thynge neyther nyght daye soo gentyll hym bothe good holy yet god sent noo fruyte theyr bodyes baraynes wherfore made vowe god yf wolde sende chylde wolde offre vp hym temple serue god bothe daye nyght thenne day ioachym went neyghboures temple offringes bysshop hyght ysachar rebuked hym openly people sayd ioachym falleth barayne hast fruyte doo frynges people god hath sent fruyte iherusalem thenne ioachym sore dysmayed astonyed rebuke thenne went home wepinge toke shepeherde pryuely shepe went forth ferre countre amonge mountaynes hylles purposed haue lyfe neuermore come home anne wyfe thenne whan ioachym gone anne ryght sorye prayed vnto god sayd lorde woo dolefull barayne may haue noo fruyte ouer husbande gone awaye frome knowe whyder gone lorde haue mercy poore desolate creature prayed thus angell came downe comforted sayd anne good comforte thou shalt haue childe thy olde age ther neuer none lyke ne neuer shall thenne anne aferde angel wordes syght hy laye alwaye prayer deed went ye angell ioachym sayd thyse wordes badde ioachym take lambe offre sacrefyce god dyde whan hadde done myddaye tyll euensonge tyme lay grounde prayer thankynge god herte morow thangel badde wente homewarde anne wyf sheep whan came nye home angel came anne badde go gate yt called ye golden gate abyde husbonde tyl came thene gladde toke maydens wente gate mette ioachym sayd lorde thanke wydowe wyf barayne shall bere childe woo wepynge shall ioye lykynge soone anne coceyued lady whan born called maria ye angell badde yt wened brought temple lefte amonge virgynes serue god nyght daye thene meke amonge virgines lyuynge yt virgynes called quene virgynes soo mekest sayntes heuen moost redyest helpe calle ony nede pnarracio pwe rede holy wrytte myracle lady ther lordes man gadred moche good lordes rente gaderer went bere lord theues sette hym robbe hym waye wood must nedes go soo whan came woode bethought hym hadde sayd ladyes sawter wonte doo kneled downe began saye thenne came lady lyke fayre mayden set garlonde heed eche aue set rose garlande bryyt wood shone therof whan done kyssed erthe went way thenne came theues toke hym ledde hym theyr mayster whiche seen al doynges thenne sayd woma sette garlande thy heed sayd syr forsothe sawe woman garlonde thenne sayd mayster thefe wote well thou arte lordes man haste moche good wolde fayne wyte woman came thou kneled doune sayd whan sawe aferde also bethought sayd ladyes psalter kneled downe say prayenge oure lady helpe nede thenne sayd loue goo thy waye praye v went way sauf sounde helpe socoure lady pbut ye shall feest fyrste founden kynge englonde hight wyllyam conqueroure sent abbot ramsey kynge denmarke message whan came see came tempest derkenes hym wende haue drowned euery man prayed besyly vnto god lady socoure helpe dyuers sayntes abbot prayed vnto lorde ihesu cryste holy vyrgyn saynt mary full deuoutly thenne came vnto hym fayre woman sayd vnto theym yf ye wyll haue concepcyon lady worshyp honoure two dayes saynt nycholas daye wyll redy thelpe socoure tyme thenne abbot sayd ye good wyll wyste sholde seruyce feest thenne sayd natyuyte saufe torne natyuyte concepcyon abbot sayd sholde done wt full good wyll thenne anone tempest ceased wel sayled forthe thabbot dyde message came agayne sauf sounde sped well euery degree whan came home tolde ye kynge vysyon ky ge made hym preche realme thus halowed holy chyrche pnarracio palso fynde seculer chanon tyme went ouer water auoutry woman begynne saye oure ladyes matyns inuytatorye aue maria ther wt fende keste hym downe drowned hym wolde haue hym helle thenne came lady sayd haste thou taken man fende sayd fynde hy seruyce goynge auoutrye thenne sayd lady seruyce anone restored hym lyfe agayne badde hym synne badde hym halowe concepcyon dyde good man euer lyfe pnarracio palso clerke euery daye vsed saye seruyce blyssed lady thenne happed counceyle frendes sholde take wyfe whan sholde wedded bethought hym hadde sayde ladyes seruyce thenne made al people go chyrche whyles sayd seruyce thenne kneled downe sayd seruyce tyll came antem lady quam pulchra e amica mea thene lady appered vnto hym sayd sayest thou fayre honest wyll thou leue take thenne sayd lady wyll thou shall thenne sayd lady yf thou wylt leue thy flesshely wyfe serue sone shall thy spouse thou shalte haue crowne euerlastynge lyfe kyngedome perdurable blysse whiche god blyssed moder saynt mary holy sayntes heuen brynge v thyder amen pde sancto thoma dere frendes day ye shal haue saynt thomas daye crystes appostle ye shall fast euen hym worshypp specyally thre cause fyrst preuynge beleue grete wonder way grete myracles dayes holy appostle preued fayth left trouble whan dysciples sayd lorde rysen frome dethe lyfe seen hym spoke hym thomas sayd wolde beleue tyll put hande syde wounde spere made thenne viii dayes whan dyscyples togyder thomas thene lorde ihesu cryste came bodely sayd pax vobis pea wt sorde sayd thomas ynde mitte manu tuam latus meu put thy hande syde wounde made spere yt smote herte et noli esse incredulus lenger beleue stedfast faythe whan thomas done anone sayd grete woder dns de lorde god beleue yt yu art god man thenne lorde sayd hym beati qui crediderunt et viderunt blessyd byleue see thou hast seen thou byleuest yet tarye ge thomas brought v sadder byleue blessynge lorde ihesu cryste speketh saynt gregory sayth thomas ynde thou hast holpen fayth woldest byleue tyll thou hade feled woundes thenne dyde mary mawdeleyne dyde byleue ye fyrste syght minus est enim maria magdalena que cici credidit quam thomas qui diu dubitauit thus thomas preued fayth byleue nede neuer varye doubte also thomas dyde many marueylles grete woundres yt dayes pnarracio pit happed kyng ynde sende messenger albanus indie requirens artificem seke crafty men countree cezar seke carpenter ye coude make hym palays plesauce thenne lorde ihesu cryste mette albanus sent wiht hym holy saynt thomas grete ynde whan thomas albanus passed see come cyte kynges doughter wedded daye wherfore maner people comauded mete amonge peple thomas albanus came sette mete thomas ete thought euer god lust ete thenne came botteler thomas smote thomas cheke badde hym ete thenne sayd thomas hym non hinc surgam donec manus que percussit camb aufertur shall ryse place tyll honde smote brought dogge thenne anone boteler went water lyon mete hym slewe hym dranke blood ete body thenne came blacke dogge caught honde yt smote thomas brought halle syght people layde downe thomas woma vnderstode thomas wordes anone kneled downe thomas cryed sayd thou art god el one dyscyples ryght yu wylt thene kyng prayed thomas blesse doughter husbonde thomas glade ther cepit erge predicare beatus thomas therfore blessyd thomas began preche tolde lorde ihesu cryst yt torned man wedded ye daye fro wyf made hym bysshop cyte wyf nonne martyr crystys sake thenne went thomas forth ynde kyng make hy palays plesaunce whan thomas come kyng glade delyuered thomas grete golde make palays thenne rode ye kyng forth meane tyme wha thomas sholde haue made palays hym thought better make palays heuen erthe deled golde amonge poore people conuerted fayth thene came kyng home wende palays hade redy whan herde thomas albanus hade done wolde haue put theym deth happed owne broder deed tyme therfor put pryson vnto tyme yt hade buryed broder god wolde whan broder laye longe deed rose deth lyf tolde kyng seen palays paradyse thomas made hym prayed kyng myght haue wolde gyue hy moche golde toke thomas thenne kyng toke counseyll sayd nay wyll haue lete hym make brother seen palays paradyse made golde arrayed precyous stone clothe golde thenne kyng toke crystendome many thousande hym whan bysshops sawe kyng moche peple forsoke herlawes torned crystendome werefore wrothe thomas thenne one sayd wolde venge god spere smote thomas thrugh body slewe hym thenne crysten peple buryed hym tombe crystall god wrought many myracles hym honde crystys syde wolde neuer come tombe euer laye also prechynge techynge taught duodecum grad virtutum assignare pprimus est vt deum crederent qui est vnus essencia et trinus personis dedit eis triplex exemplum sensibile quomodo tres persone sint vna essentia pprimum quia vna est homine sapiencia et de vna procedit intellectus memoria et ingenium memoria est vt obliuiscaris intellectum vt intelligas que ostendi possunt vel doceri ingenium est vt quod didiceris inuenias psecundum exemplum est quia vna vinea tria sunt lignum folium et fructus et hec omma tria sunt vna vinea ptercium exemplum est quia caput nostrum ex quatuor sensibus constat vno autem capite sunt visus auditus gustus et odoratus et hee plura sunt et tamen vnum caput psecundus gradus est vt baptismum suscipiat ptercius gradus est vt fornicatione abstineat pquartus vt se ab auaricia temperet pquintus vt gulam distingeret psextus vt penitenciam teneret pseptimus vt perseueraret octau vt hospitalitate amaret pnonus vt voluntatem dei requirat pdecimus est vt facienda quereret pvndecimus vt caritatem amicis et inimicis impen deret duodecim est vt custodiat hec vigile cura exhiberet pitem appostolus omnes qui oderant deum de tribus breuiter instruxit faciendis scilicet de ecclesiam diligerent sacerdotes honorarent et assidue ad verbum dei conuenirent palso ben many meruaylous wonderfull thynges done daye daye countre cometh thyde take pardon honde lyeth tombe theyr vse bysshop cyte gooth masse whan hath sayd confiteor thenne taketh braunche vyne putteth thomas honde tombe thene gooth forth masse braunche burgeneth grape tyme gospell sayd grape ben rype thenne bysshop taketh grape wryngeth wyne ye chalyce syngeth wyne houseled ye people whan ony man woman cometh worthy receyue housell anone honde closeth togyder wyll open tyll shryuen thenne wyl ope also yf ony peple debate shal brought thomas tombe cause shall rehersed thenne wyll honde torne hym ryght made one thus thomas preued byleue dyde many wodres dayes also iohan grysostomus sayth thomas came countree thre kynges coleyne thomas crystened worshypped god byrthe therfore thomas came taught fayth byleue cryste byleue may saued god brynge v amen pde natiuitate domini nostri ihesu christi frendes ye se holy chyrche maketh mynde mencyon ye grete myrth melody blyssed byrth lorde ihesu cryste veray god man yt day borne moder mary socoure mankynde especyall thre cause fyrst gyue pea man good wyll lyght derke syne drawe v loue hym thenne ye fyrst cause borne gyue men pea good wyll may well preue whan borne angel songe thus gloria excelsis deo ioye god heuen pea erth mankynde good wyll mydnyght lorde borne kynde thynge pea rest shewynge princeps pacis prynce pea come make pea bytwene god man bytwene aungell man bytwene man man true medyatour betwene god man toke nature kynde bothe bothe veray god man medyacyon knytte loue god man soo sadly yt fader heue spared hym owne sone sent hym doune worlde bye mankynde wt precyous blode grete mekenes ioye paradyse man hadde loste couetyse vnbuxsomnesse thus made pea bytwene god man man man whan aungelles sawe theyr mayster wrothe man vnbuxsomnes synne aungelles dooth hate gretely therfore kept gate paradyse wolde lette soule come paradyse tyl sawe theyr lorde souerayne borne mankynde take flesshe blyssed vyrgyn mary mooste beloued moder thenne anone loue lorde angel dyde manky de worshyp spake goodly mankynde shepeherdes kept sheep countree badde theym go cyte bethleem sholde fynde childe borne layde cratche badde hym worshyp dyden euer syn angel haue ben frendly man lowly haue done reuerence mankyde thyncarnacyon lorde ihesu cryst th made pea bytwene angel man also made pea bytwene man man ayenst tyme yt lorde wolde born made grete pea yt worlde kyngdomes countrees debate warred eche vnto ye tyme lordes byrth ther grete pea man yt called octauyan emperour rome ye gouernauce worlde worlde subget rome dured xxx yere moche yt ther maundement sente rome ye worlde comaundynge maner people sholde go cyte drewe lygnage laye peny vpon heed offre vp know lechynge subget themperour rome must ioseph ladyes husbonde nedes go ye cyte bethleem offre peple moneye offre toke oxe wt hym selle cyte make moneye dute durst leue lady behyde hym nye tyme therfor set vpon asse tooke hym whan came cyte bethleem full peple ioseph lady myght haue lodgynge torned cabon made betwix two house people ye cou tree sette theyr horse theyr ass bestes wha come towne market fou de cratche heye sette oxe asse therto taryed nyght whan lytell mydnyght lady badde ioseph goo towne loke mydwyf tyme come sholde delyuered soo whyle ioseph towne mydwyf lady delyuered lapped sone clothes layde cratche oxe thasse anone knewe lorde fyll downe knee worshypped hym ete heye thenne anone came ioseph two mydwyues zebell salome zebell founde lady clene mayden cryed sayd virgo peperit filium mayde hath born childe thenne salome wolde byleue anone went lady boustously handled lady probare vellet wolde preue euen ther hondes dryed vp thenne came angell badde sholde go touche ye childe dyde anone hole thenne wente ioseph dyde offrynge people kept lady cabon whyle childe bedde thus ye may vnderstade cryst gyueth pea people good wyll called hem childern verefyenge fyrste masse ge yt daye holy chyrche songe soone mydnyghte begynneth thus dominus dixit ad filius meus e tu ego hodie genui te lorde sayth yu art sone lorde called hym sone childe loued hy rest pea whan departeth worlde wyll brynge hym euer lastynge rest pea wyll haue rest pea shall go euerlastynge payne neuer rest pea neuer shal euerlastynge woo thus gyueth pea men good wyl lyghtneth lyketh hym good men ye shall vnderstande cryste heled oonly theym blynde soule combred derkenesse synful lyuynge saynt austyn sayth whan lorde sholde borne worlde full derkenesse specyally synne lechery synne ayenst kynde moche almoost left haue borne mankynde wherfore al dyden synne ayenst kyde tyme deyed sodenly thrugh worlde shewynge horryble abhomynable synne syght almyghty god thenne loked full derke synne theyr thoughtes alwaye synne euyll lyuynge hadde full grete nede lyghtned wherfor cryst borne mydnyght tourned derkenesse nyght daye lyght lyghtened theym euer couered combred derkenesse synne palso tyme lorde borne many doctours sayen cryst appered bryght sterre kynges thest badde go bethleem worshyp lytell childe sholde kyng iewes borne dyde euer sterre shewynge theym tyll came thyder thus lyghtened theym full derke synne kynges paynems bileued mawmetry fals goddes byleued cryste holy lyuers coleyne pthus byrth lorde ihesu cryst made many man loke full bryght tofore ful derke synne full derke soule euer setteth herte mynde thought prosperyte worshyp welfare worlde maketh inwardly blynde soo ignoraunt haue felynge grete inestimable grace ghostly syght ben made blynde abused transytory rychesse wycked worlde couetyse therof commytte vsury gete theyr good haue desyre rychesse heuen ne se lyght suche thynges mannes herte moost maketh god dystroye suche mawmetry synne lorde borne thenne kynge herode pursued lorde wolde haue slayne hym thenne moder bare hym egypte aungell badde ioseph sayd accipe puerum et matre eius fuge egiptum take chylde moder flee egypte soone came thyder mawmettes londe fell doune grounde doynge vnderstande come worlde sholde cast downe mawmetry maner syne euyll lyuynge pryde couetyse maner falshede vsed dayes therfore take hede lorde made maner thynge nought lorde lordes borne poore place poore araye poore mayden gyuynge ensample crysten people set nought ye worshyp rychesse vanyte worlde haue man neuer grete worshyp neuer moche rychesse yet leueth shall bere hym good dedes thus lorde shewed many thynges byrthe lyghtned many one full blynde tokenynge herof seconde masse daye sayd dawnynge whan nyght daye departeth whiche begynneth thus lux fulgebit hodie thus moche saye lyghte shall shyne daye vpon v fader heuen sedeth grace goostly lyght crysten people beleue truly lorde borne god man moder mary moder mayden thus beleue truely lorde ihesu cryste moder mary set full lytell vanytees worlde put al theyr hope truste ihesu cryste thus byrthe lorde ihesu cryst lyghtned many one loked full yll also drew v hym loue chyldren drawe maketh moche playe thus lorde ihesu cryste borne chylde fayrest euer borne drawe mannes loue hym whyle chylde yonge without synne amyable louynge thenne mannes aege paste innocencye doynge sythen loue onely beaute clennes soule also goodnes eche man bounde drawe hym hym worshyppe octauyan dyde themperour rome pleased moche people empyre rome yt wolde haue worshypped hym theyr god ye emperoure wyse wyst wel man durst take vpon hym none sent sybyll sage asked whether sholde ony borne hym sholde greter thenne myddaye sybyll loked sonne sawe cercle golde sonne et medio circuli virgo pulcherrima cum puero myddes cercle mayden chylde arme crowne golde whan sybyll shewed themperoure sayd hym chylde shall greter yu arte euer euer shall therfore hym worshyp reuerence thenne anone emperour toke ence se dyde worshyp hym charged people call chylde theyr god hym man thus crysten people may lerne worshyppe seruyce chylde day therfore thyrde masse daye sayd myddaye tokenynge crysten people sholde come offre worshyppe chylde moder shewe seruau te subgecte vnto hym knowelege gloryous chylde lorde god eche man sholde come hym drede therfore offyce ye masse daye begynneth thus puer natus est nobis chylde borne v sayth man al crysten people sholde bolde aferde come vnto hym haue grace full grace redy gyue mercy aske mekely due reuerence euer redy gyue mercy grace tokenyge day cryste borne bedleem well water torned ranne oyle daye shewynge welle grace mercy borne daye yt sholde gyue mercy grace wolde come hym aske mercy grace ye shall ensample pnarracio pwe rede woman defouled lechery almoost fell dyspayre drede bethought streytnesse crystes dome grete horryble paynes hell ordeyned suche synners sore aferde bethought herof crystes passyon loue shewed crysten people thought vnkynde hym suffred sore thene bethought chyldren neuer wrothe shewe neuer grete vengeauce lyghtly wyll cease forgyue wherfore woman cryed cryst praye ge hym chyldehode haue mercy anone herde voyce hye ayre sayd thy trespace forgyuen psermo breuis de sancto stephano good men woman suche daye ye shall haue hye daye holy feest moder holy chyrch prothomartyr saynt steuen whiche suffred deth goddes sake crystes ascencyon thenne stere deuocyon holy martyr wyll tell somwhat suffred crystes sake boke appostles telleth post ascencionem domini ascencyon lorde styed vp heuen appostles laboure preche teche worde god crysten people fewe serue people came came many torne faythe therfore chose vi holy men good lyuers helpe goddes seruyce whiche saynt steuen one theym fyrst wysest full grace myght holy goost dyde many myracles meruaylous amonge people though man neuer holy yet shall haue ennemyes wherfore dyuers countrees enmyte saynt steuen came agaynst hym dysputed hym haue ouercome hy dysputacyon myght brought false wytnes agaynst hym put hym dethe whan saynt stephen sawe knewe theyr malyce anone thought cease theym one iii wayes shamynge dysputacyon drede reuelacyon prayer holy oraysons fyrste sayd shamynge dysputacyon whan began dyspute hym soo full holy goost power ne myght gaynsaye hym ouer came theyr mater preued al theyr mater false sayd agaynste therfore sayd redy suffre dethe verefyenge susteynynge sayd put grete clerkes knewe lawe prophecye vnto grete shame velonye yet wolde beleue alway agaynstode hym full holy ghoost preued sayd grete reason trouthe yet wolde byleue holy ghost spake hym yet yt wolde byleue theyr coscyence yt dyde amysse sawe comynte tourne fayth wordes myracles god shewed syght yet ayenstode hy sette goddes myracles noughthy malyce enmyte cursyd hertes none reaso scrypture freted hertes hymself grutched teeth angre thought myght ouercome hy dysputacyon thenne sought yf myght haue taken hym worde crystys deth myght haue made theym cause haue put hym deth thenne saynt stephen knewe malyce lyft vp eyen vnto heuen et vidit celos apertos sawe heuen open lorde ihesu cryst syttynge faders ryght honde redy helpe hym face shone bryght angell heuen whan herde hy speke thenne fayne stoppe theyr eres though herde hym speke fals sclaunderynge god anone drewe hym cyte stone hym deth dyssclaunderer thenne toke two yonge men coude best cast stone toke clothes layde foot yonge man hyght saule saynt poule thenne whan saynt stephen sawe myght cesse theyr malyce reuelacyon shewynge tourned deuoute orysons called neweyeres daye saynt augustyn sayth day nyght hethen people vse many false opynyons wytchecraftes false beleue whiche tell amonge crysten people lest torne ye vse wherfore ye crysten people well ware lest ye deceyued ony false sorcerye takynge counceyle man afore byege sellynge lenyng ye whiche haue dyuers opynyones yf well shryuen worthy haue grete penauce theyr mysbeleue cometh ye fende god daye called cyrcumcysyon oure lorde holy chyrche telleth daye cyrcumcysed bled blode sake whan flesshe cut bled fast full sore yonge tender viii dayes olde therfore bled ye shall wete yt bled fyue tymes v quin que em vicib saguine suum nobis effudit fyrst sheddyge daye whan cyrcumcysed fere passyon ryght chylde wepeth fere whan seeth ye rod hath harme soo ye flesshe lorde swete blode drede stroge passyon yt comyge ye iii tyme flagellacyon whan beten wt scourge body ranne reed bloode iiii tyme whan nayled hade fete crosse fyfth tyme whan longyus perysshed herte spere water blode came woundes thenne toke vp crosse body lyfte vpon hye sodaynly lete crosse fall downe ye mortayse synewes vaynes ioyntes brake blode water came euery woude suffred v thenne syth cryst cyrcumcysed shed blode thus v without synne cyrcumsysyon synne remedy helpe wolde cyrcu cysed neuer dyde synne sctus augustin dicit propt quattuor causa saynt austyn sayth four cause fyrst make seeth iewes elles wolde myght haue sayd ben theyr lawe wherfore wolde receyue hym consent techynge deceyue ye fende ryght fende deceyued adam eue mankynde dampned soo fel cryste deceyue fende wherethrugh mankynde myght saued thenne wha fende sawe cyrcumcysed chylde wende taken penaunce remedy orygynall ne knewe hym fro chylde yf knowen hym verely come haue bought mankynde wolde neuer haue tysed iewes haue put hym dethe seconde cause lady wedded ioseph deceyue fende ye fende sholde wene ioseph fader co ceyued holy goost thyrde cause cyrcumcysed yt confermynge olde lawe grete co forte olde faders olde testament yf crystened cyrcucysed ben grete dyscomforte yt thyncarnacyon cryst iiii cause cyrcumcysyon lorde wyst well yt wolde come heretykes yt wolde haue sayd yt cryst body erthly fantasy flesshe blode one v haue body ayre may blede therfore put away suche erroures cryste cyrcucysed bled cuttynge flesshe whiche flesshe cut frome membre angell brought kynge charles moost precyous relyke worlde gretest worshyppe yt coude therto brought rome chyrch yt called scta scto rum foure cause cryst cyrcucysed day also called vtas natyuyte yt ye viii day lordes byrthe grete kenynge v yt goddes seruau te thynke viii dayes foloweth byrthe fyrst day thyke inwardly sede yt co ceyued foule abhomynable selfe man woman neuer fayre sawe ye mater wolde ashamed themselfe thynke euer conceyued yt foule thynge ii daye thyke greuously payneth moder byrth moche grete myracle god yt may haue lyfe iiii daye thynke feble wretched borne beestes kynde somwhat helpe themselfe saue onely mankynde neyther may ne helpe hymselfe degre deye anone yf haue helpe socoure iiii daye thynke moche peryl drede lyueth therfore euery place dethe foloweth hym euery daye redy fall hy tyme ne man knoweth onely god hym selfe incert est locus quo mors te repectat vncertayne dethe abydeth v day thynke horryble dethe whan cometh shorte space tyme maketh man stynke soo best fredes yt hathe erthe hyde vi daye thynke sorowfull departynge body soule yt may departed tyll hert body breke drede syghtes soule shall see grete fere herte breketh mors quam amara est memoria tui thou deth bytter thynke vpon ye wha yu art comynge ony man vii daye thynke dredful dome yt shall go anone streyght iugement shall thenne yt wyll thynke thyse viii dayes hope shall circucysed yt shal cut awaye lust flesshe synne dete worldes lykynge thus cometh viii daye yt vtas cryst yt ioye blysse yt neuer shall haue ende whiche god brynge v amen pin die epyphanie good frendes daye called xii daye xiii daye crystis byrth whiche daye holy chirche called epyphania dni saye ye shewynge lorde ihu cryst god man daye shewed god man thre frynges crystenyge also tornynge ye water wyne xiii daye byrth offrynge thre kynges daye xxx wynter xiii dayes byrth crystned water flom iordan daye xii moneth torned water wy weddynge cana galylee fest maketh mouit mynde mencyon thre kynges offrege therfore lete v folowen fourme holy chirche ye shall felle offryge lorde ihesu cryst god man thyse thre kynges lygnage yt prophecyed sterre sholde shyue iacob noo iewes kynde herde phecye wherfore grete desyre lust see oftentymes wha myght came togyder vpo certayne hyghe hylles thenne wolde dyspute amonge sterre happed vpon crystmasse nyght tyme lord borne togyder dysputynge sterre super montem vpon hylle dus enim erat natus lorde born et apparuit illis appyered sterre fayre childe vnder heed bryght crosse golde sayd thus go ye anone hast ye ye may ye londe iury take golde myrre ensence offre thyse thre thynges hym ye shall fynde borne kyng iewes god man shall gyde lede waye thenne anone grete hast toke bestes ben called dromedaryes ben suche ky de soo swyfte yt wyll renne ferder one daye ony best wyll renne goo thre dayes came iherusalem chyef cyte iury hopynge sholde tydynges childe borne soone torned ye cyte ihrlm lost ye syght ye sterre ladde euer ye waye tyll yt came thyder bryghter ye sone whan came ye cyte iherusale tode kyng herode tyme sayd hym vbi est qui natus est rex iudeorum borne kyng iewes vidimus enim stella eius oriente sawe sterre east venimus adorare eum become worshyp hym thenne kyng herode troubled cyte hym flaterynge hym thenne ony loue hadde hym thenne kyng hetode asked clerkis childe sholde born sayd bethleem iude thenne kyng herode asked kynges pryuely sterre badde go bethleem worshyp chylde come ayen hym telle hym myght fynde childe myght go worshyp hym thenne thre kynges coleyne passed frome kynge herode goyge towarde bethleem anone ye sterre appyered theym whan sawe sterre come ayen glad theyr hertes many place paynted kyng myddell grete ioye sterre loked bacwarde felowe behynde hym fynger shewed hym sterre yt cause myddel kyng loked bacwarde th sterre brought theym bethleem whan sterre came ouer hous lorde stode stylle thenne kynges lyghred downe wente n hous reuerence coude elynge downe offred eche theym thyse thre thynges aurum thus et myrram golde ensence myrre knowlechynge golde kyng kynges ensence god myrre man sholde deed layde graue without rottynge golde chyef metalles ensence brente holy chirche worshyp god myrre oynement kepeth bodyes rotrynge thus whan kynges done theyr offrynge techynge angell per aliam viam reuersi sunt regionem suam waye wente towarde theyr owne londes left kyng herode sterre vanysshed awaye saynt bernarde sayeth ioseph kepte golde moche hy neded trybute sholde paye emperour also kepe lady whyle lay childe bedde remenaunt deled poore people suche grete nede therto encence brente put awaye stenche stable laye myrre lady anoynted childe kepe hym wormes dysease befel kynges fynde thynge certayne people haue opynyon saynt thomas ynde crystened theym whan came countree ynde thenne sterre lyghtned theym crystys byrth holy ghost lyghtned theym theyr soules taught theym parfyght waye byleue also parfyght gracyous lyuynge moche lefte theyr kyngdome wente forth pylgremage saye iherusalem many place came forth myllayne deyed thre translated coleyne yet haue ye herde thyse thre kynges lorde ihesu cryst daye shewed god man wherfore lyke offred deuocyon sholde ye offrynges whan ye come holy chirche knelynge downe reuerence ye may one knee temporall lorde bothe knee doo worshyp hym good prayer thenne offre ye precyous golde golde soo precyous good deuote praer thenne holde vp hondes hym reuerence ye deuoute herte praye hym shewe hym loue hertes thenne ye offre hym ensence ensence sauoureth swete gyueth encensyall odoure brennynge feyre dooth good prayer sayde brennynge loue clene charyte yf thou thus thenne thou offrest knelynge thy knee make crosse erthe kysse thynke well thou arte erthe thenne must ye offre myrre ryght myrre kepeth body rotynge mynde dethe kepeth mannes soule deedly synne wyse ye offrynge thene shall ye haue moche mede hadde thyse thre kynges also shewed bothe god man crystenynge came water flome iordane went water halowed ryght cyrcumcysed conferme ye newe lawe nede therto clene without synne make sacrament yt shold wasshe theym toke crystenyng name fro synnes thenne iohan baptyste redy moche people hym came crystnynge thenne sayd iohan lorde quakynge tremblynge blyssed lorde thou art goddes lambe without synne thou hast nede crystned man goten borne synne hath nede come crystned remyssyon al synnes thenne sayd lorde ihesu iohan suffre tyme thus must fulfyll al ryghtwysnes iohn crystned lorde ihesu cryst credyble lady crystned dyscyples cryst people comen thyder whan crystned lorde went water wente oure brynke water people hym aperti sunt celi heuen opened grete lyght beclypped hy syght people holy goost came downe lykenes whyte douue lyghte vpon oure lordes heed fader heuen spake sayd thus herynge people hic est filius meus dilect quo michi bene complacui well beloued sone whiche pleaseth teche crysten people fayth ye beleue holy chyrche crysten people bounde beleue stedfastly fader sone holy goost baptismo xpi tota trinitas se manifestauit scilic scilicet pater voce filius carne spussanctus coluba et totum celu apertum est crystes baptysme hole trynyte shewed fader spake voyce whan sayd hic est filius dilectus well beloued sone bodely whan iohan baptyst sayd ecce agnus dei holy goost seen sicut columba whyte douue ben thre persones one godheed fader spake aboue sone bodely holy goost lykenes douue ye shall beleue thre persones one god trynyte beleue ye shall knowe water bryke crystnynge ye fonte wherfore beleueth thus dooth werkes beleue shall saued qui crediderit et baptisat fuerit salu erit beleueth baptysed shall saued foloweth werkes beleue qui vero crediderit condep nabitur belyueth dooth werkes beleue shall dampned werkes beleue ben mekenes charyte without two man may saued hath two wryten genelogy lorde ihesu cryst whiche redde crystmas begynneth aboue abraham cometh downewardes ioseph oure lady shewynge yt moost mekest herte moost next lorde iesu cryst suche auauceth euerlastynge blysse therfore genelogy nyght begynneth ihesu cryst gooth vpwardes abraham soo god also shewed verey god trynyte whan tourned water wyne weddynge happened yt people lacked wyne whyles meete thenne badde oure lorde sholde god yt torned water wyne man ete dranke wt myracle shewed weddynge tokenynge yt blysseth weddynges done lawe holy chyrche therfore kepe wedlocke full faythe beleue holy chyrche holy chyrche techeth ye shall come endles blysse amen pde conuersione sancti pauli frendes suche day ye shall haue saynt poules daye called conuersyon saynt poule daye conuerted tourned fro wycked tyraunt goddes seruaunt hye man proude meke man good man frome dyscyple ye deuyll goddes holy appostle man torned wyckednes grete goodnes grete helpe socoure holy chyrche therfore holdeth conuersyon mo hym onely thre cause fyrst grete myracles tornynge grete ioye defendynge ensample amendyge fyrst torned called saule ryght saule ye kynge ierlm pursued dauyd sle hy dyde saule pursue cryste dyscyples brynge dethe therfore whyle cryst went erth saule wolde neuer come techyge soone cryst styed heuen anone saule lerned coude iewes lawe began withstande gaynesayd crystes dyscyples dysputynge agaynst pursued myght full entent haue dystroyed crysten faythe daye dysputed saynt steuen myght ouercome hym bethought hym myght brynge hym dethe lefte hym neuer tyll deed ye maner fendes chyldren whan haue done cursed dede glad therof proude herte encrease theyr malyce saule gladde dethe saynt steuen wolde haue goten hym name wyckednesse passynge felowes went yt iewes lawes kepynge gate hym lettre warraunt take yt beleued cryst brynge iherusalem put dethe whan letter toke suche enuy ther wtin hert ayenst cryste people yt wha herde ony man speke anone grete angre wolde snese nose frooth mouthe angre grynte tethe thretenynge menacynge towarde crysten people aferde hym daye herde cyte damaske moche cristen people hyd drede rode thederwarde anone lorde ihesu crist shewed swetenes grace whan saule hye pryde wyll haue done moost harme aboute myddaye lorde keste grete lyght grace aboute hym whiche moche bryghter sonne lyght sayd vnto saule maner wyse saule saule quid per sequeris saule saule folowest thou anone aferde fell downe hors cryed sayd grete fere quis e tu dne lorde arte thou said lorde hym ego su iesus nazaren ihesus nazareth yt ye name manhode saule anone byleued hym sayd lorde wylt thou yt shall thenne sawe people hym lyght herde voys sawe noo thynge anone wente saule toke hym vp hondes bly de myght see ladde hy cyte good mannes hous thre dayes thre nyghtes fastynge nother ete dranke ne myght see euer prayed god drede vysyon whiche tyme holy ghoost taught hym crystis lawe thenne thyrde daye one crystys dyscyples hyght ananyas god badde hym came hym full sore aferde sayd saule frater dns iesus misit ad te qui apparuit tibi via saule lorde hath sete ihesus appyered waye thou sholdest see crystned whan ananyas layde honde vpon heed anone saw clerely ther felle eyen lyke scale fysshes whan hadde crystened hym called hym poule thenne ete comforted strenghte fewe dayes ye dyscyples thenne wente temple preched opely lorde ihesu cryste preuynge clerkely yt god man none stupebant enim omnes qui audiebant et dicebant forsothe herde hym astonyed sayd grete myracle grace god soden conuersyon cursyd lyuyge lytell soone torned god man thus may ye grete myracle god shewed conuersyon grete ioye holy chirche maketh defendynge grete ioye crysten people lytell besy destroye crysten peple anone redy encrease crysten peple yt besy gladde shed crysten menes blood thenne redy shede owne blood besy went put dethe thenne good wyll redy take dethe theym man durst preche worde god hym co forte hym spared lorde knyght openly preched worde god taught faythe euery place fore proude fyers soone made meke lowly fell grounde euery crysten mannes fote yt trespaced mekely besought theym mercy wt full pacyent herte wherfore saynt austyn lykeneth hym vnto vnycorne kynde bereth horne browe horne sleeth beestes fyghteth wt also fyers hymselfe may hunter take hym thus wyll begyle hym wyll espye vnycorne haunteth vseth walke wyl sette mayde soone vnycorne seeth mayde anone kynde wyll fall downe laye hede lappe thenne myght strength gone thenne come take hym thus sayth saynt poule fyrst fyers hym selfe durst preche ne speke hym drede whan lorde ihesu cryst shewed swetenes grace fayre mayde lawe holy chyrch anone poule fell downe grounde subget crysten people herfore holy chyrche gladde defendynge set also hye ensample hye amendynge lorde soo gracyous crysten people may saued wyll forsake mysse beleue conuerted multo magi gaudium erit celo super vno peccatore penitenciam agente quam super nonaginta nouem qui non digent penitentia ioye heuen vpon one synner repentaunt doynge penaunce vpon xcix dyde neuer committe synne therfore moost blyssed lorde wolde al conuerted wherfore hye ensample conforte synfull people set saynt poule loke vpon though man done neuer moche syne wolde forsake synne synne thenne company heuen maketh ioye melody conuercyon erthe conuercyon saynt poule moche people loue synne wt lust lykynge worlde loue god many neuer wyll leue synne neyther loue god ne desyre blysse heuen fere fende drede paynes hell saye ye god wyll neuer lese hath bought dere passyon say ben wyse god wyll none loste beware thou lese thy selfe whyle thou louest synne god haddest leuer serue fende god thou arte cause thyn owne dampnacyon whyle thou hast wyll serue fende chylde goddes chylde thou lesest thy selfe god hath ordeyned fendes tourmente theym euerlastynge payne saynt gregory sayeth shall dampned begynne theyr penaunce worlde party theyr dethe cotynueth euermore wherfore tell ensample narracio pthere man offycer lorde stode acursed tyme rode towarde man bounde founde man bare bone flesshe clene away thus ye may se contynuelly lyueth synne may full sure foule ende though ende semeth fayre ye syght yet ryght foule syght almyghty god al aungelles wyll offre take fro sayd nay ye messenger wolde haue take fro helde fast betwix two ye serge brake myddes halfe ye messenger thother half ye woma wrastelynge woma woke slepe half ye serge hode tha brennynbefore lady happed whan deed fedes came toke soule wha goynge came two aungels rebuked ye fendes bolde take ye soule without dome sayd ther nedeth none dyde neuer good dede tha sayd take bryng ye soule lady dyde whan founde yt dyde neuer good dede must nedes go helle sayd lady foude candell brennyge afore euer wyll whyle lyued therfore wyl kynde bad angell take grete serge lyght set helle lady charged comaunded sholde fende came nye let stonde brennyge euer comforte yt ben hell tha sayd ye fendes leuer leue soule tha badde lady take ye soule bere body agayne dyde whan lyue bethought byleue nothyge yt dyd also sholde bere wytnes asce syon dyde erth iewes wold byleue maner thynge myght preued witnesse iudas scariot one xii ye cryste chosen iudas lytell tofore slayne owne fader laye angell wyth sygne ye crosse shynyg golde sayd hym morow whan yu goste batayle take sygne thy honde vertue therof yu shalt haue victory thenne costantyne wonder glad anone lete make crosse tree bere tofore hym batayle whan maxencius sawe nye yt brygge fyers hymselfe forgete trappe whiche made came brygge fell downe ye water trappe drowned thenne oost wonder feyne yelde constantyne good wyll thenne costantyne yet cristened also heled leperhode anon couseyle pope sente moder quene eleyne quene iherusale prayed go seke ye crosse crist deyed thys eleyne kynges doughter englonde emperoure thenne sayde eleyne hym si vi viuere ostende michi lignu crucis yf thou wylt lyue shew ye crosse god deyed vpon elles thou shalt bret put greate distresse thenne sawe must nedes telle deye sayd anone body rose lyf thanked god thenne sayd iudas thou arte cryste truly sauyoure world yt iudas crystened holy man thenne toke eleyne parte crosse sent rome sone remenaut therof made shryne syluer made mynde cryste thenne toke rode sette priuy place hous syghte iewes dyde worshyppe honour connynge thenne fell man went another hous happed leue rode behynde hym vnwetynge thenne came iewe dwelled hous crysten man hadde dwelled thenne make hym good chere neyghboures came nyght souped wt hym sate souper spake crysten man dwelled iewe loked besyde hy corner sawe rode whan sawe anone began grynde wt tethe chyde iewe neyghboure sayd yu arte torned crysten fayth hast rode doost worshyp pryuely iewe sware nay depe coude ne neuer sawe ye tyme yet notwithstandynge iewe went tolde neyghboures sayd man preuy crysten man rode pryuely hous thenne anone came neyghboures woode wrathe bet man drewe hym tugged hym worste maner coude last sayd theymage yu beleuest vpon toke ymage bete scourged crowned thornes last made strengest theym take spere wt myght smyte herte anone therwith blode water ranne sydes thene sore aferde therof sayd take pottes fyl blode bere temple seke people dyuers maladyes iohannis fyre fyrst fyre greate clerke iohan belleth telleth certayne coutrey coutrey soo greate hete whiche caused dragon go togyder tokenynge yt iohan deyed brennynge loue charyte god deye charyte rad kyng alysaunder tyme sholde haue batayle ye kynge iude kynge inde broughte hym many olyphauntis berynge castellis tree theyr backes kynde haue armed knyghtes ye castell batayle ne knewe alysaundre kynge olyphauntes drad thynge iarrynge swyne wherfore made gader gyder ye swyne myghte begoten caused dryuen ny olyphauntes myghte well iarrynge swyne thenne made pygge crye whan swyne herde pygges none made grete iarrynge soone olyphauntes herde began fle eche one keste downe castelles slewe knyghtes meane alexander ye vyctory also wyse clerkes knoweth well drago hate nothynge stenche brennynge bone therfore gadered many myghte fynde brent stenche therof droue away dragon brought grete dysease pthe seconde fyre made wood yt wyll brene lyght wyl seen ferre chefe fyre seen ferre tokenynge yt iohans martyrdome bone brente ye shall pwe rede kynge herode broder yt hyght phylyp fayre woman wyfe herode loued well helde vnder wyfe wherfore iohan repreued hy sayd non licet tibi habere vxorem aungell came heuen tolde zacharye conceyuynge halowed moders wombe lady toke hym fro erthe byrthe angell brought name frome heuen crystned lorde ihesu cryste holy man ye shall vnderstande saynt iohan theuangelyst deyed daye holy chyrche maketh mencyo therof day holden crystmas weke thenne two iohans holden worthyest sayntes heue thenne two scolers dyuynyte one loued iohan baptyst iohan euangelyst gretter heue soo one sayde ye one gretter ye soo began fyghte thene came voyce fro heuen sayde fyghte heuen therfore fyght ye erth v ben pea soo ye therwith booth hole theyr sykenesse thanked god sayt shewyge maner crysten peple yt suffred woundes v fyue welles mercy yt suffred v ye shal vnderstode yt thyse two appostles fyrste grete synners lefte theyr synne sory contryte synned nomore lord toke ensaple wyll leue synne shall saued yt shryuen forsaketh syne mercy folowethe yt penauce shal haue mercy grace gladde fader see sone ryse frome dethe lyfe also gladde oure lorde moche gladder see ryse dedely synne neuer doo therfore shewyng ensample poule bereth swerde alle crysten peole cut away ye cheynes synne wyth sharpe swerde confessyon dedely synne byndeth sore fede therfore cut away yt cheyne peter also redy open gate heue al cryste peple lette ye shall vnderstonde poule fyrst hye soo feerse ayenst goddis seruautis durst precher deale wt hy left grete malyce feerse gracyous hye proude herte meke lowly al goddis seruautis ppeter also helde hy selfe mooste perfyte stedfast crystis dyscyples wherfore made boste vayn glory redy goo dethe wt crist sayd thus behoueth dey wha crist sayd al dyscyples sholde forsake hy peter greate boost sayd though alle men forsake hy wolde yet ouer whan cryst take peter drewe oute swerde smote seruautis ere hyghte malcus pbut soone whan sawe yt cryst take sholde put deth thenne swore stared neuer knewe forsoke cryste wha herde cocke crowe remebred oure lorde sayde hy cocke crew iii thou shalt forsake thenne peter wente forth et fleuit amare wepte bytterly hyd caue durst come amonge bredren shame tyl oure lorde sente hy name peter euer ashamed sory trespas booster vnstable wordis afterwarde true stable grouded stablenesse perfyght lyuynge moche cryst called hym peter yt stone englysshe thou layeste stone thou shalte fyde soo peter stedfast neyther wele wo neuer fleytered euer stoode sted fast crystes lawe euer syne myde amede yt done amysse afterwarde grete abstynence ete brede oyle wortes full selden flesshe wered syngell kertyll mantell euer often herde ony man mynde ihesus anone began wepe full sore whan herde ony cocke crowe tercio nisi quis tus fuerit ex qua et spiritu sancto saye withoute one baptysed maye entre kygdome heuen palso men yt euyll entrete theyr wyues wyth chylde betynge tredynge vnder theyr fete troublyge theyr vncurteys langage syne greuously moost greuously yf chylde perysshe therby vn aug maius dampnu est missione vnius anime quam milium corporum saye synne letynge one soule thousaunde bodyes pthe thyrde cause yt oure lady vysyte elyzabeth yt ihesus sone wombe sholde wyse sanctyfye iohan ye baptyst instygacyon ye holy goost whiche sayde iohan glad daunced moders wombe et exultauit infans vtero meo c maye ye lerne goodnesse grace may come vnto v yf worshyp oure lady dowtelesse wyll growe therof greate ioye holy goost wyll secretis god also shall shewed wherfore lete v ofte deuoutly say aue maria salutacion maye sure yt wyl resalute v ayene helpe v wha haue moost nede pmoreouer oure lernynge ye shall vnderstonde holy scrypture founde oure lady spake moche cantycle magnificat whiche wryten feste whiche enlarged grete laude god gyuynge thankes benefetes rede spake foure tymes foure grete benefeytes myracles folowen ther vpon pfyrste whan spake ye angell annuncyacyon forth conceyued oure sauyour ihesu cryste pthe seconde day wha vysyted elyzabeth wherthorugh iohan baptiste fulfylled holy goste sanctefyed moder wombe pthe thyrde spake temple whan soughte ihesu sone sayde fili li quid fecisti nobis sic c whiche tyme contynuelly subget moder lady also ioseph instruccyon pthe iiii tyme whan spake feest archytryclyne lorde torned water wyne psoo processe may take goodlernynge blyssed lady speke lytell nothynge speke se laude god prosperyte v lady sayth mathewe xii de omi verbo ocioso c euery ydle worde speke shall gyue acompte laste daye iugemente thenne muste folowe shall gyue strayte acompte noysom speche thre maner synners ben offende theyr speche fyrst ben yt swereth wytyngly thynge true synneth deedly whyther game ernest playnly shewed thomas secuda secude q xcviii also offende gretely swere theyr chyldren yt shall chastyse theyr offence accordnge yet wyll decreto omne iuramentum est seruandum nisi vertat contra salutem animaru xxii q iiii qd dauid euery othe kepte without preiudyce hurte mannes soule also synne gretely yt swere god sayntes theyr bargeyns makynge deceyuynge theyr neyghboure onely grete thynges also small apple sellynge peeres flesshe fysshe swerynge god lady ye gete noo mo ye gete noo better chepe suche byer syde swereth god wyll gyue eyther foude lyers departe ala cristen man sholde swere falsely worlde wynne po peryllous domageable vnto whiche vse saye theyr bargaynes marchaundyses makynge vnto preiudyce extreme sorowe theyr soules god helpe forsake god take deuyll suche vengeaunce suche punysshement god fall vpon suche synfull abhomynable ben syght god vse suche laguage grete shall theyr paynes withouten amendemente seconde ben blasphemer swereth ye wou de sydes bone body lorde sacrament awlter suche suche people synneth gretely vnde augustinus non minus peccant qui cristu blasphemant regnantem celis quam qui christum crucifierunt ambulantem terris whiche englysshe lesse syne blaspheme cryste reygnynge heuen dyde crucyfyed cryst walkynge erthe vnde paulus ad hebre vi rursum crucifigentes filiu dei suche people moche may crucyfye agayne ye sone god ihesu cryst whiche synne swerynge membres cryste lorde somtyme punyssheth hole towne cyte countree tempest thonder pestylence vnde quoda decreto qn que multitudo populi propter delictum vnius punitur dis xlv sed illud psuch blasphemer olde testament afore cryst borne stoned dethe vt habetur leui xxiiii ihesu yf soo trowe ryght many sholde stoned dethe lorde punyssheth theym otherwyse dayes somtyme suche theyr membres swere elles suffre theym dye sodayne dethe mysfortune saynt gregory dyalogus xvii chapytre fourthe boke wryteth sheweth men lerny ge certayne deuylles rome came chylde v yeres olde wantonly brought vp yt whiche blasphemed lorde fendes toke hym vyolently frome faders lappe trysed hym rent body pyeces soule caryed pytte helle dampned eternally wantonesse premembre wel yf lorde suffre punysshement doone babe lytell chylde fyue yere olde trowe ye wyll forgete se vnpunysshed ben ryper aege dyscrecyon nay ye sure thyrde curseth theyr neyghboure thou shalte vnderstande wyttyngly yre vengeaunce curseth neyghboure synneth deedly ofte dooth oftymes seen ye vengeaunce yt desyre theyr neyghboures falleth vpon themselfe vnde genesis xxvii qui maledixerit tibi sit ille maledictus c palso synne greuous yf name god suche euyll speche cursynge thus oure lorde gyue myschefe suche greuous saye clause puttynge therfrom name god saynt thomas sayth lefull curse vnreasonable thynges ben creature god thenne vnlefull curse ony man pnow may leue othes blasphemynges cursynge neyghboures haue pacyence pray theyr amendement folowe mekenes lorde blyssed moder mary vysyte ofte good prayer neyghboure helpe charyte graunte v qui sine fine viuet et regnat secula seculorum amen pde translatione sancti thome frendes suche daye ye shall haue translacion saynt thomas ye martyr yt day take oute graue bone layde shryne ye shall man ordeyned byrth holy man worthy saynt yt shewed fyrst moder fader olde age knowe ouer fyrst knowe moder nyght lay bed slepynge thoughte thomas laye cradell wepte whan herde hym wepe called norse say de loke ye chyld whan came chylde fonde al clothes frompled wolde haue amende myght fold gretnes thought toke thone ende norse thother ende soo moche myghte folde chambre went halle yet wolde went chepe syde cheef strete london thoughte sprad london thenne morowe wente confessoure told hym dreme sayde dame yu arte moche holden god ye chylde yt cradell shall greate power yt london shall gouernauce whan thomas couenable age fader sente abbay merton yt house chanons go scole daye fader came loke howe dyde whan thomas came afore hym anone hys fader felle downe syghte peple dyde hy grete reuerence thenne pryoure ye place rebuked hy sayde thou olde fole reuerence sholde doo thou hym thenne toke ye pryour asyde sayde wote ful well haue doo chylde shal worthy man tofore god crysten people shal hym worshyppe thenne wexed thomas wyse actyfe wysdome yt archebysshop cauterbery sete hy made hy chaunceler englonde gouerned offyce wysely made afterwarde arshebysshop caunterbery thenne anone tourned greate holynes prayer fastynge almesdedes doynge wered harde heyre nexte body breche ye whyche full vermyn horryble syghte see yet chauged one xl dayes also man greate almesdedes caste greate loue god drad deye pthenne rebuked kynge mysdedys yenst holy chirche oppressed reame thenne kynge grete indignacyon exyled hym oute reame dyde thomas greuaunce coude exyled hym alle kynne frendes bothe olde yonge croked lame blynge wymen chyldebed yonge chyldren armes soukynge moche people woo defaute helpe made swere vpon boke sholde neuer tary tyll come tofore thomas encrease paynes whan thomas sawe wepte sorowe grete copassyo theym yet ordeyned yt better atte ease frau ce englonde thenne whan god wolde yt thomas sholde passe oute world byddyng pope counseyle kynge fraunce thomas came caunterbery owne chyrche whan kynges knyghtes herde therof four cursed lyuers wente v day feste crystmasse slewe hy owne chirche aulter say te benet lefte hym dede thenne monkis place wepynge makynge grete sorowe beryed hym newe tombe redy made pbut thenne god shewed grete myracles hym pope alysaunder sente letter englonde archebysshop stephen abbottis prelate salesbury monkes clerkes many wente place thomas laye l yeres kneled ye erthe prayenge thomes deuoutly helpe foure toke vppe tombe greate drede quakynge fo de lytell wrytynge lyeth resteth thomas archebysshop caunterbery prymat englonde pope legate slayne ryghte holy chirche fyfte daye cryste masse greate deuocyon yt syght cryed saynte thomas thenne toke ye hede archebysshoppe kysse kyssed thenne behelde woundes sayde vngracyous wounded thus soo layd hym shryne couered clothe golde sette torch brennynge people wake nyghte thenne morowe came statis londe bare ye shryne place wyth wherfore ye shalle come god holy chyrche praye holy woman yt wyll praye oure lorde v maye haue grace ye fyrste tyme grace dyde penaunce loste grace flesshly luste made myrroure synners yt wyl forsake synne doo penauce shall haue grace yt whiche loste syne fader grete lorde nye kynges blood greate lordshyp iherusalem whiche gaaf lazarus sone gaaf mary castell magdeleyne ye lordshyp longyge ther ye whiche castell name called mari magdeleyne lady therof thenne many bokes sayen saynt iohan euangelyste wedded oure lordo bad hym goo wt hym kepe vyrgynyte dyde clene vyrgyn magdeleyne went forth gaaf synne moche lost ye name magdeleyne callen synfull woman often seen oure lorde made greteste synner yt holyeste afterwardes soo whan oure lorde sawe tyme gaaf woman grace knowe selfe haue repentauce synnes thenne whan mary herde cryste mannys house called symon pharyse toke boxe oynemente suche ye peple vsed tyme hete ye sonne went thyder durst shame goo tofore fete behynde hy herde hym speke toke grete sorow herte wepte tenderly ye teres eyen wasshed crystes fete wyth here hede wyped wt loue herte kyssed anoynted noo worde spake ony man myghte softly herte cryed mercy made vow wolde neuer trespace pthenne lord hadde pyte vpon caste oute seuen fendis forgaaf synnes herynge al thenne toke suche loue cryste lefte lordshyps mawdeleyne goodes hym forth grete loue hys passyon hys dyscyples fledde frome hym lefte hym neuer tyll helpe layde hym tombe whan man durst go thyder fere knyghtes kepte hym spared cu tenebre essent c wha derke dawnynge toke swete bawmes anoynte crystes body shewed loue bothe wyll dede wherfore cryste lyfe heled martha syster reed flyxe vii yere tofore payned sore et resuscitauit lazaru mortuis reysed lazar brother frome deth lyfe layne iiii dayes stynkynge graue whan lorde rose frome dethe lyfe appered suffred touche hym kyssed fete thenne whan knowen iewes cryst shewed many token loue whan cryst styed vp heuen toke mary martha syster lazarus maxencius many put olde shyppe see haue drowned god ordeyned thynge wyll brought saufe londe called myracle rested vnder banke nygh ye temple thenne mary sawe moche people comynge towarde ye temple sacryfyce theyr mawmettes lorde countree came wt magdaleyne gracyous gracyous wordes torned agayne lorde grete lust speke sayd thus yf god thou spekest gracyous soo grete power thou sayest praye hym may haue chylde wyfe barayne wyl beleue hym thenne mary sayd wolde within shorte tyme lady conceyued chylde thene lorde anone made ordeyne euery thyge longed hym go iherusalem peter wyte hy der magdaleynes prechynge true vytayled well shyppe made hym redy thenne came lady prayenge hym myghte go grete prayer ye lorde graunted thenne assente made mary maudeleyne kepe lordshyppes goodes yt mary sette crosse eyther theyr sholders bad goo name god wha seyled day nyghte grete tepest arose moche wende al haue drowned pthenne lady sore aferde therewith began trauayle delyuered manchylde maudeleyne sayd byrth fyll downe dede lorde made greate sorowe lamentacyon sayde ala ala wretche shal chylde nowe moder dede nedest must ye chylde deye also noo womannys helpe kepe pthenne cried maudeleyne sayde ala mary doste thou thus thou behote chylde moder dede ye chyde must nedys deye fawte woman helpe self loke euer whan shal drowned helpe mary haue compassyon chylde thenne sayd shyp man cast body see shall neuer haue reste whyle ye shyp sayd lorde dede lyeth swoune fere praye lete v haue ye shyp yon de roche leuer graue cast water none erthe make graue left hangynge roche stone chylde moder couered wt mantell toke god mary mawdeleyne kepe wente way whan came iherusale spake peter bad hy good coforte though wyfe dede god myghte restore lyfe ayene thenne peter shewed hym place lorde quycke dede tolde hym byrthe passion resurreccyon ascencyo enformed sayth made hy stedfast cryste whan ii yere peter sente hy home ayene badde hy grete wel mawdeleyne felysshyp thenne wha ye lorde came ferre ye see sawe place wyfe laye longed sore herte goo thyder prayed shypman set hy sawe lytell chylde syttyge see sonde pleyng smale stone soone ye chylde sawe hym ranne forth rocke folowed tyll came lefte wyfe toke vp mantell fou de ye chylde soukyng moders pappes thenne thanked god mary maudeleyne sayde mary yu art greate god yt haste keped yonge chylde soukynge vpon dede body greate comforte ioye yu wylte pray thy lorde wyf myghte restored lyf euer boude thy seruaut wyll whyle lyue thenne worde spake sayde blessyd mote yu mary mydwyfe nouryse chylde whyle haue pylgremage thenne sayd man wyfe arte yu lyue sayd ye syr nowe come fro pylgremage ye tolde euery place kneled downe tha ked god mary magdeleyne whan came home foude mary prechynge techynge peple anone kneled downe thanked tolde peter sayde prayed telle sholde wolde doo good wyll thenne mary bad sholde distroye ye temple mawmentry byld chirches make fontes crysten peple within shorte tyme londe crystened thenne mary gaaf contemplacyon went ferre wildernesse therty wynters vnknowen ony man descendebant angeli et eam ethera leuabant angellis came seuen tymes daye bare vp ayre fedde heuenly fode wha god wolde sholde speketh wysshe crystes fete bad preest goo maxencius bysshoppe byd hym ester day mournynge chyrche wyl mete whan come ye chirche sawe howe mary borne vp two cubites fro erthe augellys sore agast ne mary called hy come nere goo saye masse myghte houseled thenne syghte ye peple wha masse done houseled receyued goddis body fourme brede anone therwyth gaaf vp goost thenne toke bysshop holy body layed tombe stone wrote lyfe worshyppe god dyde soo gracyously synfull peple wyl leue theyr synne thus ye maye come euerlastynge blysse whiche god brynge v amen pde festo sancti iacobi apostoli frendis suche day ye shal haue sayt iames daye appostle ye shall faste euen worshyppe god holy appostle iames holy came holy kynde ladyes systers sone broder saynt iohan euangelyst thassent ye appostles sent spayne preche worde god ye people combred synne mawmetry myght torne ix persones yt whiche left two preche seuen toke wt hym iurye herde one called hermogines dyscyple hyght philetus two begyled soo people iames torned crystes fayth anone torned agayne mawmetry thenne iames blamed torne frome euerlastynge blysse euerlastynge dampnacyon thenne hermogynes herde therof came dysputed wt iames fayth hopynge fendes craft haue ouercome hym thenne iames dyde many myracles yt phyletus forsoke hermogenes mayster hermogenes wrothe sent company fendes sayd go ye brynge iames phyletus bounde vnto whan fendes came iames aungell god redy bounde fendes yt cryed iames appostle haue mercy v bounde sore wt yren chaynes wo v euery syde sayd iames wherfore ye come hyder sayd hermogynes sent v hyder brynge phyletus boude hym goddes aungelles haue bounde v wo v suffre payne thenne sayd iames wyl lose ye go hermogynes brynge hym hyther bounde hym harme thenne sayd hermogynes thou haste sent v haue boude yren chaynes wyll bynde brynge iames thenne sayd iames false hermogynes hath doone v moche trybulacyons dysease gyue v leue auenge bothe v vpon hy thenne sayd iames nay soo mayster ihesus bad good agaynst euyll thenne iames bad phyletus vnbynde hermogynes thenne sayd hermogynes knowe malyce fendes praye iames gyue thy power elles fendes wyll sle iames gaue hym owne staffe wente boldely owne hous toke bokes kest theym see came iames fell downe knee cryed hym mercy thenne iames gladde crystned hym taught hym fayth holy man god wrought many myracles hym thenne herde iewes therof toke iames bounde rope aboute necke ledde hym vnto kynge herode prayed hym iames dethe elles wolde torne theyr nacyon crystes faythe destroye theyr lawe thenne herode commaunded smyte heed wha deede hermogynes phyletus wt many dyscyples toke iames body durst iewes bury toke theym shyppe went see prayenge god brynge wolde body buryed thenne god gouerned ye shyppe landed spayne quene called lupa yt wolfe called cursed lyuynge thenne toke body layde vpon stone stone waxed soft body sanke downe stoone lyke ben tombe made therfore thenne kept corp whyle went quene lupa sayd wolde receyue iames lyfe god sent body thyder buryed wherfore pray place burye body worshyp suche holy man quene dyde wolues kynde wyst well yt kynge spayne yll man maners wolde harme sent hym praynge ordeyn place body myght buryed dyde cursed man shold toke put pryson bounde fast hande fote grete yren chaynes sate mete aungell came lete pryson badde go theyr way dyde whan kynge herde sente two knightes wc moche people brynge agayne whan ye knyghtes came brydge yt gone ouer wolde haue gone brydge brake ye knyghtes al people drowned thenne kynge aferde vengeaunce sent theym peasybly prayed come agayne sholde haue theyr desyre whan came agayne kynge comaunded cyte crystned whan ye quene herde yt wrothe thought ye harme dyspyte coude sent prayenge come wolde ordeyne hym best wyse whan come sayd go suche hyl haue ox bulles take yoke wayne laye corp therin lete theym choyse theyr waye thyder lede wayne graunt place bury corp thus dyde grete malyce hopynge wylde bestes wolde haue dystroyed whan deed bodyes slay wery lay downe hous welles loked vp ye dong swalowes fel eyen blyde toke pacyently thaked god hys vysytacyo god restored hy syght ayene iiii anna temple iherusale whan ioseph lady bare cryste yt temple candelmasse daye prophecyed crist sholde fall anna soo holy yt whan wedded seuen yere husbonde deyed thenne went ye temple nyghte daye tyll iiii score yere olde thenne grace god see hy bodely deyed armes v anna ladyes moder wha lady age brought temple left ye vyrgynes age lerne moyses lawe serue god nyghte daye anna husbonde called ioachym oure ladyes fader come ye kynred dauyd prophetes told longe tofore kynred dauyd sholde descende downe cryst wryten bokes yt kepte ye tresorye ye temple kynge herode iherusalem thoughte torne ye lyfe god hy eyre toke bokes oute tresory made brenne mynde cryst sholde haue forgote meane haue torned lygnage dauyd hym wherfore bokes telleth howe ioachym descended fro dauyd pbut whan herode hadde done foule dede yet ther good wyse men yt copyes bokes home ye tolde ioachym came ye kyngdom dauyd dauyd many chyldere one theym called natan ye whyche come leuy nother called panther hy came barban yt ioachyms fader yt maryed ladyes moder pater eius ioachym mater vero ana vocati ioachym ladyes fader moder anna whan chylde gyuen maryage ioseph ioachy anna ended theyr lyfe full vertuously therfore god sayth good tree comyth good frute soo good woman came holy ofsprynge soo lete v serue holy woman yt maye pray v euer amen pfestum transfiguracionis domini celebratur vi die augusti satyrdaye euer ye fyrste hole weke lente redde gospell mathewe ye xvii chapytre assupsit ihesus petru iohane ye whiche shewed yt sauyoure toke iii dyscyples peter iames iohan brother ledde vnto hye moute yt called thabor trasfygured byfore face shone ye sone hys clothyge whyte ye snow appered moyses hely spekynge hym c done lernynge grete co forte ioye yt come ye lorde thus transfygured soo greate bryghtnesse betokeneth glory ye soule body euery crysten man woman shall haue yf lyue well worlde kepe comaudemetis daye greatly pryuyleged holy chyrche moche yt order ben gyue day thoruth crystedome grete pardon grauted day dyuerse place people rome wt hy wha romayns senatours herde drede loue made decius emperour whan phylyps sone herde telle yt fader dede wyse ferde leest deci wolde haue slayne hy gaue faders tresour holy chirche bare pope sixt laurece prayeg hy ye deci slew hy sholde dele tresour holy chirche poore people nede thenne decius slewe phylyps sone feere leest wolde haue venged faders dethe whan come mannes state treasoure pope syxtus laurence treasoure put laurence pryson thenne man hyght lucyllus pryson yt grete wepynge lost syght thenne laurence made hym se agayne crystned hy wherfore many blynde men woman came laurence theyr syght thenne themperour sent laurence delyuer ye treasure thenne prayed hym thre dayes respyte wolde shewe hym treasour thre dayes laurence lete pryson went gadred poore people gyder myght fynde blynde lame croked thyrde day brought themperoure palays sayd lo euerlastynge treasour wyl neuer fayle wyl endure euer heuen shewed laurence largenesse agaynst couetyse deled goddes sake goodes rychesses hadde myght haue spente vayne pleasure worldly operacyons yf hadde wolde also tourmente in passyon shewed perfyte loue feruent swetenes thene emperour grete furoure anger commaunded brynge forthe maner instrumentes tourmentrye scourge nayles stone salte pytche brymstone brenny ge cole yren shaftes barres yren gredyrons comaunded sholde spente worne vpon laurence wolde shewe treasoure forsake god beleued adoure doo sacryfyce mawmettes ydolles thenne sayd laurence thou vnblyssed man mete drynkes haue euer desyred sought ryght swete delycyous mete drynkes pleaseth satysfyeth thy body tourmentes pleasen soule maken stronge myghty suffre passyon lordis sake themperour wroth commauded bete hym scourge full knottes leue tyll blode ranne downe euery syde layde cheynes yren brennyge sydes yt brenned flesshe fro ye bone euer laurence thanked god hertely decius wode wo sayde thoughe yu wyth thy wytchecrafte scornest tormentys yet thou sholdeste scorne comaunded ayene bete hy whyppes knottes lede tyll bone bare thenne laurence helde vp hede prayenge god thenne came voyce fro heuen sayde thou muste suffre tormentes passyon loue deci herde hymselfe thou shall come greate ioye blysse thenne sayd decius people ye maye alle fendes come coforte hym go bete hym ayene scourge knyght themperours hyghte romanus sawe angell shete sylke come wype laurence sydes forsoke emperoure became dyscyple saynt laurence laurence anone crystened hym thenne decius made smyte romanus hede thenne decyus dyde make greate fyre set gerdyren theron roste laurece thrested hym downe fyre forkis thenne laurence loked vpon theperoure sayd yu wretche yt syde rosted ynough ete therof whyle syde rosteth drede thy tormentis cast eyen vp god sayde lorde ihesu take spyryte yelde vp goost thenne tormentours went theyr way left body lyenge thenne come crysten people toke body beryed wyth grete lamentacyon thus laurence shewed mekenes ayenste malyce largenes ayenst couetyse ayenst passyon loue swetnesse grete loue god made hym set noughte tormentes body saynte gregory telleth preest yt hyghte staculus besy mende chirche saynte laurence yt destroyed lombardes wanted brede werke men made moche sorowe therfore prayed god saynt laurence besely helpe loked ouen foude full newe whyte brede wende wold haue serued weke founde inough tyme werke makynge pnarracio pwe fynde yt emperoure cursed man lyuynge whan dede came legyon fendes fetche hym came holy heremytes cell made greate noyse heremyte greate meruayle therof opened wyndow spake one came behynde asked name god sayde fendes sente emperoure dede loke yf myghte haue theyr rewarde thermyte comaunded theym come agayne hym knowe sped dyde soo sayde synnes layde balaunce nye ouercome thenne come brennynge though tempte hym none boden ony thynge helpe soucoure vnto soule shall lete downe brydge obedyence soner better dyde oure lady whan augell gabryell tolde concepcyon sone lete downe brydge none rylle knewe wheder frende enemye sayd sholde contryue mayde kepe vowe chastyte made fore herde lete downe brydge obedyence sayd ecce ancylla domini lo goddes owne honde mayde done thy worde castell treble thryes double walled fyrst wall betokeneth wedlocke fyrste wyfe vnto ioseph elles iewes wolde haue stoned lechoure yf hadde contynued without wedlocke ferther wall betokeneth pacyence ynner vyrginyte whiche clene maydehode lytell worthe strengthed wall pacyence lytell helpe maydenheed lytel worth nothynge suffre persecucyon dysease way playnynge grudgynge claterer iangeler curser waryer scolde gaue soo grete delyte sone wordes bare herte lyfe techynge cryst somoche taught foure euangelystes marke mathewe luke iohan moche wrote namely saynt luke wrote moche manhode cryst fulfylled offyce mary best whan sone styed vp heuen lefte besynesse gaue contemplacyon tyll sone fette worlde thus euery man vnderstonde may se gospell conuenyent redde toucheth lyfe lady thenne day thende lyfe worlde clerenes thenne sayd wyll well soo yt may se thenne sayd aungel come suche place yu shal se thenne gladde thought wolde hyde one eye loke soo whan came yt place layde hande ouer ye one eye sawe yt eye came lady sawe went way anone blynde eye sawe thenne syght lyked hym well wolde fayne se agayne prayed nyght day myght se agayne thenne sayd aungell yf thou se agayne thou shalte lese syght eye sayd wyll well though thousande eyen come suche place thou shalte se whan came sawe thenne sayd lady good seruaunt whan thou sawe fyrst yu lost one thyn eyen wylt thou whan yu hast loste eye thenne sayd dere lady wyll well though thousande eyen thenne sayd lady thou hast grete lykynge yu shalt haue thy syght bothe thyn eyen agayne well euer yu haddest better thene serued lady euer lyues ende wente seruyce worshyp god saynt bartylmewe ye shall vnderstonde bartylmewe asmoche saye filius suspendentis whiche saye sone hangynge vpon vpo water ye shall vnderstande god hangeth vpon water two wayes fyrst whan hanged vpon cloudes fyrmament tyll seeth tyme lette downe another waye hangeth vpon water whan man woman sory theyr synnes wepynge sore trespace bytterly god taketh teres hangeth hye hylle heuen sayntes heuen may haue syght grete ioye al sayntes aungelles ben heuen whan maye se man woman hathe done amysse many trespaces forsake theyr synne therfore teres man woman sory theyr synnes sone ben serueth hym hangynge vp foure wayes deuocyon holy orysons prayenge faith monycyon suffrynge passyon hangynge god warde deuoute orysons whiche sasayd mouth thought hert herte alwaye hangynge vp towarde god bothe worde dede preest sayth masse sursum co da holde vp hertes thus holy saynt barthylmew euer herte god deuocion pnarracio pwe fynde wryten thus kneled hodred tymes day hondred tymes suffrynge passyon whan bysshop temple sawe people almoost tourned crysten fayth lefte fendes mawmetry went vnto ye cyte kynge called astrages broder kynge polymyes co playned hym sore sayd yt man come
