made cyte bare bare waye myght wente temple toke tresour iewels precyous stone bare awaye thus cursyd man dyde destroye many kyngdomes bare holy crosse owne countree themperour eraclius herde therof full wroth sory sente cosdre trete wt hym eraclius crysten man cosdre answered cursedly sayd wolde treate tyll peple forsake crystendom sacrefyce mawmettes emperour eraclius betoke god gadred hym oost peple fyght wt cursyd kyng cosdre hopynge god gete holy crosse ayen whan cursyd kyng cosdre came fell suche fantasye madnesse toke sone al gouernauce reame lete make hous hymself maner awter lyke vnto heuen made shynynge golde precyous stone set hymself myddes chayr golde commaunded peple sholde calle hym god sate holy crosse ryght honde stede sone left honde tame kocke stede holy ghost hymself myddes stede trynyte thus sat lyke madde man sone herde eraclius comynge wente ayenst hym met hym grete water ouer whiche water brydge thassent theyr oostes two chyef captayns myddes brydge sholde fyght theym bothe endes ye brydge sholde drawen vp whiche yt vyctory sholde haue kyngdomes eraclius full fayth crosse trusted prayer people yt ouercome enmye cosdres peple sterynge holy ghost torned fayth free wyll themself whan crystened wente eraclius wt oostes ye olde kyng cosdre satte trone sayd hym thus cause thou hast doo worshyp holy crosse thou shalt chose yf thou wylt crystened haue thy kyngdome ayen lytell trybute rest pea elles deed forsoke crystened anone eraclius smote heed made crye yt tresour sholde dealed amonge men precyous stone iewels sholde kepte restore chirches destroyed bare crosse ierusalem whan came mount olyuete towardes cyte ierusalem rydynge trapped hors wolde haue ryden ye cyte ierusalem sodenly yates felle togyder playne wall thenne gretely astonyed meruayled gretely vengeaunce made grete mone thene came aungell stode vpon gate sayd quando rex noster c whan kynge heuen came way gate towarde passyon rode trapped hors clothe golde mekely symple asse gyuynge ensample mekenes people thenne aungell went way thenne kynge deuocion yt coude myght anone dyde clothes shyrte went bare fote bare legged thenne gate opened went gate iherusalem temple offred crosse agayne thenne ye grete ioye people crosse grete myracles yt god shewed worshypped afore worshyppe crosse cast downe lyft vp wherfore daye called exaltacyon holy crosse saynt austyn saythe crosse fyrst grete spyte velony grete worshyppe emperoures kynges worshyp grete reuerence pnarracio pwe hede legenda aurea iewe came chyrch defaute man chyrche went rode grete enuy cryst cut rodes throte anone blode sterte clothes clothes al reed blode thenne hydde rode preuy place went home crysten man mette hym sayd hym thou hast slayne hast thou done hym iewe sayd nay ye crysten man sayd thy clothes ben blody hym thenne iewe kneled downe sayd forsothe god crysten people beleue vpon grete vertue tolde hym done cryed mercy herte soo crystened holy man euer wente vnto euerlastynge ioy blysse whiche god brynge v al amen quatuor temporum good frendes weke ye shall haue ymbre dayes wednesday fryday saterdaye yt whiche dayes calixtus ordeyned foure tymes yere conuenable aege fast certayn cause ye shal olde faders fasted foure tymes ye yere agaynst foure hye solempne feestes yf wyll shewe v good chyldre must faste folowe rule vsed therfore fast foure tymes fyrst marche seconde whytsontyde thyrde bytwene heruest sede tyme fourth crystmas marche tyme yt dryeth vp moysture ye erthe wherfore fast yt tyme drye erthe body humures yt nedeful body soule ye tyme humour lechery tempteth man moost ony tyme yere also fast whytsontyde gete grace ye holy ghoost yt may loue charyte god worlde caritas cooit multitudine pcto rum charyte couereth ye multytude synnes also must fast haue mekenes hertes put away pryde yt renneth within v also fast bytwene heruest seed tyme haue grace gader fruytes good werkes ye hous conscyence ensample good lyuynge amonge people yt comyn wt bothe ryche poore also fast wynter sle stynkynge wedes synne foule erth flesshely lustes yt maketh good augels good people wt drawe fro v ryght nettle breneth rose floures growe nye hym wyse vycyous man woman stereth setteth fyre yt ben company cause fast foure tymes yt yere euery tyme thre dayes betokeneth thre specyall vertues helpeth man grace fastynge deuout prayenge almesse dede doynge opynyon moche people dayes ben called ymbre dayes bycause elder faders wolde dayes ete breed cake made vnder asshes etynge reduced theyr mynde yt asshes soo sholde torne agayne wyst soone torned away dylycious mete drynkes toke none hede easy sustenaunce caused thynke dethe wyll cause man desyre hym nedeth abstayne hym selfe al maner bodely lustes encrease vertues wherby may come euerlastynge blysse pde sancto matheo appostolo good frendes suche day ye shal haue saynt mathewes daye whiche crystes appostle ye shall fast euen come holy chyrche worshyp god saynt mathew gretely comended holy chyrche certayne holy vertues obedyent cryst ye fyrst callynge preched gospell wtout faynynge suffred passyon wtout ony denyenge fyrst obedyente cryst ye fyrst callynge sate certayne place besy gete good cryst came yt way loked hym bad hym come go hym thenne kest grete loue cryst yt left goodes yt sued cryst forthe full symple full poore also fedde cryst gladly daye prayed cryst ete wt hym made cryst grete feest dylycate mete drynkes fedynge cryst company fedde yt wolde come crystes sake moche people sued cryst whersoeuer went et secuti sut eu turbe multe dyuers cause many folowed hy heled theyr sore dyuers sykenes se ye myracles yt cryst dyde shewe ete drynke wt hym yt enmyes yt lerned ye lawe yf myght haue taken hym wt ony worde wherby myght haue accused hy refourmed vertues doctryne techynge ye appostles many vn versus morib signa cib blasphemia doctrina fuere causa cu turba secuta fuit whan mathew fedde cryst thus come wt hy cryst made hym one dyscyples gaue hym knowlegynge preche beleue goddes worde boldely euer yt spared neyther loue ne drede soo mathew appostle came tyme cyte preched yt called nadabar founde moche people taught fendes craft nygromancy taught soo many thynges meruaylous yt grete wonder many mennes wytte sand al people sholde beleue worshyp mathewe anone delyuered theyr nygromancye soo people knewe openly fendes crafte wherfore people whiche dyde beleue nygromancy made dragon fendes crafte spyt degorge flambes fyre theyr mouthes brenne stenche slewe moche people dyde brynge dragon haue deuoured saynt mathew wha saynt mathew herde therof made crosse hym went ayest anone ye dragon fel downe deed hym thenne sayd mathew people yf ye haue ony myght reyse theym agayne lyfe power sayd mathewe yf goddes seruaunt wolde make theym ye purposed techynge mayster ihesu cryst good ayenst euyl wherfore bydde dragon aryse go suche place ye shall neuer greue man beest anone rose wente theyr waye thus mathewe torned moche people came se syght preched people tol ioyes paradyse sayd euer daye neuer nyght euer youthe neuer aege helthe neuer sykenes rose lylyes floures without welowynge popyngayes nyghtyngales dyuerse byrdes euer syngynge loue rest pea euerlastynge charyte soo byleueth cryst dothe commaundementes shall come theder without endynge thus preched cyte cursed people toke hym put eyen kest hym pryson tyll toke aduysement dethe sholde deye thenne came au gell saynt andrewe preched ferre countree brought hym ouer see saynt mathewe whan andrewe sawe mathewe foule anone andrewe wepte prayed god hy anone god restored mathewe syght agayne andrewe wente agayne owne countree preche agayne came fro whan mathewe pryson wente preched cyte nabadaran whiche kynges sone deyed sente kynge mathewe prayed hym restore sone lyfe agayne dyde wherfore kynge wyfe doughter yt called eufegeme toke crystendome moost parte ye people god hadde chosen eufegeme holy woman godwarde mathewe blessid gaue vayle chastyte charyte holy woman kepar many vyrgyns deyed fader came kynge yt called hertagus whiche loued mayden eufegeme prayed mathewe helpe hym might haue sayd mathewe yt myght wedded kynge heuen myght breke spousehede hertageus wrothe badde slee mathewe stode sayd masse ye auter came one behynde hym slewe hym crysten people buryed body chirche bad ye kynge sette fyre eufegemes hous euery syde brenne therin mathewe appered badde good chere anone torned fyre fro hous kynges palays lefte nothyng saue kynge yonge chylde hym kynge smyten meselry foule grete payne wo slewe hymselfe vengeaunce fell hy selfe wolde haue done vnto ye may wel se grete myracles holy man therfore lette v serue hym wyll praye v lorde amen pde sancto michaele archangelo good frendes suche daye ye shall haue saynt myghelles daye tharchaungell daye holy chirche maketh mynde mencyon aungelles grete socoure comforte helpe mankynde hadde aungelles specyally saynt mychaell thre prerogatyues yt wonderfull appyerynge merueylous myracles werkynge vyctoryous fyghtynge wonderfull apperynge sayt gregory sayth wha almyghty god wyl werke ony wonderfull dede thenne sendeth mychaell seruaut banerer bereth shelde sygne armes wherfore sent moyses aaro egypt werke merueyles though sygne moyses werkynge done mychael departed reed see kept water two partyes whyle people israhell wente thrugh passed lad forth flom iordan kept water lyke hylle eche syde theym whyle passed sauf sounde londe behest also mychaell keper paradyse taketh soules sent thydre also shal slee antecryste ye mount olyuete shal bydde ye deed aryse come dome angelles wt hym shal brynge al instrumentes lordes passyon crosse ye crowne spere nayles hamer spoge eysell gall scourge thynges crystys passyon yt shall dampned yt sette nought ne byleue passyon thus appyereth wonderfully wroughte also myracles merueylously apulia hye hylle yt hylle called garganus nye grete cyte dwelled ryche man dyuerse catell bestes wente hylle happed bulle lefte behynde bestes thenne man seruaunt went seke bulle founde hym standynge hole grete denne thenne one shot arrowe hym arowe torned ayen smote hym yt shot arrowe hurte hym sore pthenne sore ferde merueylled myght meane wente bysshop tolde hym cause bysshop prayde god haue parfyght knowleche thenne mout garganus mychaell appyered hym sayd goddes wyll sholde hurte ye shall knowe well keper ye place wherfore go ye make chirche ye denne bysshop made fayre chirche also mychaell appyered bysshop badde hym go hylle toppe vnto mount gardell foude bulle tyed sholde make chirche worshyp god saynt mychaell two roches stone eyther syde yt werke myght vp thenne saynt mychaell appered man hyght haymo badde hym go put awaye ye roche drede thynge man wente thyder sette sholders badde roche go vtter name god saynt mychaell hylles wente vtter moche neded werke pnarracio pwe rede also lyf saynt gregory grete multytude people rome sawe arrowes fyre come ayer slewe moche people thenne saynt gregory prayed god cesse ye pestylence sawe angel standynge vpon castell walle wypynge blody swerde ye agell sayd saynt mychael sent thydre punysshe peple synne thus mychaell merueylle myracles werkyng also vyctoryous fyghtynge whan ye cytezens sepontyne oppressyd wt paynems sholde gyue batayll prayed oft sayt mychaell helpe ye nyght ye batayl sholde mychaell appered ye bysshop sayd hy haue drede go ye batayll boldely wolde helpe hy soo ye morowe wha batayll sholde hylle garganus ouercouered grette myste pand arrowes come myst fleynge fyre boltes thonder hurte moche people paynyms moche slewe ye nyght moche people infydeles many slayne alyue sawe grete myracle god crystned saynt iohan euangelyst sayth appocalyps mychaell aungelles fought wt lucyfer heuen called dragon aungelles wt helpe god mychaell better droue ye dragon aungelles ayre bytwene heuen erth soo yet thycke mote sonne cryst came heuen blast thonder therfore yet whan thonder fall downe erthe fere goo vp agayne tyll haue doone harme make debate stryues manslaughter make grete wyndes bothe londe water moche harme yet wolde doo yf drede god saynt mychaell theyr sorowe se soules aungelles heuen place tofore also spyrytes stode stedfast towardes god flaterynge whiche saynt mychaell droue heuen yle see ye shall pa saynt brandon sayled see came yle sawe tree ryght grete bothe heyght brede meruayle se whiche tree sate many birdes thycker ye bowes whyte snowe thenne prayed god knowe thenne came one theym sate shyppe borde batered wynges made sounde lyke organ thenne sayd brandon yf yt come lyke messager speke tell ye ben thene sayd aungelles stode stedfast beleue mychaell therfore dryuen oute whan mychaell droue lucyfer augelles yet haue euery day remedy worship god pthan mychaell wonderfull apperynge merueylous myracles doynge wherfore lette v worshyp holy vnderstande cryst iiii euangelystes marke mathewe luke iohan wrote ye gospel gospell say goddes worde holy euangelystes wrote onely yt god spake also dyde suffred mankynde sholde knowen mankynde euermore thynke goddes worde four lykened foure dyuers beestes ben portrayed foure partyes crosse euery syde cryst marke lyon mathew man luke oxe iohan egle let man suppose suche bestes lykened suche bestes dyuers cause bycause mathew wrote moost crystes manhede therfore lykened man luke wrote moost crystes sacryfyce dethe therfore lykened oxe oxe offred sacryfyce olde lawe tokenynge cryst sholde offred synne people sacryfyce auter crosse marke wrote moche ye resurreccyon therfore lykened lyon bokes saye tell whan lyon hath yonge whelpes shall lye deed iii dayes ben whelped cometh ye lyon seeth whelpes deed anone maketh rorynge cryenge yt dede whelpes wake therwith queken take lyfe whan cryst layd thre dayes tombe thenne fader spake hym bad hy ryse rered hym frome deth lyfe palso iohan lykened egle kynde flyeth hyghest ayre nexte sonne iohan wrote moost godhede lytell manhede cause yt lykened foure dyuerse bestes pbut ye shall vnderstonde luke lykened oxe iii maner wyse yt thought worde dede offred thoughte god fyrst besy gete goodes worlde wt crafte bokes tel fyrst leche couetyse good slewe many bodely offeded god greuously yt none offred thought sacrefyse bokes sayth god hyghly pleased wt thought yt wha man sory synnes h herte thynketh verely sake mende hy also offred worde sacrafyce wonte spede speche many ydle wordes came appostle tourned speche ye profyte cryste people wherfore wente lady taught hy ye gospell yt wrote mayden lady cheryshed hy ye taught hy ful goodly ye augel came message sayd answere gaue thynge dyde sone doyg tyll oure lorde styed vp heuen whan luke lerned perfyghtly loked marke mathew wryten toke wrote obscurly derkly wrote playnly openly thynge thus prechynge techynge offred worde vnto god pand also offred dede vnto god sacrafyce payned hym selfe dyuerse penaunce fastynge alsoo harde lyuynge wepynge praynge also dyde wryte persecucyon appostles suffred iewes iherusalem whan grete pursuyte tourmentes crystes sake wrote ye persecucyon saynt stephen stoned dethe thenne went saynt luke saynt poule sued hym many myscheues dyseases full grete drede neuer departed hym tyll poule deed thenne wente luke countree called bethany preched worde god tyll xli wynter aege deyed full fayre full holy ghoost lyued holy vertues dethe god shewed hym many fayre myracles ended cryst went euerlasty ge blysse whiche god brynge v amen pde sanctis simone et iuda frendes suche daye ye shall haue ye feest symon iude ye shall fast euen morow come chyrche worshyp god holy appostles pye shall vnderstande yt eyther hath two name yt one called symon zelotes yt iudas iacola iudas thadeus shewinge name yt man hath worlde deyeth passeth myde whan deed wherfore euery crysten man sholde besy take hym name yt sholde wryten boke lyfe sholde laste euer therfore two appostles suffred grete penaunce trauayle trybulacyon dysease last payne deth crystes sake meke herte clene conscyence symon moche say obedyece yt maketh man meke herte iudas moche say confessyon ye clenseth mannes coscyence syne thus dyed gaue men ensaple suffred dethe crystes sake deyed clene conscyece thenne shall wryten booke lyfe grete worshyp ye fraternyte heuen grutchen theyr hertes dysease persecucyon euer pleynynge haue nede praye god healed sykenesse yt haue theyr spyrytes pnarracio pwe rede lyfe apostle kynge called abagarus lepar herde lorde ihesu cryste dyde many myracles heled theym yt seke wrote letter wyse kynge abagarus greteth iesus sauyour welle ye precheth ye countrey ierusalem haue herde thy myracles thou doost soo thou heleste maner sekenesse wythoute ony herbes salues blynde croked lame merueylle thou reyseste dede bodyes lyfe wherfore thynke herte byleue yt thou arte goddis sone come downe frome heuen erthe lyued amonge people one wherfore wryte thou wylt come hele leperhode greueth full sore soo vnderstonde iewes haue ordeyned doo deth haue lytell cyte yt good honeste plenteuous suffysaut v lyue shall haue pea thene cryst wrote agayne sayd thou art blyssed beleuest hast seen thou woldest sholde come say must doo came wyll sende dyscyples yt shal hele thy leprehede thenne cryst myght come hym grete desyre se hym sent hym paynter mayster crafte paynte crystes vysage coude whan paynter came cryst loked vysage shone bryght yt myght loke theron made grete sorowe mournynge come soo ferre myght spede purpose thene cryst toke clothe paynter wyped face therwith thenne forme face theron thenne paynter bare ye kynge thenne kynge wonder gladde dyde grete reuerence wt herte thenne crystes ascencyon thomas ynde assent appostles sente kynge abagarus whan sawe thomas saw suche shynynge face yt wende cryst thenne sayd thomas kynge beleue cryst yu shalte hole sayd beleue hole hym fayne wolde wroke put hym dethe anone hole thenne iudas went symon went bothe togyder percy preche dyde many myracles torned ye kynge xlii thousande crysten fayth crysten people encreased strongely kyge meyny crystned withdrewe theyr offrynges theyr mawmettes bysshoppes lyuy ge wherfore wrothe gadred togyder toke appostles ledde theym theyr temple doo sacryfyce theyr mawmettes elles sholde deed thenne came aungell asked theym yf wolde haue theyr ennemyes deed sayd desyred haue theyr ennemyes torned crysten faythe aungell asked yf wolde suffre martyrdome crystes sake sayd wolde suffre dethe thenne commaunded tourned mawmettes temple commaunded fendes come pull ymages pyeces dyde bysshop wrothe theyr goddes fell pyeces anone came thondrynge lyghtnynge cloue temple thre partyes downe grounde thenne bysshoppes sodeynly slewe appostles thenne kynge toke theyr bodyes buryed ryally made fayre chyrche worshyp god holy appostles pde solempni festo omnium sanctorum frendes suche daye ye shall haue halowen day ye shall fast euen ye morowe come chyrche worshyp god lady halowen good frendes ye shall vnderstande yt feest ordeyned thre specyall cause ben fyrst temple halowyge omyssion fulfyllynge also neclegent lyuinge fyrst temple halowynge whan romayns lordes worlde made temple rome lyke doue hous named pantheon set myddes ye temple ymage chefe mawmet rome euery londe worlde ymage name londe ymage wryten vnder fote ymage made nygromancy yf ony londe torned emperour anone ymage londe wolde torne backe ymage rome face walle whan bysshoppes came ye temple founde ony ymage torned anone wolde goo emperour tel hym thenne wolde ordeyne hoost people sende ye londe set rest pea temple endured thus vnto ye tyme pope bonyface fourthe came thenne went emperour yt called foca prayed wolde gyue hym ye temple myght put oute multytude mawmettes halowe worshyp god lady halowen gaue temple ye pope came pope yt called gregory commaunded al holy chyrche halowe feest lyke begonne also feest ordeyned pope fulfyll omyssyons many sayntes dayes yere leue vnserued many yt may serue echone hymselfe saynt iherome sayeth eche day yere xm martyr take ye fyrst daye ianuary wherfore holy chyrche ordeyned daye sholde fulfyll haue left behynde al yere thus euery sayntes euen hath worshyp v yf kepe well day worshyp god lady halowen also feest ordeyned halowed clense v neclygence vnconnynge also worldly occupacyons doynge full recheles kepynge holy dayes therfore feest ordeyned sholde make amendes moche may haue trespaced feestes therfore vnderstande ye grete peryll breke feest ony worldy occupacyon werkynge synne doynge byenge sellyge ony falshode contryuynge also ye shall vnderstande day prayer shall sooner herde ony day daye sayntes heuen come togyder pray god v therfore ye may well knowe comynge togyder shall sooner herde yf came one two theymselfe pthe holy sayntes whiche ben heuen sometyme bothe flesshe blode body bone elder faders full gladde make moche ioye whan may gete ony prayer almesdedes v whiche may presente sauyour blyssed lady prayenge v shewe declare ensample sayntes cometh assembleth togyder daye ye shall pnarracio pwe fynde wryten legenda aurea yere feest ordeyned halowed keper saynte peter chyrche rome daye matens mydnyght whan peple gone frome matens greate deuocyon yt wente euery auter ye chirche sayd deuocyons whan gone aboute thenne wente hye aulter felle aslepe spirite rauisshed saw fader heuen syttynge mageste grete multytude angellis aboute hym thenne fayre quene wt crowne hede rychely arayed greate company vyrgyns maydens suynge ye kyng rose aeynst bad fet chayre golde sette therein thenne came one clothed camellys skynnes hym sued grete copany gode men came nother lyke bysshoppe hy many bysshoppes came greate multytude hadde ben knyghtes moche people come kynge dyde hym worshyp thenne byshop began saye mateyns thenne spake man angell lad asked hym thyse people araye thenne sayde ye angell ye kynge god selfe ye quene lady yt clothed camellys skynnes iohan baptyste patriarkis prophetes hy bysshoppe saynte peter apostle cofessours wt hy ye knyght saynt george wt martyr comyners yt good true lyuers seruauntys god vpon erth came thanke god greate worshyp ye haue erthe prayed besely god theym erth shold haue mercy pthis cause thys feest fyrste founde therfore lete v come chirche worshyp god al halowen yt maye praye v yt maye laste ende ye nombre yt shall worshyp god ye boke speketh saythe thus vidi turbam magna qua nemo dinumerare poterat many yt nombre al pray v euermore maye come blysse amen pin die animarum good frendys suche daye ye shall haue soules daye daye soules purgatory abydyng mercy god haue moche nede helpe ryght holy chyrche worshyppethe alle sayntes holpen prayer theym ryghte soo holy chirche ordeyned day synge rede doo almesdedes hauynge full byleue relese theym ben purgatorye theyr peynes wherfore god wyll yt chrysten peple theyr power daye releue ye leest prayer almesdede day done gretly releueth ye shall vnderstode yt ben foure thynges yt greately helpen soules yt ben purgatorye ben thyse fidelium amicoru oratio elemosynaru largio salutaris hostia et ieiunioru obseruatio prayer frendes deuoutly sayd almesdede doynge mass syngy ge abstynence fastyng prayer helpen moche soule lyke lorde yt hath man pryso ony dystresse atte yt prayer hy yt loueth releseth partye shewed ensample pnarracio pwe fynde wryte legeda aurea yt yt hadde house faste chyrche yerde syde yt dore opened ye chirche vsed custome ofte came wente say euery tyme de profudis cryste soules happed tyme pursued enmyes went homwardes whan come chyrche yarde kneled downe thought saye de profundis thyse enmyes came anone ye dede bodyes rose euerychone suche strumetes wroughte wyth theyr lyues anone droue away hys enmyes wha sawe cryed god mercy man euer prayed dyde almesdedes payne thus may wel preue deuoute prayer helpen many soule ben purgatory also almesdedes helpen many soule sicut aqua extinguit igne ita elemosina extinguit peccatu c ryght water quencheth fyre almesdede quencheth ye fyre brenneth theym yt ben purgatory yf ben good lyf parfyghte charyte done yf almesdede done theym ben ioye haue nede therto put tresour holy chirche goddes wyll dealed reueleth theym haue moost nede therto god assygneth haue moost nede soules yt ben holpen therwith thanke soule done thus ye may well knowe ye almesdedes helpen gretly soules yt done ben purgatory often holy men haue herde fedes crye make grete sorowe wt almesdedes ye soules taken fro pnarracio pwe rede olde tyme good people wolde alhalowen daye bake brede deale crysten soules yet ben vsen fewe fynde legenda aurea knyght sholde goo batayll hadde cosyn loued passynge well sayd hym thus yf slayne ye batayll sholde selle hors deale value poore people almesse praye crysten soules happed slayne cosyn loued well hors toke hym owne vse ne soone knyght appyered cosyn sayd thus hym thyse viii dayes hors thou hast made brenne purgatory therfore god wyl take vengeauce forsoth quod daye thy soule shall helle fende ego purgatus vado regnu dei purged shall goo ye kyngdome heuen anone horryble noyse herde ayer fendes caught man bare hym awaye thyrde helpeth masse whan ony soule appyereth ony man haue ony helpe desireth mass prayeth haue mass songen hym ryght mete drynke conforteth man whan feble sacramet awter conforteth soules ye mass ben done wryten legenda aurea bysshop suspended prest coude saye none masse requiem songe euery daye deuoutly connynge thenne daye bysshop wente towardes matens semed hym deed bodyes rose came aboute hym sayd thou hast sayd masse v ouer thou hast taken preest awaye v loke amended elles god wyll short tyme take vengeauce sake thenne bysshop gretely aferde anone badde preest synge masse requiem dyde tofore dyde ofte myght pnarracio palso fynde fysshers set nettes heruest fysshe toke vp grete pyce yse coldest yse euer felte wolde melte sonne soo brought yse bysshop hadde grete brennynge hete foot coldest euer felte spake voys hy yse sayd soule yt suffreth penau ce yse haue frendes yt wyll doo mass shall delyuered penaunce thou shalte hole thy sykenes yf yu wylte saye masse sayd wolde synge hym bad tell hym name euer whyle masse layde yse vnder fote euer sayd masse yse melted away within whyle yse molten soule frome payne bysshop hole sykenes thenne soule appered hym wt moche ioy sayd wt thy mass syngynge payne euerlastynge blysse tolde bysshop sholde dye soone come euerlastynge ioye whiche god brynge v amen pde sancto martino episcopo good frendes suche day ye shall haue saynt martyns day whan martyn xv yere aege cut mantel two pyeces rode amonge knyghtes yet crystned gaue halfe mantell poore man goddes sake yt asked almesse thene nyght god ye clothe sayd aungell martyn yt yet crystned hath clothed clothe martyn herde worde heuen anone crystned anone left worldes occupacyon gaue hy holynes soo rode tyme yt waye fende came lyke man met hym asked wheder wolde sayd thyder god wyll sayd fende wyll thyn enmye thenne sayd marten god helpe therfore drede marten wexed holy yt rered deed bodyes lyf grete holynes chose bysshop turon tyme men grete peryll lyke spylt one knewe holynes marten sayd marten helpe anone holpen also rode tyme vysytacyon hounde ranne hare vnder hors foot thenne pyte best bad hounde stande stylle lete best go anone hounde stode stylle put erthe also sawe adder swymynge water sayd thadder nomine din iubeo te redire name god comaude go ayen thou comest fro anone torned ayen marten syghed wonder sore sayd sory yt serpentes heren men wyll heren tyme came gate cyte hyght parys kyssed horryble mesell anone hole kysse also pacyente many tymes owne clerkes mocked hym yet suffred pacyently wroth tyme rode waye vysytacyon hymself maner hadde rough mantell blacke came carte waye caryage beestes carte sawe blacke wauerynge wynde fledde awaye brake theyr gere carter whyppe bete marten gaf hym many sore stroke suffred mekely sayd nothynge wolde haue gone theyr waye myght stere fro place tyll knewe marte thenne cryed hym mercy thenne anone gaue hem beestes passed fayr forth harneys saue ynough also tyme marten satte celle fende come hym lykenesse kyng shynynge crowne sayd come fro heuen speke byleue cristus ego sum cryste marten loked hym sayd lorde ihesu cryst wyll come suche araye thou cryste shewe thy woundes anone fende went waye left horryble stenche behynde hym yet tyme came ayen marten repreued hym toke people hym synned shryuen torned ayen synne done tofore sayd though thou take theym thy grace god wyll thenne sayd marten wretche thou wylt leue thy persute crysten people aske mercy meke herte trust god mercyfull wyll gyue ye mercy wha marten sholde passe worlde laye deed bedde fede came satte hym dysputynge hym yf myghte haue caught hym ony worde mysbyleue ende marten sayd hym go hen thou cruell best thou shalt thynge fynde amysse god shall receyue thenne made laye hym asshes heyre thenne sayd vii psalmes letanye gaf vp ghoost buryed owne chirche moche honour thenne liiii wynter came bysshop translated hym whan made thynge redy layde honde marten body haue borne forth myght thenne thought bysshop marten wyll remeued left thenne came fayr olde man badde hym go ayene wolde helpe hym thenne bare body tombe without lettyng whan seruyce done olde man vanysshed waye knewe well saynt marten thenne god shewed many fayr myracles hym pnarracio pit happed tyme two beggers one lame myght go blynde myght see make people haue compassyon theym blynde bare lame lame taught blynde sholde goo thus gate moche good easy lyfe euer aferde mete shrene saynt marten leest wolde haue heled theyr syknesse tyme stretes ende tornynge sodenly corner met shryne saynt marten anone hole blynde myght see ye lame myght goo cryed saynt marten sayd marten thanke good haue thy sake tofore thanke hele must go labour traueyll gete lyuynge people wyll gyue v noo almesse tofore lyued full easely lytell trauell fared daye ye shall haue saynt katherynes daye holy vyrgyn martyr kyges doughter came grete byrthe set mynde god set nought pryde vaynglory rychesses worlde vanyte set onely ihesu whan scole lerned whyle anone wolde dyspute ony clerke yt wolde come enspyred holy goost whan herde tyme maxencyus come towne alexandry moche people ryally cyte dommed theym came make solempne sacryfyce goddes golde syluer lykenes bulles calues bestes thenne saynt katheryn sawe blyssed went temple rebuked emperour boldely sayd dyde foule amysse worshyp fendes leue worshyp god heuen made thynge nought sent man lyfe wytte hele preued grete reason cryst bothe god man bought mankynde passyon dethe crosse taught yt euery man sholde honoure god leue false mawmettes thenne emperoure wrothe badde take warde tyl myght la ser soo meane season sente gretest maysters wysest clerkes myght ony coutree ferre hym whan comen bad go dyspute katheryne ouercome sholde haue ryght wel theyr laboure thenne wrothe come ferre dyspute woman sayd ye leest scoler scole ynough ouercome katheryn dysputed helpe holy goost conuerted theym euerychone faythe lorde ihesu cryst moche redy suffre dethe crystes sake thenne anone maxencius commaunded make grete fyre brenne theym therin helpe holy goost fyre brenned theyr bodyes ne leest clothe yet lay fayre deed ben slepe thenne themperour made doo katheryn naked bete wt sharpe scourge blody full woundes put apryson vii dayes without ony mete drynke thenne ye quene grete lust speke katheryn toke knight wt yt hyght purphyryus went katheryn thenne sawe angell set shynynge crowne golde quenes heed purphyryus heed bad stedfast within thre dayes sholde come heue suffrynge martyrdome thenne sente emperour katheryn wende haue founde nygh deed yt god sent meete heuen whan empe sawe lyue wood wrothe made set bytwene two wheles torned one vpwarde downewarde full hokes swerdes poyntes rase katheryn thenne came aungell wynde brake slewe iiii tyrau thenne sawe quene myracle came kynge husbande rebuked hym yt sawe myyt god openly wolde beleue theron thenne bad ye kynge lede forthe quene cut pappes ye body hooke thenne smyte heed purphyryus buryed lxxx knyghtes yt martred purphyryus beheded also thenne spake themperoure katheryn sayd wolde wed yf wolde forsake cryst beleue goddes sayd sette nought hym goddes whan sawe made smyte heed thenne anone stede blode came fayre mylke thenne came aungell bare soule heuen aungelles came bare ye body ayre soo mounte synaye buryed worshyp god werketh many fayre myracles daye fote mounte abbay monkes lyueth grete abstynence abbay hye stronge walled barred aboute yron wylde beestes abbey lyeth saynt katheryn fayre tombe alabaster bone fette th der morshyp aboue chyrche busshe god stode whan spake moyses wrote lawe two table stone busshe grene fayre day also abbey grete meruayle euery monke hath lampe oyle brennynge whan shall deye knowe lampe draweth deth soo derketh lampe whan abbot deyeth bredren shall sy ge masse holy goost burye hym solempnely whan masse doone shall fynde bylle wryten awter shal abbot chese theyr abbot also saynt katheryns nyght al byrdes countree cometh thyder eche bryngeth braunche olyue theyr bylles vyrgyns pryncypall yt thou seest saynt katheryne yt hyd face fro bycause thou hast left thy deuocyon fro euen fastynge man repented hym soone yt done dede torned agayne deuocyon fasted holy man faythe credo deu patrem oipotente creatore celi et terre seconde thynge thou sholdest knowe god ben thartycles faythe whyche grace mercy ben purchaced god eche vertuous dede strengthed fayth artycles folowynge shal shewe fyrst beleue god fader almyghty maker heuen erthe beleue god one beleue god deuyll beleueth god saye yt wordes ben true yet many one fayleth beleue wordes god true say theyr good dedes sholde haue euerlastynge lyfe theyr euyll dedes paynes helle wolde eyther drede loue amende beleue god sayth saynt austyn cleue god loue fulfyllynge wyll beleue thus thou synne agaynst god lacke beleue yet power punysshe yf thou wylte leue seconde et thesu christum filiu eius vnicum dominu nostrum beleue ihesu cryst onely sone lorde vnderstande ihesu cryst sone heuen wt fader without begynnynge fader dooth nothynge without ye sone ne sone without fader thus bothe ben almyghty pthe thyrde qui conceptus est de spiritusancto natus ex maria virgine beleue conceyued holy ghoost borne vyrgyn mary cryst seconde persone holy trynyte dyde take flesshe blode lady holy ghoost without medlynge man beynge mayde fore conceyued hym without synne soo without synne bodely payne chylded hym veray god man pthe fourthe passus sub poncio pylato crucifix mor tuus et sepultus beleue suffred payne vnder ponce pylate done crosse deed buryed cryst sone god suffred mekely trespaced neuer sholde mekeli suffre moche haue trespaced also crucyfyed sholde also chastyse flesshe penaunce withstandynge synne buryed token sholde hyde good dedes fro praysynge vaynglory worlde haue mynde erthe herytage kynde bodely flesshe pthe v descendit ad infernatercia die resurrexit mortuis beleue went doune hell thyrde daye arose frome dethe lyfe cryst thus bodely deed lay sepulcre without ye soule thyrde day arose godhede departed fro body went downe hell delyuered holy soules vertue godhede thyrde daye arose frome dethe lyfe token yt lyght dethe hath dystroyed double dethe shall aryse goostly dethe thre maner medycyns contrycyon confessyon satysfaccyon pthe vi ascendit ad celos sedet dexteram dei patris omnipote ti beleue yt styed vp heuen set hym faders ryght hande thus cryst apperynge dyscyples resureccion dyde ete theym token veray man passyon lo stye heuen hyghed mankynde aboue au gelles openynge heuen gate shewe mankynde way come thyder praye humayne lygnage pthe seuenth inde venturus est iudicare viuos et mortuos byleue come deme quicke dede cryst ihesu god man shal come ye dome deme makynde quyck dede good euyll theyr dedes shal come ye dome demed hethen men syne without law therfore withoute lawe muste perysshe also shall demed dampned fals crysten men yt byleuen iesu cryste withoute loue good werkis shall subgettis accuse theyr euyll curate yt wolde repreue theyr synnes ne teche comaudemetis god also chylderen vnchastysed shalle repreue ther faders moders wold chastyse theym theyr wantonnesse shall poure accuse ryche wolde helpe theyr myschyef amede therfore whyles thou arte haue mynde sodeynly vengaunce falleth fyndeth yt shall deme viii credo spiritu sanctum byleue ye holy goost thyrde persone trynyte holy goost also god wythoute begynnynge endynge euen wytte myghte goodnesse wyth fader sone thre persones ben one god almyghty ix sanctum ecclesiam catholicam sanctorum commumonem byleue holy chyrche comonynge sayntes holy chyrche thrugh oute worlde holy one crysten men sacramentes holy chyrche comoneth gyder therfore forboden chyrche chyrche yerde clamoure stryfe daunsynge drynkynge ony dyshoneste march occasyon synne sholde gyuen foryeuenesse sholde asked holy chyrche parted thre one worlde theym sholde saued mercy god euer fyghtynge ayenst thyse thre enmyens world flessh ye deuyll nother purgatory soules yt abyde grete mercy almyghty god thyrde cryste heuen hede sayntes whiche free frome al maner dyscencyons thyse thre shall one daye dome goyng ihesu theyre hede blysse neuer shall haue ende comonynge sayntes whan eche thyse thre partyes helpen heuen helpen two prayer erthe helpen theym purgatory theyr prayer almesdede thyse two helpen heuen whan theyr ioye blysse encreaced thus eche comoneth wt x remyssionem peccatorum byleue remyssyon synnes ame de theyre lyfe doo penaunce wyllynge leue theyr synnes ende charyte shal haue foryeuenesse theyr synnes cryste dethe passyon fader gate v forgyuenesse also godhede forgyueth orygynal actuall syne theyr baptym pthe xi carnis resurrectionem byleue rysy ge body mankynde daye dome shal ryse fro deth lyfe body soule gyder neuer departed thenne haue ended dedely synne shall goo body soule euerlastynge payne hell withoute mercy haue well lyued ended charyte dedely synne shall wende body soule gyder blysse euermore blysse speketh saynte mathew last artycle xii et vita eterna ame byleue euerlastynge lyfe thyse ben artycles fayth whiche euery man truly sadly byleue maye saued wythoute fayth possyble please god pthyse ben x commau dementis god thyrde thynge thou sholdest knowe god x commaundementis whyche hymselfe wrote two table stoon toke theym moyses shewe people promysynge theym wolde kepe theym blyssynge wel welfare theym wold curse grete sorow myscheue pa asked cryste myght doo haue euerlastynge lyfe answered sayde yf thou wyll entre euerlastynge lyfe kepe commaundementis preue yf thou kepe commaundementis thou fulfylleste lawe god shall haue euerlastyng lyf pthe fyrst commaundeth thou haue god hym ne yu worshyp serue ne gyue thy truste none creature ymage ne thynge grauen hym forboden mawmetry false enchauntementis whitchecrafte false charmes dremes mysbyleues ony man woman hope helpe wythoute almyghty god ye synne dedely sekenesse losse good putte youre fayth byleue ye sholde haue lorde god deuylles mynystres fals witch whiche bryng many soule deuyll pfor byleue wytches worde thenne wordes scrypture preest teched theym pall suche haue goddys curse lest foure tymes yere grete sentence euery daye oure prime ymages palso ye shall vnderstonde clerkys saye theyr bokes sholde lyue sholde lewde men lerne ymages whome sholde worshyp folow lyuynge goddis worshyp ymagis euery man forboden therfore whan thou comest chyrche fyrste beholde goddis body wnder fourme brede aulter thanke hym wouchesauf euery daye come fro holy heue aboue helth thy soule loke thou crosse therby haue mynde passyon suffred thenne thymages holy sayntis byleuynge theym syghte theym thou maye haue mynde ben heuen folowe theyr lyfe moche thou mayste yf thou thus worshyp loue serue god thenne shall worshyp loue serue thou shalte fulfyll fyrste moost commaundement pthe second thou take vayne holy name god pthou takeste name god vayn whan thou torneste ayene synne thy baptym thou takest vayn also whan thou swerest forswerest rekest afore thyng sayth saynt iames swere ye leest ye fall vnder dome god onely reserued god sayth saynt iehan thou swere hym trouth ryghte wysnesse therfore thou swere see thou compellyd dome ryghte enuy loue drede ryghtwysnes declarynge troughte yf ony thyse fayle periury ware therfore ye vse questis consystory hereth peryll ye stonde wyttyngly forsworne boke pthe kook betokeneth holy scrypture suffrayes chyrche whyche thou forsakeste whan thou forswerest thy hondes goodes werkys euer thou dyddest whyche thou forsakest whan thou wythdraweste thou forsakest also god almyghte oure lady saynte marye ye sayntes heuen merytes holy sacrament hooly betakeste thy selfe deuyll helle thou ame de ye thou goost hen yf sholde punysshed thus swerynge shall blaspheme dysmembre hym swerynge herte nayles woundes suche whan ben repreued herof sayne gode haue god mynde suche lewdnesse kepen styll theyr grete othes thy seruaunt dyde agaynst thy byddynge saynge dyde haue yt mynde wolde thou wrothe hym moche must god whan thou doost agaynst ye byddynge saye may well swere swere sothe false excusacon thou sholdest swere alway whan thou sayst sothe wolde cryst haue forboden swerynge moche swerynge oft swerynge therfore sayth moche swereth shall replete wt wyckednes sorowe ne vengeaunce shall departe fro house sayth also noo man wyll beleue theym swere subtyl excusacyon therby false man may swere well true man soo sholde well beleued true man falser swereth forswereth begyleth therfore yf thou wylte beleued without ony swerynge true thy worde lete ye ye nay nay token yu sayst thy mouthe thou sholdest say thy herte saye one thynge thynke pthe thyrde haue mynde halowe thy holy dayes say sondayes boden almighty god vi dayes made heuen erthe see vii daye rested therfore blyssed made holy stede therof crysten men grete deuocyon halow ye sondaye whiche fyrst daye ye worlde wherin god made lyght daye god gaue moyses lawe ye daye rose dethe lyfe daye holy goost gaue wysdome appostles cryste preche declare trouth crystes lawe day also clerkes saye shall also daye dome therfore shall euery woman daye besy hym goddes seruyce lerne lawes fle synne flesshely lustes tauernes suche chaffere letteth theym reste oure lorde yet many folke yt whiche suche dayes besy worldly werkis synnes weke euer wyll rest techynge ne loue ne drede god thyse moste lyke hel neuer reste euer laboure paine breke also holy day yt spende theyr tyme ydelnes vayne playes ydell speche bacbytyng theyr euen crysten sayth lorde haue mynde halow thy holy day yu sholdest put oute thy herte worldly thoughtes occupye heuenly desyres thynke god hath done made yt nought lyke hym soule rausonned ye pyt hell owne precyous herte blood also owne goodnes kepeth ye nyghte daye thy ryght wyttes fro bodely myscheues many one daye fallyth ayenst ye gyuest hym drynke galle bytter synne brekest commaudementis bothe worde thoughte dede thus haue mynde thyse asketh rest body soule holy daye reste sygnyfyeth rest blysse shal haue yf rest hym holy daye flee sy ne iiii worshyp thy fader moder maner faders ben yt thou muste worshyp fyrst ye fader heue made nought nonrryssheth thy body erdly fode comforteth thy soule heuenly desyres defendeth fro deuyll maketh therof blysse heuen thus maye noo man fader lord god seconde fader gate thy moder bare yt whome thou shalte subget seruysable two cause thy enge lyf thenne thou shalt also worshyppe gyue thy goody frely yf haue nede thou haue comforte counseyll teche theym meke maner thy connynge shall please god beware thou obey theym synne yf dede lyue well pray theyre saluacyon lesson sholde euery fader moder bodely gostely teche theyr chyldern iii fader man woma age namely tho vertuous moost specyally thy gostely fader whyche whan yu haste respaced maketh god atte one thy soule passeth thy body thy ghoostely fader passeth ye flesshely thy moder holy chyrche also thou muste buxum wyth thy power mayteyne moder tho euer shall saued thus worshyp obey thou sholdeste thy fader moder sayeth saynt austyne yt thou thus obeyeste theym sayth wyll almyghty god obey prayer fyft thou shalt sle say bodely ne ghostely synne cryeth vengauce afore god wytnesseth olde law new therfore slee man sleeth shall slayn bodely goostely bothe yet yt trespasse openly muste sleyne theym bere temporell swerde brekynge commaundamente ghostely slaughter also many wyse one whan hatest thyne euen crysten consenteste wycked thoughtes thyne owne herte another whan thou lyest bacbytest flatereste synne wylte repreue de fautes also thyself wha thou wyttyngly dooste dedely synne whan thou hast ye goodes ye worlde wylte helpe thy broder nede whan thou defrawdest thy neyghbour also bi false weyghtes mesures paye ge laborer hyere whan thrugh neclygence thyselfe state offyce thou stondest perysshed spylled therfore slee noo man honde tongue ne herte smyteth shall smyten bacbyteth sclaudreth mansleer cursen sayd cursed preuely smyteth cursyth warryeth wylleth vengaunce euen crysten pthe vi commaudement thou shalt lechery cursyd sy ne defouleth body soule al moste pleseth deuyll synnes moost comynly geteth one leest getety ii moo syne god almyghty often hath taken grete vengauce moche worlde drowned saue viii persones alone synne made synke vnto hell fyue cytees sodom pthe deuyl synne tempted many maners fyrste folyly lokynge honeste wordes thenne fowle touchynge kyssyng ye dede syghte fyrste darte thyse lecherous seken therfore ye wymmen araye ye selfe nycely seen folys though ye haue noo wyll synne yourselfe youre nyce araye countenaunce ben cause many soulys dampnacyon whiche ye shall answere atte hygh day dome sayth salomo ye ame de therfore nother countenaunce ne araye stere ye man syne ne haue vysage popped ne pulled crowled nother youre face couloured ne youre hede hye wyde layed costelewe kercheues ne youre body curyous clothynge ne nyce shap counsell saynt poule lete araye shamefastnesse heelyng hedes kerchef couer shame thus sayth saynte poule commaundement breken al tho fleshely luste ben wedded gyder kepynge thorder wedlocke lyue bestys wythout dyscrecyon flesshe moueth hem pand synne seuen husbandes sara strangled wyth deuyll therfore ye wedded ware suche thynges done wherby concepcyon byrthe myghte letted pfor doth wyse wylfully natural kynde asketh synneth moost greuously dedely synne v cause man taketh wyfe one cause generacyon thenne noo synne another cause yeldynge dette thenne synneth rather deserueth mede another eschewynge synne whan incontynent may kepe hym selfe thenne venyall synne sayth saynt austyn another cause fulfyllynge lechery whan man vseth hote mete drynkes medecyn spyces enforceth hymselfe myghtyer fulfyll synne lechery thenne trowe sayth deedly synne fyfth cause whan knoweth agaynst kynde moost deedly therfore yt ben wedded saynt gregory sayth thus study eche please make yt therwith ye dysplease maker vii commaundement yu shalte stele forboden maner wronge takynge withholdynge withdrawynge ony mennes gooddes quycke deed robbynge reuynge sleyghtes dysceytes begylinge byenge sellynge symony vsury extorcyon wt al theyr brauches thus desyre ryche sayth saynt poule fall snare deuyll depe dampnacyon theyr soules prophete sayth also yt falsely purchaceth maketh grete buyldynges wo sayth wronge holde house house felde felde sayth ryght wronge wronge ryght crafty men labourer saynt poule byddeth yt truely theyr laboure wtout slouthe elles theft man witholde labourer hyre cryeth vengeaunce tofore god especyal foloweth vsury whan thou lenest money theym haue nede certayne wynynge tymes ende lendynge thou takest seruyce presentes gyftes another whan thou lenest halfe wynnynge paye hole yu lenest though al lost another whan thou byest thynge moche lesse worthe another whan thou sellest thy chaffere derer leny ge another whan thou hast thynge tofore ye tyme corne rype another whan thou takest beest pore man condycion yf deye shall stande poore man sayth pharysyens therfore vse leful chaffere wyne without subtylte sleyght moche thou mayst yt reasonable thy sustenaunce thyn estate dewe desyred wyse man lorde whan sayd neyther rychesse ne pouerte gyue good lorde necessary lyuelode pthe viii thou shalte bere noo false wytnes forboden maner lesynges conspyracyon forswery ge yt thy neyghboure leseth catell frendshyp good suche ben called chyldoen deuyll put trouthe brynge falsehede put cryst brynge deuyll lesynge standeth onely fals wordes also false werkes yf thou crysten man lyue therafter elles thou lyest thre maner lesynges one whan thou lyest full purpose hurte thy neyghboure thenne deedly synne another whan thou lyest thy neyghboure trouthe thenne moche synne thyrde whan yu lyest dysporte wyllynge hynder ony persone two ben venyall thou haue custome therfore beware maner lesynges another hate ne mede bere false wytnes ix thou shalte desyre thy neyghbours wyfe vii commaundement god forbedeth dede lechery theyr desyre token bothe ben deedly synne yet wene dede synne cryst therfore wyllynge suche clene within without bothe body soule sayth whiche seeth woman couetyse theyr lust lechery theyr herte thus shrewde thoughtes man oftymes departed fro god yet saynt byrgyt vysyons sayeth yf euyl thoughtes sometyme come man sholde wene hy selfe rather aungell man thynge cometh hymselfe none god therfore man sholde knowe infyrmyte hath cometh hym selfe ye strength hath cometh god necessary suffre somtyme grete mercy god tempted wt euyll thoughtes whiche yf consent ben purgacyon soule keper vertues therfore wha shrewde thoughtes come withstande fyrst subgestyon let thy soule alway labour consent delyte thenne haue mynde ye bytter paynes cryst suffred thendles blysse ye ioye heuen thou must lese yf thou consent ye bytter paynes hell also thou shalte haue yf thou deye yf thou thus shalte thou haue de thy laste ende neuer synne pthe x commaundement last thou shalt desyre thy neyghboures thynge house londe oxe horse neyther nothynge desyres couetyse scrypture maketh cion balaam nachor anany gyesy achab iesebell many fell grete myschefe bothe body soule therfore ye well ware suche false desyre take noo mannes good agaynst wyll leest fall dyde thynke also without satysfaccyon hauynge wyll amende therof make restytucyon pope ne none hym may dyspence yet thou standest accursed holy chyrche grete se tence foure tymes yere shall suche false desyres thenne prouffyte whan curse almyghty god shall thus abyde noo man dredeth curse god nowe whan sauyour ihesu cryst shall say daye dome scrypture maketh mencyon go ye cursed fyre hell euerlastynge thenne shall bothe drede fele worde go ye cursed shall paynefull doctours sayeth ye paynes thousande helles though al gadred one x commaundementes ben brought two ye gospell loue god aboue al thynge thy neyghboure thy selfe fyrst thou shalte loue god thy herte thynge nerer thyn herte god thy soule thou suffre synne abyde within thy soule loue god thy mynde yt thou spare myschefe please god thy neyghbour also thy selfe good yeull moche thy selfe helthe sykenes welthe wo thus loue thou shalte kepe goddes commaundement onely drede payne commaundementes sholde eche man tell teche chyldren thus badde lorde moyses wordes sayd whiche take daye shall thy herte thou shal tell thy sone thynke slepynge wakynge syttynge goynge thou shalte bynde sygne thy hande wryte theym doores lanternes thy house shalte rule thy thoughtes wordes dedes preuy aperte eche place commaundemetes god forgete wordes sayd ne falle fro thy herte dayes thy lyfe thus gouerne ye meyny sayth saynt austyn speke thus chyrche soo sholde ye home ye may gyue true rekenynge god theym whiche ben subgectes vnto tell theym sayeth grete loue swetenes heuenly thynges grete bytternes horryble paynes helle ye shall answere theym moost strayte daye dome counseyle theym neclygent wyse lerne commaundementes drede sentence foloweth yf thou wylte voyce thy lorde god saythe thou kepe doo commaundementes curse shall come take thou shalte cursed cyte fylde cursed shall thy relyques fruyte thy boby fruyte londe droues thyne ox flockes sheepe yu shalte cursed goynge goynge oute thou shalte smyte wyth honger sekenes pestylence adres fyre hete corrupte ayre sayth shall pursue thou shalte perysshe yf thou wylte voyse lorde yt thou lerne kepe commaundementes shall make hyer dwellynge erthe blessynges shall come take thou shalte blessed cyte felde fruyte thy body frute londe flockes thy sleep droues thy bestys thy bernys thy celleres thy goynge goynge oute werkes ho dis soo yt euery shall see yt name god called vpo yt shall drede shall gyue ye rayne tyme sayth therth shal brynge forthe sede tree shall replete frute thou shalte haue pea thy coutree thou shalt slepe noo man shall fere thyse blyssyngis shall take yf thou lerne kepe comaundementes therfo haue mynde preceptis god byddynges ye moost besy yf thou kepe shal kepe brynge blysse neuer shall haue ende ame fourth thynge thou sholdest knowe god seuen sacrametis holy chirche whiche mynystred people person prestys haue power therto whyche fyue fyrste baptysme confyrmacyon shryfte howsell anoyntynge euery man woma holde payne cursynge certeyn tyme ye lawe gyueth thother two maye noo take order wedlock owne wyl thyse sacramentis toke theyr begynnynge gracyous welle syde lord ihesu cryst passyon ryght oute adamis syde whyle slept taken rybbe eue made ryght soo deth lord ranne oute syde bothe blood water vertue whiche passyon sacrametis holy chyrche toke fyrste theyr strength theyr begynnynge fyrste sacrament batpty whiche orygynall synne borne synnes defoyled ben wasshen awaye thrugh passyon criste ther betaken v fayth byleue holy chirche wythoute whyche maye noo man saued therfore comaunded euery cryste woman feleth quycke chyld kepe frome heuyng shouynge grete trauayle fallynge myscheues yt sholde myscheue chyldes lyfe soo loste body soule eche woman byfore trauayle chylde come chirche take shryfte housell peryll deth myghte falle byrthe also mydwyf tho yt aboute chylde yf peryll deth sholde crysten wyse crysten name fader sone holy goost thenne sprynge chyld water thou forgete thyse wordes crysten yf crystened maner atte home shall cristened eftsone chirche grete peryll nayle god eftsones vpon crosse yf lyue crystenyng home brynge chyrche shall haue hole seruyce lackethe tyme peryll dethe fader moder maye crysten theyr owne chyldren without harmynge theyr spouschode godfaders godmoders ben borowes tofore god theyr god chylderen therfor ben bounde teche theym loue ryghtwysnes charyte chastyte kepe theym frome deedly synne specyally teche theym commaundementes bylyue man wyfe sholde holde atones chylde fontstoon ne fongyth shall fonge atte confermynge atte nede fader ne moder ne noryse ne none sholde suffre noo yonge chylde theym bedde whyle slepe ne presse theym faste cradell ne suffre theym lye slepynge ne wakynge withoute keper goostly kynrede throughe fongynge chyldern atte fontstoon ix wy one betwene chylde godfader another betwene chylderen godfaders another ye chylde wyfe godfaders fleshely knowen tofore nother betwyx godfader fader hym crystened nother betwix preest chylde baptysed nother betwix chylde chylderen hym baptyseth nother betwix hym baptyseth wyfe hym baptysed fyrste knowe nother bytwene baptyser moder hym baptysed ben also ix afore bysshoppe atte co fermynge forme letten spowsehode made fordooth spowsehode made seconde sacramente confyrmacyon bysshop maner noyntynge forhede hondes bysshop wherby holy goost gyueth strength agaynste feblenes synne forne fader marke impressed soule wherby thou shalte knowlege fayth loue cryste euery crysten man woman bounde brynge theyr chylderen soone may namely yere age shall haue grace lyfe blysse dede confermed mow receyue none sacramente nother shal washe hede forhede thre dayes reuerence holy oyle thyrde sacramente shryfte penaunce ye whiche euery man woman bounde anone resonable wytte atte xii yere euery yere clene shryuen onys atte leest atte theyr owne curate may euery daye see synnes euer dyden thynke vpon whan loke theym may haue shame drede theyr hertes theyr synne thrughe grace god mow leue theyr synne yet notwythstondynge ye ben bounde ouer yere shewe youre shryfte youre owne curate yf ben ony haue affeccyon nother lette wete whome shall haue ryght good leue crystes blyssynge myne deceyte owne soule hyde synne fro entente myghte lenger abyde therein done haue done many yeres knowe theyr counseylle wene wolde dyde suche lyke thadder yt hydeth venyme preuy place wolde engender lamprey tourneth taketh vp ayene thus one yere ye come youre curate ye caste oute venym youre synne atte pardon preuy place anone eester ye take vp ayen thefte auoutry suche ben worse ye afore ye done begyle selfe nede grete penaunce iudas wha betrayed cryst tolde synne true herdman dyd cayphas pylate wha sayd haue syned body betrayenge ryghtwyse blode hadde saued toke none hede therto sayd yt v auyse sayth haue cure ryght soo thus trowe went owne herdeman wha ye go thenne sholde brybery stolen goodes suche restored auoutry cursed synnes thus dystroyed say desyre haue shryft payne saue charge haue soules leuer mynyster al sacramentes yt longeth myn offyce forty tymes one doo dystroye false subtylte yt ye vse shryfte agaynst helthe soules god helpe also whan thou comest shryft thou shalt come grete sorowe herte mekely knele preest hym goddes stede tell hym holy yu hast mysgouerned thy lyfe full wyll hertely thy penaunce enioyned therfore e le shryfte many set nought theyr penaunce doynge haue tolde theyr syne preest suche begyle themselfe veray sacrament shryfte dependeth specyally thre thynges wtout whiche thou mayst truely shryuen yt sorowe herte shryft mouthe penauce doynge though thou sorye thy synne shryue auayleth seth ne thy penaunce auayleth wyte wel thou mayste yf thou sholdest reken man ende thy rekenynge thoughe thou xx lib det ryght thou shryuest makest rekenynge wt preest goddes stede thou make seeth therfore paye thy det penauce doynge nought token thou arte sory thy synne yf thou sory therfore haue sayd tofore thy shryft nought thou synnest agaynst holy goost whiche ye moost peryllous synne therfore yf thou wylte haue blysse heuen thy penaunce thenne thou shalte haue grace pardon thy synnes thre wordes contrycion confessyon sarysfaccyon standeth vertue pardon worlde lady saynt mary vysyons holy woman saynt byrgyt telleth whan pardon prouffyteth whan saynge yt cometh pardon hath wyll leue synne restore hath wrongfully taken wyllynge syght god sayth vysyteth remyssyon pardon synnes hath wyll leue olde vanytees ne ye inordynate affeccyon kepeth styll wronge getynges false deceyte subtyltees also loueth world hym selfe wyll flee shrewde customes ne restrenyne flesshe superfluytees ryght nought auayleth hym pardon ne indulgence accordeth saynt gregory sayth thus thou makest neuer satysfaccyon thy synne sayth yf thou feere thy synne euery body wyll desyre pardon fewe none wyll sholde haue pardon thrugh trust coloure pardon many cursed dede doo synne trust therof ony good deed grete synne pryde yu neuer full good vertues ghoost sowne hole speche thus sayth ye holy man saynt bernarde preestes muste also euery daye dyspose theym say masse yf may therto bound sayt bernard sayth persone lorde euery man th haue made gyue power make offre sone incarnate tofore ye fader saluacyon world yf thou haue power synge syngeste saythe thou benymeste aungellys heue theyr ioye thou benymest mankynde trauaylyge erth theyr helpe wytnesse v preestis pthe seuenth sacramente wedlocke whiche baynes muste asked thryes holy chyrche pthis lawfull knyttynge togyder man woman fourme holy chyrche assent theym gyder lawe god neuer departe whyles theyr lyues lasten remyssyon synnes getynge grace whan taken true entent thoughe noo trouthe plyght flesshely dede done yf ben full age accorde hertes gyder fore god wyfe husbonde pall gyue asketh better correccyon iherom sayth gyue poore sustayne theyr ryches may man excuse hym almesse gyuynge halfpeny poore somtyme pleaseth god hondred shelynges ryche yf yu may gyue hym gyue hym chastyse hym trespaceth saye repreue bete doo due correccyon pthe fourthe comforte sorowfull gyftes wordes comforte suche fyfth forgyue trespace yf thou wylt forgyue god wyll forgyue rancour offence thou must nedes forgyue accyon ye amendes ben thyn owne wyll syxte thou suffre mekely pacyently whan ony man woman ony preiudyce offence agaynst prompte redy synne feruent doo penaunce good werkes operacyons moore preste redy suffre dysease trybulacyon doo yf ony man chyde blame repreue doo wronge kepe scylence set sharpe worde ye shylde suffraunce thynke moost benygne sauyiour redemptoure payeng dewte eche thynge dewly longeth god praysynge thankynge goodes kynde fortune grace hath gyue lente therof gyue parte many benefaytes preseruynge frome many myscheues vengaunce thou haddest fall daye seest many one fall sholdeste happely thyselfe haue fall gracyous kepynge haue pto thy neyghboure thou muste also yelde loue charyte saye thou doo ryghte reason hym thynge thou woldeste dyde yf thou woldest sholde true paye dettys begyle subtyltees sleyghtes byenge selyng yf thou woldest also proude enuyous whrathfull couetyse glotenous slouthfull ne let cherous thou thus thynges thou woldeste thy neyghboure thou hym thenne thou doost ryghtwysnesse thyself also thou muste haue besynes lerne fulfyll wyll commaundementis god withstonde synne shrewde lyuynge pthe fyfth vertue wysdome vertue departeth good frome euyll techeth v beware sleytes deceytes wretched worlde lykewyse freyle flesshe cursed ennemye deuyll helle pand dyspyse set noughte alle may ii good chose better saynt austyn sayth many one dothe thou must dyspyse ye worlde hate flesshe louers worlde lytell whyle ago v thynge lefte theym powder wormes take hede ben nowe men thou arte sayth dranke laughed ladde theyr lyfe erthe myrthe iolyte poynte descende helle profyteteth theym theyr vayne glorye theyr shorte ioye pompe worlde dylycates luste flesshe false rychesse grete meany euyll couetyse theyr laughter theyr playe theyr pryde theyr boost pafter luste grete payne sorowe fylle theym maye falle sayth thou arte man erthe erthe thou lyuest erthe thou shalte tourne agayne ben ye wordes holy doctoure saynt austyne remembraunce shall make wyse hardy dispyse youre enemyes worlde flesshe deuyll saynt isyder sayth none thynge better thenne wysdome ne none thynge sweter lustyer thenne knowlege ne none thynge worse thenne lewdnesse therfore knowe thou thou shalte flee wheder yu shalt go ploue wysdome shewed shall come besy aboute shall lerne vi vertue strengthe maketh myghty hardy wythstonde many grete pthat none worse dampnable synne synne pryde ben gyltye lyste repreued theyr synnes ne theyr defautes anone wyth greate stourdynes galled horse touched sore wyncheth wryeth pand seken may mayntene lord haue synned sayth sory synne wyll amende therfore god toke awaye moche vengaunce shold haue synne ryghte thus shold ye repreued youre synne mekely come curate minister god occupyeth stede tyme felysshyp rose agaynst moyses aaron greate pryde therfore erthe openede swalowede theym alle quycke downe hell palso people nynyue theyr greate boldenesse pryde hadde theyr hertes tourne ayene theyr synnes hondred score thousande people byble reherseth sheweth destroyed dodely enmyes therfore euery man beware synne wysely loke myroure mekenes techeth hym shall pfyrst consyder thou made foule stynkyne slyme fylthe synne lechery borne thy moder wyth grete sorow payne norysshed greate labour anger kepte greate drede thou arte sacke foule dunge swetenes fruyte cometh tree leues cometh floures frute lycenettes fleen herbes also cometh ryght swete odoryferous smel lykewyse aboue lyke semblable maner wyse beneth partyes stynkynge fylthe ende thou shalte wormes mete torne agayne erthe tyll daye dome thy body soule shall ryse agayne day sayth malachy shall brenne hote ony furneys fyre prowde men stoble whiche shall brent yt shall neyther rote rynde therfore sayth isyd mekenes make thy sadde vysage hygh worshyp haue grete mekenes hygher yu art meker thou sholdest make thy self thynke souerayne lorde ihesu meked hym dethe thy sake mekenes vtter remedy agaynst pryde sanatyf salue agaynst myscheues synne maketh haue mynde thy shorte abydynge strayte dome thou shall come mekenes yt thou sholdest haue pthe seconde synne enuy whan thou arte sory thy neyghbours welfare ioyest euyll fare wycked synne come many braunches one hatred whan thou art lothe speke spoken ony thyge whiche myght torne thy neyghboure good prouffyte another false demenyge dedes agaynst thy neyghbour pthe thyrde backebytynge speke euyll behynde thy neyghboure whiche thou mayst ne wyll auowe afore hym though thou speke euyl thy selfe yu hastly kynge grete delectacyon euyll spekynge hym soo doynge thou synnest deedly onely whiche speketh euyll neyghboure alsoo yt whiche wyll gladly suche euyll spekynge defaute synne soo yf berer noo bacbytynge ne bacbyter therfore sayth isyder gladde falle euyll fare thy neyghboure leest god tourne wrathe frome hym soo thou sholdest falle worse glad sorowe desesed euermore mourne myscheef yu woldeste thy owne loue pea outwarde warde pea men make pea hate flee chydynge beware awaye thoccasyon stryfe lyue alway pea lete noo thynge passe thy lyppes maye defoyle ye eeres herers vayne wordes take vayne coscience suche worde suche soule therfore besy speke lyketh nedeth take hede thou spekest spekynge spekynge ryght wel ware thou mayst call ayene thou hast sayde putte fro thy tonge synne bacbytynge defoyle thy mouth nother manys synne sory hym thou bacbyteste nother drede thyselfe whan thou blamest nother thynke thyne owne synne loke mennys thou shalte neuer bacbyte yf thou wylte beholde thy selfe therfore ne lysten none suche tytelers ben lyke gylty heter bacbyter desyre wyt perteyneth yt aske neuer ony man dothe spekyth sayth leue besynes perteyneth greate besynes amende thy synne moche thou beholdest mennys sor man knoweth whether worthy hate mede saye payne ioye many one semeth v ryghte good yet ayenst god happely ryghte noughte many one also semeth v ryghe nought yet ben hym ryght dere therfore man deme put iugemente estymacyon god thus charyte knyt vertues thou muste destroye foule synne enuye pthus charyte stondethe loue god loue thy neyghboure whyche twoo lawe god abydeth one maye loued without yf thou loue god thou wylte haue none hym ne thou wylte take hys name vayne ne breke thy holy sondayes yf thou loue thy lorde god also thy neyghbours thou wylte noo manslaughter ne thefte ne false wytnesse bere ne letchery ne desyre thy neyghbours wyfe ne gode charyte fulfyllynge goddis loue thendynge good werkys charyte pacyente benygne hath none enuye wertcheth shrewednes loueth pryde coueyteth noo worldly worshyppes seketh noo propre goodes wroth thynketh none euyll ioyed wyckednes trouth taketh thynge mekely byleueth god sayth hopeth blysse suffred harmes neuer dyscomfyted thorugh goddis helpe abyde longe falleth neuer downe world ne kepeth man byleue maketh hym stable vnder hym wexith obedyence pacience ouer cometh al wronges without hym man pleaseth god hym man peryssheth ptherfore ayenste enuy seke charyte wyth grete studye thou mayst haue thy lyuynge dwell parfyghtly ther thyne endynge amen pthe thyrde synne wrath whyche wycked styrynge mannys herte wherby wyll auenge hymselfe vp euyn crysten cometh many shrewde spyces fyghtynge chydynge hurtynge betynge grutchyng warryng cursynge cruellys man slaughter desyrynge vengaunce pthere ben also foure specyall one wha thou art soon moued soone swaged easy another whan thou art soon swaged shrewde pthe thyrde whan thou arte soon meued soone swaged perylous pthe fourth longe thou meued soone swaged moost easy therfore ayenste thyse braunches thou muste arme vertue pacyece thynke sorowe myghte falle thy wordes dedes thenne put crystes passyon paynes betwene suche paynes myghte suffre shall thy wrath soone slake pin foure thynges spyrytuelly necessary haue pacyence one ayene thyne enemye cruell thou nedest pacyence softe speche slaketh wrathe ptherfore yf ony aduersyte falleth suffre pacyently whether thou haue deserued yf thou haue deserued thou arte worthy yf thou haue thou hast thy rewarde cryst wha sayth blesed ben pacyente shall called chyldren god panother wha thy souerayne correcteth thy defautes thou muste pacyente drawe thy horne pryde snayle whan towched dyde adam voys oure lorde pthe thyrde losse thy good iob whan good gone mekely sayde oure lorde gaaf lorde hath take lyke hym done name blessed pthe pouerte nother sekenesse thou sholdest flee frome hym therfore pacyente grutche ayenst scourge lorde ihesu cryst also lykewyse ferthermore thou grudgest thou styrest god agaynst sayth saynt isyder pthe fourthe synne couetyse yt whiche wronge desyre yt man hath haue ony thynge hath ryght therto stondeth two thynges pry cypally one whan thou wrongfully purchasest getest ony maner thynge sacrylege symony stelthe vsury ony maner falshede gyle worldly men vse whiche caste theyr besynes couetyse yt ne recke come good synne gylty money worldly wynnynge vse playe dyce table whiche vtterly forboden holy chyrche many synnes cometh therof fyrste couetyse yt thou hast wynne dyspoyle thy felawe another grete vsury xii ix double quyte thirde encrease godes lesynge many vayne wordes ben vsed grete dyspyte god faythe fourthe euyll ensample thou gyuest yt beholde fyfth lesyng tyme whiche yu myght haue done many good werkes syxte dyspyte dysobedience thou doost thy moder holy chyrche forbyddeth suche playe vii fraude deceyte yt yu doost also thy felawe play viii cursed wrathe stryfe cometh therof wherby ofte thou renyest thy god lesest thy kyndly wytte ix brekyng thy holy daye tho dayes moche vsed excercysed tenthe manslaughter whiche ofte happeneth dame enleuenth ydolatry thou co mysen thou makest agaynst dyse token aboue vnto myghty god mycheues many mo mysfortunes cometh sory playe thou getest wynnest forsayd playe besynesse thou hast hadde therwith thou mayst reioyce nedes thou must gyue dystrybute vnto poore nedy yf thou haue hym thou makest playe strength agaynst wyll thou arte bounde restore hy agayne whiche hath lost playe also thou brekest commaundementes god whyder thou wyne lese thyn harme thou lese thou lesest god heuen yf thou wynne yu wynnest deuyll hell lawe canon sayth preest deken yt gyueth dyce dronkenes yf leue certaynly da pned subdeken clerke lewde man yt vse muste eyther leue lacke theyr howsell therfore euery man beware playe suffre wyse done may lette consente therto fauoure ony wyse ben grete peryll doer seconde poynte wronge withholdynge whiche yu fallest ofte thou doost god almyghty thy neyghboure holy chyrche thy dutees thou sholdest dutye goddes lawe wylfully wtholdest theym onely wrongfully geteth also wrongfully withholdeth ben deedly syne synne spryngeth many shrewde braunches mawmetry ambycyon nygardshyp treason vsury symony raueyne theft sacrylege suche pthese synnes ben cursed sayd tofore thynge contraryeth wyll commaundement god fyrst commaundement contraryeth whan thou withdraweth fro god ony thynge thou sholdest worshyp hym seconde also whan lytell wynnynge thou takest name vayne thyrde whan worldly besynesse getynge money thou brekest thyn holy daye fourthe whan couetyse auaryce thou withdrawest takest fro whan couetyse yu steleste thy neyghboures good pthe viii whan questes also consystoryes thou forswerest bereste false wytnesse pthe ix ten whan thou desyreste falsely thy neyghboures wyfe ony good
