deuyll couetysehe gytueth foure commaundementes seruauntes one thou kepe well thyne owne another thou gyue ne doo noo almesse thyrde thou lene poore drede lesynge pthe fourthe thou withdrawe thy meany frome mete drynke spare thy good foure shrewde commaundementes eche man beware flee suche couetyse desyre good salomon dyde desyred none rychesse pouerte nedefull lyuelode accordynge estate thynke thoughe thou haue neuer soo moche thou shalte leue naked thou cameste worlde agayne naked saue ragge thou shalte goo oute therto thus care thou hast olde shete atte thy goynge hen fyfte synne glotony whiche vnskylfull lykynge loue yt man hath taste takynge mete drynke erly late yf sekenesse grete nede excuse synne spryngen foure braunches one whan thou eteste drynkest gredly falle fastynge dayes wyll abyde houre noone sytte lenger atte mete ete tyme nother often tymes quenche theyr hunger breed spyces ouermoche drynke drede hu ger thus breke vygyles ymberdayes frydayes lente suche another whan thou castest lyue delytes pleasure passynge thyn estate haste noo ioye whan thou mayst speke suche welfare thynkynge best beset thou doost spende theron thou mayst well vse suche dayntye mete drynkes synne sayth saynt gregory synne neyther mete ne drynke appetyte talent thou delytest moche therin pthe thyrde surfet whan thou pomperest thy body moche mete drynke thou mayst broke lesest thy syght speche wytte iangelynge bostynge wenynge saye well ryght sayth agaynst reason ordre fall whiche maketh ryot rere soupers destroye vytayle whiche many poore man myght releued susteyned pthe fourthe curyosyte yt whan thou canst holde apayde easy fare gadrest many curyous mete encrease thyn appetyte quenche thyn hongre fall whiche waste theyr goodes desolute etynge drynkynge grete feestes bankettes makynge agaynst cursed braunches thou must kepe abstynence mete drynkes nothynge dryueth away sekenesses ne dystroyeth lust flesshe dooth mesurable takynge mete drynke fyue maner folke ben excused fastynge say woman chylde labourer pylgrymes yonge chyldren olde folke seke people al synneth ete twyes daye mesurable sustayne nature theyr appetyte pthere dyuers abstynences fastynges dyuers maner persones pthe seke man absteyneth withholdeth hym fro mete drynke may ete drynke medycyne nedy hath wherof couetous wolde spende gloton ete ypocryte beholde holy vertuous man deserue mede absteyneth hym bothe frome excesse mete luste synne thus sholde eche man kepe hys power techeth saynte poule whan saythe praye straungeres pylgrymes ye absteyne frome flesshely desyres fyghte ayenste thy soule also destroye thy bodye pthyse myscheues comen glotony engendrethe sore brynge sekenes destroyeth vertues dulleth wytte hasteth deth worse maketh lyke beste fuller thy body emptyer thy soule vertue therfore vse vertue sayth sayte austyne thyse vertues shal folowe pabstynence saueth thy mynde sharpeth thy wytte clenseth thy syghte maketh holy thy fame swageth thy synne maketh stronge thy blode norysheeth thy mary destroyth lechery renneth thy bloode lengtheth thyn age pthe vi synne slouthe greuaunce anoy gostely dedes one spryngen many shrewde braunches one drawe longe tary goode dedes thou sholdeste whiche myghte torne helthe thy soule many panother dulnesse heuenesse herte letteth loue god maketh thou haste lykynge goddis seruyce though thou praye thy herte thero thyrde ydelnesse whiche moche vsed letteth v begynne ony good werkis lyghtely maketh v leue whan begynne pand made kynde trauayle synne sloughthe holdeth v ydelnesse ease agaynst oure kynde therfore thou wylt saued thou must flee ydelnesse enmye chrysten soules stepmoder goodnesse alle vertues key vyces alwaye doo good werkis sayth sayt iherome occupyed lyghtly take temptacyon syethe hym aboute salomon sayth mooste foole loueth ydelnesse heuen shall receyued ordeyned theym haue besyed theym vertue erthly paradyse shall neuer neuer mannes laboure ne purgatory shalle scourged men helle deuylles shall neuer haue reste therfore besy vertue alwaye thynke noo thynge maketh man soo soone enclyne synne ydelnesse pthe seuenth synne lecherye flesshely synne cometh luste lykynge flesshe poute thys spryngen many braunches one fornycacyon dedely synne done flesshely bytwene syngell man syngell woma agaynst lawe god techynge holy chyrche ptherfore holy chyrche byddeth noo man chylde ne woman chylde passen seuen yere age lye gyder bedde drede fornycacyon ne syster ne brother drede inceste panother called auoutrye spowsebrekynge whether doone bodely goostely gretter synne mysheues therin thou dooste sacrelege saye thou brekeste sacrament wedlocke wher comen ofte vnryghtful heyres fals maryages pthis synne dowbleth ofte tymes whan done man maryed woman maryed one thyse foure myscheues folowes theym customably vse synne one pouerte another lesynge membre thyrde perpetuell pryson pthe fourthe sodeyn deth fayleth hardely yf custumably vsed sayd tofore panother incest thy kynne thyne affynyte pa nother whan thou mysusest thyne wyfe dooste ayenste kynde order maryage thou mayste slee thyself thyn owne swerde ryghte thou mayste thyne owne wyfe synne onam iacobus cosyn smyten deth seuen husbondes sara also pthis sacramente sholde done vsed honestely grete reuerence panother whan man synneth wyth kynde wyfe contrary ryghte perylous maye wedde none kynne yf doo maryage noughte worse maye knowe wyfe noo warde infourme wedlocke without dedely synne requyred panother moste stynkynge whyche synne ayenste kynde deuyll techeth man woma dyuersytees syne abhomynable named oonly shryfte theym falle therein pfor gretter horryble synne auayleth thy shryft shame tellynge greate parte thy penaunce pthis soo dyspleasynge god made reyne brymstone fyre destroyed fyue cytees sodome gomere deuyll himselfe causeth synne hath shame dede pthyse many flesshely synnes whiche ben dedely eueryche werse othere comen oute fowle synne lechery whiche well knowen theym lyuen luste theyre flesshe therfore flee occasyons sayth saynte poule saye syghte wymmen kyssynge touchynge suche pthis wyse scaped ioseph synne lady whan lefte palle mantel ranne awaye thynke also vpon fynyshement ende lykewyse nyghe dredefull streyte dome whiche thou shalte come vnto horryble inestymable paynes also tourmentes whiche perfounde depnes helle made redy suche horryble synnes loke thou presume thyself maner wyse noble kynge dauyd wyse kynge salamon sone stronge sampson ouercomen vnhappy synne also maner wyse also speke lecherous wordes thy herte mynde loue holy scrypture draweth man moche therefor vse also prayer fastynge good lawfull occupacyons wythdrawe frome superfluitees excesse hote mete drynkes yf thou lyue thy flesshe thou shalt dede sayth scrypture saye dampned vnto euer lastynge payne helle ptherfore shytte gate thy body thy soule fro thyse myscheues synne saye thy fyue wyttes bodely goostly consente hym pfyrste thyne eyen shrewde lewd thynges bac bytyge euyll wordes couceyles thy mouth frome vnlawful taste glotony lewd kyssyges rybawdry wordes thyhodes frome lewd towchyge thyselfe fro stelthe takyge menes goodes agayst wyll thy foot also frome pathes synne wretched wayes thou myghtest drawe pthese ben bodely wyttes pthan take thy ghoostly wyttes mynde vnderstondynge reason ymagynacyon saye haue mynde kyndenesse god thy laste ende thou shalte neuer synne ye shal vnderstonde also crystes loore techynge lete euer thy wyll redy worshyppe hym thoughte worde dede without ony werynes lete reason also rule thy dedes inwarde outwarde crystes loore tehynge withouten oony deceyte blyndenesse thy owne selfe pand alwaye haue ymagynacyon vertuous lyuynge nedefull werkes dredefull dedes ioye blysse ordeyned heuen theym leue theyr synne shall saued horryble paynes sorowes shall suffre endlesly whiche theyr synnes shall dampned dongeon helle whiche ben ix maner horryble hydeous paynes nyne maner people shall tourmented clerkes sayeth pthe fyrste fyre euer brenneth neuer gyueth lyght whiche thoughal ye water see cast sholde queche fyre passeth fyre paynted dooth fyre passe oures fyre shall euer brenne alway brenned fyre false couetyse pthe seconde passynge colde yf grete hylle fyre casten therin sholde torne yse shall tourmented ben colde loue malyce fende pthe thyrde payne wormes horryble serpentes dragon neuer shall deye lyue fyre fysshes dooth water shall gnawen gnawe theym selfe venymous hate theyr euen crysten pthe fourthe abhomynable stynke wherin shall lapped delyteth theym foule stynke synne lechery pthe fyfth shal betynge myghty fendes hamers yren wherwith shall payned beten without seasynge wolde chastysed ye techynge goddes wordes pthe syxte payn derkenes whiche tenebrous thycke myght felt hande horryble derkenes shall bounde lyueth present worlde derkenesse foresayd synne wyll come cryst whiche veray lyght holy lyuynge leuynge synne whyles myght pthe seuenth payne open shenshyppe shame synne whiche shall apertly knowen hydde paynfull reprefe synfull folke specyally wyll knowlege theyr synne god due maner ne ashamed hym shal ful herde tourment pthe eyght horryble syght deuylles rorynge cryenge ferefull sorowfull voyce wherwith thus shall payned toke none hede holy ensamples good dedes ne prechynge techynge goddes wordes byddynges pthe nynthe fyry bondes wherwith shall bounde honde fote membres spendeth theyr membres lymmes ye deuylles seruyce lust lykynge theyr bodyes pthese nyne paynes shall synfull suffre forsoke left vnwysely felawshyp nyne ordres aungellys theyr synfull lyuynge amende goo hen therfore sory thy synne amende whyles thou arte thou mayst escape horryble paynes reygne oure lorde ihesu cryst hyghe blysse heuen euer myrthe trauayle fredome bondage helthe longe sekenes rest trauayle lyfe deth perfyte loue without drede euer daye without nyght thou shalte haue seuen ioyes thy body seuen thy soule thy body fayrenes swetenes strengthe luste helthe mortalyte thy soule wysdome frendshyppe accorde power worshyppe surety ioye without ende whiche brynge v v deyed rode ihesu cryst goddes sone amen sondaye last enfourmed homely wyse worthynes mannes soule whan synne synne defowleth thy soule sacrament penaunce also salue sanatyfe al maner sore synnes whan dyscretly vsed pnow ye leue god shall declare thre partes penau ce contrycyon confessyon satysfaccyon ye fulfyllynge soules thus haue ben wounded synne may refourmed brought agayne grace pfyrst contrycyon sayd cut hertes clothes confessyon also sheweth hertes afore preest open speche mouthe satysfaccyon ye worthy fruytes penaunce thus thre thynges hooly sacrament penaunce preued confessyon also sayd sawter haue trauayled sorowes shall make moyst bedde euery nyght teres sayth haue trauayled make satysfaccyon synnes sorow myn herte hauynge mynde longe haue lyued haue spet tyme goodnes haue left vndone moche euyll haue done synne haue lost ye felawshyp heuen ioyned felawshyppe fendes also vale teres full wretchednes byrthe brought forthe vnto mannes synes sorowes shall come vnto dredefull dome gyue rekenynge leest moost syne eue dyde worde dede thought knowynge wheder shall worthy hate mede wolde also blysse whiche may come without grete tourment trybulacyon sorowe pthese consyderynge thyn eres werkes thou shall well knowe perceyue thou arte cause thyn owne sorow myschaunce soo shame thou shalte fall contrycyon wynne grace mercy moost mercyfull lorde god ryghte harde endurced herte sayth saynt bernarde neyther benefaytes almyghty god may grynde molyfye ne horryble paynes helle may feere ne ioyes heuen may susteyne ne temporall tourmentes ne sorow may chastyse many one contryte knowe contrycyon ptherfore ye shall vnderstande contrycyon inwarde sorowe thy soule fourmed grace whiche cometh forthynkynge synne drede hyghe iugement stedfast purpose confessed doo satysfaccyon commaundement chyrche also conuersyon thyn herte euyll goodnesse frome deuyll god frome vyce vertue pthere many haue contrycyon perfyte wha thy herte touched handes god inspyracyon make perfyte sorowfull somwhat lesse moche thou begynnest tourne called attrycyon whan wyl desyre synne euery parte fully forsaken full sorowe herte thenne contrycion veray contrycyon serche synne porygen sayth also verey contrycyon abhorre loth gaye superfluous araye desyre hygher wepynge fle slaughter speke fewe wordes werke ryghtfully euer haue drede inwarde sorowe thyn herte thy synnes thou louest thynge thy sorowe whan thou doostle se paboue creature god loued thenne moost sorowe losse creature wha yu commyttest deedly synne thenne thou lesest thy god therore grete contrycyon sorow thou must gete hym agayne loke moch thou hast grace sayth saynt gregory moche thou must haue sorowe thy synnes pthe soules blysse may haue contrycyon cause theyr ioyes ben replete wyth plenteuousnes glory ben hell maketh sorowe sorowe fourmede grace pthe soules purgatorye hathe sorowe fourmed wyth grace yet merytory moche sholde haue hadde thus lyfe mercy oonly helpeth blamefully herde saythe saynt iherome wepe deth frende harme temporel loo wepe sory synne thy contrycyon therfore muste sharpe thou hast offended thy heuenly fader bodely goostly fedyth many wy yet muste thou sharp thou haste offendede thy lorde ihesu goddis sone heuen precyous blood hys mercy delyuered frome bondes synne crueltee offendes byternes paynes hell though lorde sayde euery man sayth lord lord shall entre kyngdom heuen yet leue hym haue hym tauerne contrycyon saye hym dauyd dyde meke contryte herte lorde thou shalte dyspyse pand shall gyue grace ioye whan thou goost hen fawcon whan hath taken praye desyreth therof herte cotence lorde ihesu whan raunsoned v helle desyreth noo meke contryte herte v therfore fauconer wyll gyue herte fawcon fyrst wyll kytte thenne take blood wasshe muste thou gyue thy herte oure lorde fyrste kytte wyth knyf contrycyon pand thenne take blood synne confessyon wasshe satyssfaccyon knyfe passyo kytte hertes clothes hauynge mynde blaade knyfe made spere hede nayles precyous body herte thrylled withalle hafte made holy tre crosse vyrell made crowne thorne aboute hede whette knyfe blessed body soo harde cruelly tourmentede crosse lefte noo hole ioynte make also shethe thy knyfe whyte skynne lorde ihesu cryst paynted reed blody woundes soo many toppe heed vnto sole ye fote hole place hym left vnscourged wt cordes bounde pyler de knyfe gyrdle thy herte doubte thy herte neuer harde thou faythfully pryte thy mynde passyon thy harde herte wyll begynne breke thus mayst thou lerne suffre repreues oure lorde ihesu whiche suffred many pthere ben vi thynges sholde stere grete sorowe thy synnes pthe fyrst somtyme ye daye nyght sayd bethynke thou hast lyued whan thy synnes come thy mynde haue inwarde sorowe remorse thou hast greuously offe ded thy god thy maker redemptoure pthe seconde thou ashamed thy synne elles daye dome shall shewed worlde ope ly vnto thy grete shame confusyon thyrde yu haue grete obhomynacyon fylth synnes thou hast thus comysed bothe syght god man seneca sayth though wyst yt sone sholde vnknowen bothe god man yet wolde abhorre lothe fylthe synne fourthe thou haue drede daye dome paynes hell day speketh saynt peter vnneth ryghtwyse man ye daye shall saued sayth shall thenne synnefull man aperethe whiche breketh dayly hestes preceptes lorde often many tymes beholde ye daye sayth saynt iherome quake herte whyder ete drynke elles ony thynges euer thynke trompe god sowneth myn eeres byddeth synnefull wretche aryse come dome fyfth thou haue sorowe losse heuen grete offence doone thy maker syxte thou haue thre folde hope fyrst forgyuenes thy synnes ben alone forgyuen hope also grace good werkes alwayes encrease thenne hope blysse wherwith thou mayst afterwarde rewarded thy good werkes prophete sayd yt sholde wasshe euery nyght bedde teeres semeth ye cotrycyon forgyuenes sholde cotynuall knowe harde yet thy wyl thou mayst haue contynuall contrycyon euer full purpose leue lothe thy synne thus nedefull confessoure knewe suche one cometh contynually beynge sory inwarde outwarde nedeth neuer gyue hym lytell penaunce though doone grete horryble syne myght venge bewayle synnes dethe sholde payne suffre purgatory yet sorowe must mesurable trusty hope thou falle heuynes dyspayre must also generall hole synes yet sharper one gretenes must doone offence done god onely drede euerlastynge payne maner contrycyon breketh snare chaynes deuyll releaseth bondes oblygacyons euerlastynge payne tourment delyuereth frome seruage horryble company deuylles maketh chylde almyghty god heyre blysse heuen whiche tofore chyldren deuyll brennynge bronde perfounde pyt hell onely contrycyon also auayleth confessyon satysfaccon may hadde offende god thre maner wyse herte speche dede soo nedeth satysfaccyon thre maners elles synne forgyuen onely contrycion may auayle also whan thou arte contryte purposest afterwarde abstayne maner syne knowlegest thy synne soone thou mayst doost also due satysfaccyon dome chyrche moost sure way pthe seconde wasshynge confessyon doone thy mouthe ryght soule wasshen made whyte sowkynge sorowe also wt salte fretynge teres thyn eyen soo lowly confessyon thy mouthe thou muste rubbe thy foule spottes synne rusted thy soule maner wasshynge speketh prophete dauyd sayenge thus thou shalte sprynge lorde ysope shall clensed thou shalte wasshe shall made clene whyte snowe ryght lowely confessyon doone thy mouthe thy curate purgeth maketh whyte thy soule ony snowe worlde se therfore confessyon confessyon doctours scyence lawfull declaracyon synne tofore done thynge wherby preuy goostly sore sykenes opened wt hope forgyuenes pthre maner co fessyons ben one warde thy soule thou madest knowen god seconde tofore iuge hope forgyuenes god thyrde tofore goddes vycarye preuy synne pryuely opened pof speketh scypture sayd tell openly yf thou haue ony thynge saye shewe thou mayst therby iustyfyed pthe grete flagellacyon payne passyon oure sauyoure redemptoure grete remedy ayenst synne orygynall actuall pthe vertue wherof expressyd sacramente holy chyrche withoute whiche may man hole therfore confessyon nedefull preuythe scrypture saynge thus proude wyll obeye precept preest shall dede haue also lorde fader heue euery man woman hauynge yeres dyscressyon bounde one parsone make confessyon onys yere sy ne owne curate also nedefull reason preueth wyse thou haddest trespaced thy neyghboure ryghtful thou sholdeste sette thyne owne payne atte thy lust ne hath wronge neyther meane coude myghte set resonably wronge declared pthe prest ordeyned meane sette thy paynes wronge thou haste done thy god thy synne nedeth thenne thou shewe truly thy trespace vnto hym maye set suche penaunce wherby thou mayste able come presence thy lorde god palso euery dome resonable muste iuge persone gylty ye preue must preues elles wytnes ayenst thy wyll wylfull knowlege syth dome penaunce fre ayenst thy wyll cause thou goost therto wylfully thenne shalle processe dome promyse ne wytnesse freely thy propre confessyon pand muste iuge may forgyue condempne god oonly releseth synnes pand soo tyll toke mankynde confessyon herte suffysed requyred asked confessyon vocyall whiche made man man moche wyth v fourme therfore ordeyneth men vycaryes thou sholdeste confesse whome gaaf power bynde vnbynde thus confessyon nedefull reason promyse holy scrypture oure lorde gaue power preest bynde vnbynde whan sayd whoos synes ye forgyue ben forgyue whose synnes ye wythholde ben wythholde yet power vertue god loseth power god cryst sayth saynt austyne v crucyfyed whiche man none synnes forgyuen ptherfore oure lorde gaaf openly holy gooste men gyuynge vnderstondynge synnes forgyuen thorugh merytes men thorugh goodnesse holy goost whan arose deth sayde dyscyples take holy goost whose synnes ye forgyuen sayth spyryte god forgyueth ye soo maye forgyue may forgyue without man sacrament grace sayth saynte austyne god forgyueth somtyme euyll men grace alone gyueth hym selfe yet remyssyon synne wercheth booth hymselfe holy gooste thus man dooth awaye synne cryste alone psaynt ambrose doctoures sayth ye worde god forgyuethe synnes preest iuge yet hymselfe hath noo power hym alone deyed synnes psaynt iherome sayth power cryste gaaf apostle resurreccyon hath holy chyrche bysshoppes prestes specyally peter successours alle sholde vnderstonde whoo soo parteth hym frome vnytee fayth maye neuer losed frome synne ne entre blysse heuen pthe preest losed none verely god tho tourneth te penaunce thenne mynystreth ryghtfully vertue god hadde proufyted lazare wente oute tombe yf hadde sayde lose hym lete hym go cryst voys reysed hym frome sepulcre pand soo wente bounde myghte fete vertue hym reysed hym thys goostely done herte repentaunt man whan thou hereste man repentaunce synne thenne begynneth lyue agayne whan confessethe hym thenne broughte sepulcre yet losed see therfore whome whan losed cryste sayth tho ye haue losed erth shall losed heuen take hede sayd tho say man excepte soo repentaunt aske fogyuenesse chyrche shall haue foryeuenes yet though chyrche synne may worthely forgeuen dede maye ryse oure lorde crye within forth pfor done within v hym pthe dyscyples loosed hym lyuynge whome mayster reysed fro dethe sholde haue reysed hym dede sholde haue shewed strength vertue thus hath holy chyrche auctoryte spowse lose fro al maner synne saynte austyn saythe seuenty tymes seuen ben charged forgyue say euery man repentaunt asketh forgyuenes yet may euery preest generally doo tyme nede auctoryte byshop ryghte man hath power ete hath whereof soo prestes power haue power yet muste gyue theym theyre soueraynes whan moche shall execute maye noo man cheese hym confessour aboue without auctoryte hym ellys theym hathe power vnder hym nedes must shryuen owne curate yet certeyne cause byleue curate maye whan curate lacketh discressyon panother whan thou chaungest thy housholde arte vagabonde peryll dethe por whan thou entrest see soo greate peryll thou mayste also confesse laye man haue forgyuenesse thus yf thou scape muste charge thou shewe thyne owne curate also pylgrymes marchauntes goer aboute dyuerse countrees wyse pother cause ben yt thy curate must sende tofore bysshop wherto yu must nedes obeye sorye yt yu hast offende haue pthe token confessyon thyse pthe st shame whan thou shryueste sayth sayt iherome shamed al wayes thou haste gone synne thy confessyon fylthe synne thou sheweste pfor oonly lorde seeth sayth also holy company heuen ptherfore shamed maketh sooner haue mercye oure lorde saynt marye mawdeley ne shamed confesse synnes audyence presence alle feest confessyon teeres therfore broughte blysse pthe seconde mekenes worde lokynge chere wyth oute ony stordynes publycane thoughte hymself vnworthy lyfte vp eyen heuen pand poule also obeyed callynge oure lorde soo sholdest thou byddynge thy goostely fader pand noo wyse tary thy shryfte thyse perylles shewynge ye ben yet vnshryuen take gode hede thys lesson see peryl ye stonde pthe fyrste vncerteynte lyfe scrypture sayth noo man knoweth ende ne howe ne maner shall dey pand alle thou sholdest euery space tyme lyke wyse euery place redy preste receyue thy dethe also nother encreasynge multeplyenge thy deedly synne deedly synne euer yf anone done awaye shryft draweth hym sayth saynt augustyn thou encreasest thy synne ryght thouencreasest thy payne another drede tornynge agayne ferder thou goste fro god thy longe abydynge synne harder torne agayne thy good lyfe also grete sekenes thy payne somtyme grete yt thou mayst repentaunt must also hole one another grete spece ypocrysye vseth moche people wolde holde holy better ben saynt bernarde sayth confessyon trouthe thy mouthe prouffytable clennes thy herte yf thou seke swete al partyes thy body token lyfe yf pertyculer token dethe ryght soo thou tell thy synnes token saluacyon whan cryst heled man gospell speketh made hym halfe hole hole soo whan forgyueth forgyueth neuer dele therfore holde thyn herte thy lorde god sayth prophete water oyle leest fatnes abyde mylke leest whytenes appere ne wyne lest sauour abyde thou heldest thyn herte oyle shryuest thy small synnes leuest grete ye fat behynde thou heldest mylke coloure excusacyon makest thy synnes whyte fyrst fader adam dyde woman eue woman serpent thou heldest also wyne leuynge thy synne thou kepest sauoure within therof whan thou delytest lecherous wordes comunycacyons hast ioye grete delyte se vanytees auauntest lewdnesse done fore synne moost greueth god therfore holde thy herte water neyther fatnesse coloure ne fauoure abyde alle cyrcunstaunces maner place cause tyme age estate moche longe suche agree thy synne also muste naked made messengyre ne letter thyne owne mouthe gaye termes suche wyse neuer foule thy confessoure maye knowe meanynge doo wylfully theef henge vpon crosse achor muste also faythfulle thou haue full hope forgyuenes thy synnes mercy god thou goo hen accusynge thyselfe none sayenge iosue dauyd synneth dyde mys excusynge custome felysshyppe freylte also good entente vayne glory specyally offence done withoute ony feynynge pfor dyuerse cause confessyon profytable fyrst peryll synne thy confessoure sheweth also shame thou haste thy confessyon whiche greate relees thy payne pa nother sheweth thy concyence sykernes forgyuenes confessyon also god gloryfyed deuylle confounded vseth ofte confessyd temptacyon shall ouercome deuyll sayte austyne sayth oftener thou arte cofessyd thy synnes hope foryeuenes lyght lyer sayth thou shalte haue grace foryeuenes thy synnes onys yere spedfull make thy confessyon generalle specyall poynte deth shame herof shall greate parte thy satysfaccyon pthe thyrde parte penaunce sayde tofore satysfaccyon pthys grounded wordes prophete sayd naaman go wasshe seuen tymes iordan thou shalt clensed al thou haste defacede wyth spottys synne though sokede bytter sorowe thyne herte clerely rubbed wyth confessyon yet muste haue many dyuerse rensynges satyfaccyon tyll soo clerely purged purgatory maye clerely appere syghte oure lorde yf thy contrycyon grete thy penaunce maye lesse yf lytell thy payne muste nedes gretter soo grete maye suffyseth thy saluacyon psatysfaccyon dyuerse doctoures puttynge waye cause synne takynge hede theyr subgestyons also obligacio done gode werkes god mekenes lownes herte qualyte quantyte synne satysfaccyon must doo wylfully wythoute grutchynge muste plener generall euery synne resonably pa preuy penaunce preuy synne open penaunce open synne pthre pryncypall werkis ben satysfaccyon almes prayer fastyng pthyse thre oure lorde fulfylled passyon redempcyon oure synne ptherfore almes sholde doone shall telle almes lowynge thyne herte wylfull compassyon theym ben nede dede mercy compassyon thy neyghbours myschef ben thre maners almes one contrycyon thyne herte synne thou offerest thyself god nother gyuynge bodely tresoure thyne hond thyrde pyte compassyon hauynge thy neyghboures myscheue ptemporalle almes thou mayste somtyme gyue goodis vntruly goten say whan thou knoweste whome thou shalt restore yet muste done counseyle thy goostely fader pand tythe thou getest thefte somtyme chaunged thenne delyuereth shall aske agayne somtyme chaunged shall asked ayen whan tourneth taker cause come theft robbery raueyn symony vsery soo theym shall noo almes gyuen pfor muste restored ayene whan hauynge chaunged shall asked agayne pa gyftes comyn wymen iogelers suche thenne shall begyue almes palso yf thou fynde thyge ony value tyme thou haste done thy besynes wytte dewly owyd thou shalt spende almesse counseyle thy goostelyfader haue nede palso thou shalt gyue thyne almesse good badde frende enmye yf thou power lorde sayth gyue euery man asketh torne away thy face sayth thoby yet sayd gyue good man receyue synner saye gyue nature susteyned synne nourysshed pthou nourysshest synne geuest thy good iogelers iapers suche lyue idelnes suffre poure man haue hungre myscheef suche maner gyuyng forbode pyf pyte sayth saynt ambrose shall swete moche plenteuous muste thenne good vertuous lyuynge thou shalte rather gyue thy kynne neyghboure theyr nede ben vertuous pthou shalt also gyue olde men wymen chylde yf haue nede rather pand falle grete pouerte myserye whan suche pouerte falleth happeneth vnto ony maner persone thoroughe ryotous garmentes araye pompe presente worlde yet rather gyue thenne poure vnserued open thy herte alle aske loue god wythoute dyffyculte gyue wyth charyte wyth good wyll porellys thou makest noo dew satysfaccyon thy synne also glad chere meke spyryte thou vayne glory dyspyte poore man thou arte gyue hastely tary hym yt suffreth anguysshe sayth salomon gyue also dyscrecyon yf thou haue moch gyue moche yf thou haue lytell gyue lytell sayth thobye thus bodely goostly euery man may gyue almes pferther agaynst concupyscence thy flesshe thou haste fastynge harde goynge lyuynge bytter wepynge knockynge thy brest knelynge sharpe dyscyplyne roddes thyn owne hondes trauayle pylgrymage trybulacyons anguysshe sekenes suche bodely dyseases pacyently suffred scourge god suche penaunces wylfully taken dyscrete confessoure wyll put parte thy satysfaccyon penaunce pfastynge wylfull abstynence frome mete drynke wherby synne wasshen thy flesshe made lowe desyre euerlastynge blysse goostly fastynge frome deedly synnes temporall ioye saynt iherome sayth prouffytable feble thy boody fastynge whan thy herte swelleth pryde fast sykenes may ete pouerte ypocrysye ye worshyppe god thou muste modere thy fastynge thy stomacke greued moche excesse lytel mete mesurably rempreth prouffyteth bothe body soule dysposeth goostly trauayle ete moche delycate mete whan faste two meles wha fast maner breke theyr faste also prayer agaynst pryde two maner one inwarde thy soule without wynge voyce panother also ordeyned thre partyes satysfaccyon agaynst pryde myght putte awaye thenne oure lorde wyll grau te thynges thou mayste praye condycyon thynges withoute condycyon haue grace blysse oure blyssed ihesu cryst thou mayst axe withoute condycyon saynt hour specyally ordeyned tyme prayer whiche moost specially longen relygyous men oure lorde afore passyon trauayled nyghte prayer oure blyssed lady ioseph also rose euery nyght atte mydnyghte sayd grete deuocyon pdeuocyon clerkes saye tendernesse herte wherby thou brekest lyghtely teeres also wyll loue lyfte vp god heuenly creature menynge inwarde outwarde seruyce thy lorde god ihesu cryste suche deuocyon purgyth bothe boody soule pand thus deuocyon may knowen two pryncypall token one gretnesse voys outwarde grete fyre knowen flamme another teeres ryght fyre dryueth oute moystoure fro wete woode deuocyon bryngeth oute teeres thyne eyen prayer pwell hym hath suche plente teeres pfor dysposed grace ben haue grete plente teeres fro daye daye prayer deuoutely redynge spekynge yet wyll leue theyr wycked synne trauayle withstonde theyr temptacyons knowe ne kepe preceptes oure blyssed lorde ihesu cryste suche teeres ben accepte dewe sacrefyce oure blyssed lorde ihesu cryste yf thou full contryte sayth aldrede truste faythfully mercy god truely confessed wyllynge doo thy penaunce wyll retourne agayne thy olde synne thenne sayth suche teeres pleasen god wasshen awaye thy synnes tormente deuyll sayth saynt bernarde thenne kyndes tormentes may doo syth deuocyon must euery prayer yet tyme therof sholde pryncypally vsed tyme masse foure cause one presence oure lorde god oonely godhede also manhode tooke loue mannes soule pthe seconde multytude aungellys euermore presente yelde worshyppe almyghty god pthe thyrde grete prouffyte spede bodye soule haue vertue holy sacramente processe ryght may determyned ended pand tho pee londe destrouble pand tho blood drawe man woman vyolence vylonye make drawe chyrche chyrcheyerde wherfore chyrche chyrcheyerde entredyted suspended pand alle tho ye ben agayne ryghte oure lorde kynge tho werre susteyne ayenste kynge wrongfully tho comune robber reuers mansleers themselfe defendynge pand tho ben agayne greate charter kynge confermed courte rome tho false wytnes bere wrongefully namely cause matrymonye courte courte pand tho false wytnesse brynge forth ryght matrymonye dystrowble man woma por dysheryte ony man londe tenementes ony catell pand false aduocates mede putte forthe ony false excepcyons quarelles thrughe whiche ryght matrymony done ony maner ryght stede iugement pand tho mede fauoure malycyously man woman brynge oute theyr good fame wycked por make lese theyr worldly goddes honoure theym putte wrongefully theyr purgacyon whiche fame ne renowne knowen fore tyme pand alsoo whiche malycyously graunges persones vicaryes ony holy chirche agaynst theyr wyll pand tho ony maner good meuable vnmeuable awaye e strengthe wrongefully away drawe waste whiche cursynge may assoyled tylle haue made wyttyngely childern wytten ony man malyce pand tho varye flee theyr generacyons theyr chylderne destroye drynkes ony crafte pand tho fals money make therto assente pand tho good money clype shere
